Chapter_Header: 1
Verse_Ch: 1:1 以色列人出埃及地后，第二年二月初一日，耶和华在西乃的旷野，在会幕中对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses in the wilderness of Sinai, in the Tent of Meeting, on the first day of the second month, in the second year after they had come out of the land of Egypt, saying,
Verse_Ch: 1:2 你们要按以色列人全会众的家族、宗族，照人名的数目，逐一计算所有男丁的总数。 ###EN### Take the sum of all the assembly of the children of Israel, by their families, by their fathers' households, according to the number of names, every male, head by head.
Verse_Ch: 1:3 凡以色列中，从二十岁以上能出去打仗的，你和亚伦要按他们的军队数点。 ###EN### From twenty years old and upward, all who are able to go forth for military service in Israel, you and Aaron shall number them by their companies.
Verse_Ch: 1:4 每支派中要有一个在自己宗族中作首领的，与你们在一起。 ###EN### And with you there shall be a man from every tribe, each man the head of his fathers' household.
Verse_Ch: 1:5 这些辅助你们的人，名字记在下面：属流便的，有示丢珥的儿子以利蓿； ###EN### And these are the names of the men who shall stand with you. From Reuben: Elizur the son of Shedeur.
Verse_Ch: 1:6 属西缅的，有苏利沙代的儿子示路蔑； ###EN### From Simeon: Shelumiel the son of Zurishaddai.
Verse_Ch: 1:7 属犹大的，有亚米拿达的儿子拿顺； ###EN### From Judah: Nahshon the son of Amminadab.
Verse_Ch: 1:8 属以萨迦的，有苏押的儿子拿坦业； ###EN### From Issachar: Nethanel the son of Zuar.
Verse_Ch: 1:9 属西布伦的，有希伦的儿子以利押； ###EN### From Zebulun: Eliab the son of Helon.
Verse_Ch: 1:10 约瑟的子孙中，属以法莲的，有亚米忽的儿子以利沙玛；属玛拿西的，有比大蓿的儿子迦玛列； ###EN### From the children of Joseph: from Ephraim: Elishama the son of Ammihud; from Manasseh: Gamaliel the son of Pedahzur.
Verse_Ch: 1:11 属便雅悯的，有基多尼的儿子亚比但； ###EN### From Benjamin: Abidan the son of Gideoni.
Verse_Ch: 1:12 属但的，有亚米沙代的儿子亚希以谢； ###EN### From Dan: Ahiezer the son of Ammishaddai.
Verse_Ch: 1:13 属亚设的，有俄兰的儿子帕结； ###EN### From Asher: Pagiel the son of Ochran.
Verse_Ch: 1:14 属迦得的，有丢珥的儿子以利雅萨； ###EN### From Gad: Eliasaph the son of Deuel.
Verse_Ch: 1:15 属拿弗他利的，有以南的儿子亚希拉。 ###EN### From Naphtali: Ahira the son of Enan.
Verse_Ch: 1:16 这些都是从会众中选召的，都是宗族支派的首领；他们是以色列军中的统领。 ###EN### These are the ones who were called from the assembly, the leaders of the tribes of their fathers; they were the heads of the thousands of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 1:17 于是，摩西和亚伦带着这些按名指定的人， ###EN### And Moses and Aaron took these men who had been designated by name.
Verse_Ch: 1:18 在二月初一日招聚全会众；会众就按他们的家族、宗族，照人名的数目，从二十岁以上的，都逐一登录。 ###EN### And on the first day of the second month they gathered all the assembly together; and they registered themselves by their families, by their fathers' households, according to the number of names from twent and upward, head by head.
Verse_Ch: 1:19 耶和华怎样吩咐摩西，他在西乃的旷野就怎样数点他们。 ###EN### As Jehovah commanded Moses, so he numbered them in the wilderness of Sinai.
Verse_Ch: 1:20 以色列的长子，流便子孙的后代，按他们的家族、宗族，照人名的数目，从二十岁以上，凡能出去打仗的男丁，逐一被数点； ###EN### And the children of Reuben, Israel's firstborn, their generations, by their families, by their fathers' households, according to the number of names, head by head, every male from twenty years old and upward, all who were able to go forth for military service;
Verse_Ch: 1:21 属流便支派被数点的，有四万六千五百名。 ###EN### Those who were numbered of them, of the tribe of Reuben: forty-six thousand five hundred.
Verse_Ch: 1:22 西缅子孙的后代，按他们的家族、宗族，照人名的数目，从二十岁以上，凡能出去打仗的男丁，逐一被数点； ###EN### From the children of Simeon, their generations, by their families, by their fathers' households, those who were numbered of them, according to the number of names, head by head, every male from twenty years old and upward, all who were able to go forth for military service;
Verse_Ch: 1:23 属西缅支派被数点的，有五万九千三百名。 ###EN### Those who were numbered of them, of the tribe of Simeon: fifty-nine thousand three hundred.
Verse_Ch: 1:24 迦得子孙的后代，按他们的家族、宗族，照人名的数目，从二十岁以上，凡能出去打仗， ###EN### From the children of Gad, their generations, by their families, by their fathers' households, according to the number of names, from twenty years old and upward, all who were able to go forth for military service;
Verse_Ch: 1:25 属迦得支派被数点的，有四万五千六百五十名。 ###EN### Those who were numbered of them, of the tribe of Gad: forty-five thousand six hundred fifty.
Verse_Ch: 1:26 犹大子孙的后代，按他们的家族、宗族，照人名的数目，从二十岁以上，凡能出去打仗， ###EN### From the children of Judah, their generations, by their families, by their fathers' households, according to the number of names, from twenty years old and upward, all who were able to go forth for military service;
Verse_Ch: 1:27 属犹大支派被数点的，有七万四千六百名。 ###EN### Those who were numbered of them, of the tribe of Judah: seventy-four thousand six hundred.
Verse_Ch: 1:28 以萨迦子孙的后代，按他们的家族、宗族，照人名的数目，从二十岁以上，凡能出去打仗， ###EN### From the children of Issachar, their generations, by their families, by their fathers' households, according to the number of names, from twenty years old and upward, all who were able to go forth for military service;
Verse_Ch: 1:29 属以萨迦支派被数点的，有五万四千四百名。 ###EN### Those who were numbered of them, of the tribe of Issachar: fifty-four thousand four hundred.
Verse_Ch: 1:30 西布伦子孙的后代，按他们的家族、宗族，照人名的数目，从二十岁以上，凡能出去打仗， ###EN### From the children of Zebulun, their generations, by their families, by their fathers' households, according to the number of names, from twenty years old and upward, all who were able to go forth for military service;
Verse_Ch: 1:31 属西布伦支派被数点的，有五万七千四百名。 ###EN### Those who were numbered of them, of the tribe of Zebulun: fifty-seven thousand four hundred.
Verse_Ch: 1:32 约瑟的子孙中，以法莲子孙的后代，按他们的家族、宗族，照人名的数目，从二十岁以上，凡能出去打仗， ###EN### From the children of Joseph: from the children of Ephraim, their generations, by their families, by their fathers' households, according to the number of names, from twenty years old and upward, all who were able to go forth for military service;
Verse_Ch: 1:33 属以法莲支派被数点的，有四万零五百名。 ###EN### Those who were numbered of them, from the tribe of Ephraim: forty thousand five hundred.
Verse_Ch: 1:34 玛拿西子孙的后代，按他们的家族、宗族，照人名的数目，从二十岁以上，凡能出去打仗， ###EN### And from the children of Manasseh, their generations, by their families, by their fathers' households, according to the number of names, from twenty years old and upward, all who were able to go forth for military service;
Verse_Ch: 1:35 属玛拿西支派被数点的，有三万二千二百名。 ###EN### Those who were numbered of them, of the tribe of Manasseh: thirty-two thousand two hundred.
Verse_Ch: 1:36 便雅悯子孙的后代，按他们的家族、宗族，照人名的数目，从二十岁以上，凡能出去打仗， ###EN### From the children of Benjamin, their generations, by their families, by their fathers' households, according to the number of names, from twenty years old and upward, all who were able to go forth for military service;
Verse_Ch: 1:37 属便雅悯支派被数点的，有三万五千四百名。 ###EN### Those who were numbered of them, of the tribe of Benjamin: thirty-five thousand four hundred.
Verse_Ch: 1:38 但子孙的后代，按他们的家族、宗族，照人名的数目，从二十岁以上，凡能出去打仗， ###EN### From the children of Dan, their generations, by their families, by their fathers' households, according to the number of names, from twenty years old and upward, all who were able to go forth for military service;
Verse_Ch: 1:39 属但支派被数点的，有六万二千七百名。 ###EN### Those who were numbered of them, of the tribe of Dan: sixty-two thousand seven hundred.
Verse_Ch: 1:40 亚设子孙的后代，按他们的家族、宗族，照人名的数目，从二十岁以上，凡能出去打仗， ###EN### From the children of Asher, their generations, by their families, by their fathers' households, according to the number of names, from twenty years old and upward, all who were able to go forth for military service;
Verse_Ch: 1:41 属亚设支派被数点的，有四万一千五百名。 ###EN### Those who were numbered of them, of the tribe of Asher: forty-one thousand five hundred.
Verse_Ch: 1:42 拿弗他利子孙的后代，按他们的家族、宗族，照人名的数目，从二十岁以上，凡能出去打仗， ###EN### From the children of Naphtali, their generations, by their families, by their fathers' households, according to the number of names, from twenty years old and upward, all who were able to go forth for military service;
Verse_Ch: 1:43 属拿弗他利支派被数点的，有五万三千四百名。 ###EN### Those who were numbered of them, of the tribe of Naphtali: fifty-three thousand four hundred.
Verse_Ch: 1:44 这些就是被数点的，是摩西、亚伦、和以色列中十二个首领所数点的；这十二人各代表自己的宗族。 ###EN### These were the ones who were numbered, whom Moses and Aaron numbered, with the leaders of Israel, twelve men, each one for his fathers' household.
Verse_Ch: 1:45 这样，凡以色列人中被数点的，按他们的宗族，从二十岁以上，能出去打仗， ###EN### So all who were numbered of the children of Israel by their fathers' households, from twenty years old and upward, all who were able to go forth for military service in Israel,
Verse_Ch: 1:46 所有被数点的，共有六十万零三千五百五十名。 ###EN### Even all the numbered men were six hundred three thousand five hundred fifty.
Verse_Ch: 1:47 利未人却没有按宗族的支派数点在其中， ###EN### But the Levites were not numbered among them by their fathers' tribe.
Verse_Ch: 1:48 因为耶和华曾对摩西说， ###EN### For Jehovah had spoken to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 1:49 惟独利未支派你不可数点，也不可在以色列人中计算他们的总数。 ###EN### Only the tribe of Levi you shall not number, nor shall you take the sum of them among the children of Israel;
Verse_Ch: 1:50 只要派利未人照管见证的帐幕和其中的一切物件，并一切属于帐幕的；他们要抬帐幕和其中的一切物件，并要伺候帐幕，在帐幕四围安营。 ###EN### But you, appoint the Levites over the Tabernacle of the Testimony and over all its furnishings and over all that belongs to it. They shall carry the tabernacle and all its furnishings; and they shall minister to it and shall encamp around the tabernacle.
Verse_Ch: 1:51 帐幕将起行的时候，利未人要把它拆卸；帐幕将支搭的时候，利未人要把它竖起。近前来的外人要被处死。 ###EN### And when the tabernacle sets out, the Levites shall take it down; and when the tabernacle encamps, the Levites shall set it up. But the stranger who comes near shall be put to death.
Verse_Ch: 1:52 以色列人安营，要按着他们的军队，各归本营，各归本纛。 ###EN### And the children of Israel shall encamp, each one by his own camp and each one by his own standard, according to their companies.
Verse_Ch: 1:53 但利未人要在见证的帐幕四围安营，免得忿怒临到以色列人的会众；利未人要看守见证的帐幕。 ###EN### But the Levites shall encamp around the Tabernacle of the Testimony, that there be no wrath upon the assembly of the children of Israel. And the Levites shall keep the charge of the Tabernacle of the Testimony.
Verse_Ch: 1:54 以色列人就这样行；凡耶和华所吩咐摩西的，他们就照样行了。 ###EN### Thus did the children of Israel do; according to all that Jehovah had commanded Moses, so they did.
Chapter_Header: 2
Verse_Ch: 2:1 耶和华对摩西、亚伦说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses and to Aaron, saying,
Verse_Ch: 2:2 以色列人要各归自己的纛下，在自己宗族的旗号那里，对着会幕，在四边安营。 ###EN### The children of Israel shall encamp each by his own standard with the ensigns of their fathers' households; they shall encamp facing the Tent of Meeting on every side.
Verse_Ch: 2:3 在东边，向日出之地，按着军队安营的，是属于犹大营的纛；犹大人的首领是亚米拿达的儿子拿顺， ###EN### And those who encamp on the east side toward the sunrise shall be of the standard of the camp of Judah, according to their companies; and the leader of the children of Judah: Nahshon the son of Amminadab;
Verse_Ch: 2:4 他军队被数点的，有七万四千六百名。 ###EN### And his company, that is, those who were numbered of them: seventy-four thousand six hundred.
Verse_Ch: 2:5 挨着他安营的是以萨迦支派；以萨迦人的首领是苏押的儿子拿坦业， ###EN### And those who encamp next to him shall be the tribe of Issachar; and the leader of the children of Issachar: Nethanel the son of Zuar;
Verse_Ch: 2:6 他军队被数点的，有五万四千四百名。 ###EN### And his company, that is, those who were numbered of them: fifty-four thousand four hundred.
Verse_Ch: 2:7 又有西布伦支派；西布伦人的首领是希伦的儿子以利押， ###EN### Then the tribe of Zebulun; and the leader of the children of Zebulun: Eliab the son of Helon;
Verse_Ch: 2:8 他军队被数点的，有五万七千四百名。 ###EN### And his company, that is, his numbered men: fifty-seven thousand four hundred.
Verse_Ch: 2:9 凡属犹大营，按着军队被数点的，共有十八万六千四百名；他们要作第一队起行。 ###EN### All who were numbered of the camp of Judah: one hundred eighty-six thousand four hundred, according to their companies. They shall set out first.
Verse_Ch: 2:10 在南边，按着军队是流便营的纛；流便人的首领是示丢珥的儿子以利蓿， ###EN### On the south side shall be the standard of the camp of Reuben according to their companies; and the leader of the children of Reuben: Elizur the son of Shedeur;
Verse_Ch: 2:11 他军队被数点的，有四万六千五百名。 ###EN### And his company, that is, his numbered men: forty-six thousand five hundred.
Verse_Ch: 2:12 挨着他安营的是西缅支派；西缅人的首领是苏利沙代的儿子示路蔑， ###EN### And those who encamp next to him shall be the tribe of Simeon; and the leader of the children of Simeon: Shelumiel the son of Zurishaddai;
Verse_Ch: 2:13 他军队被数点的，有五万九千三百名。 ###EN### And his company, that is, those who were numbered of them: fifty-nine thousand three hundred.
Verse_Ch: 2:14 又有迦得支派；迦得人的首领是流珥的儿子以利雅萨， ###EN### Then the tribe of Gad; and the leader of the children of Gad: Eliasaph the son of Reuel;
Verse_Ch: 2:15 他军队被数点的，有四万五千六百五十名。 ###EN### And his company, that is, those who were numbered of them: forty-five thousand six hundred fifty.
Verse_Ch: 2:16 凡属流便营，按着军队被数点的，共有十五万一千四百五十名；他们要作第二队起行。 ###EN### All who were numbered of the camp of Reuben: one hundred fifty-one thousand four hundred fifty, according to their companies. And they shall set out second.
Verse_Ch: 2:17 随后，会幕要起行，有利未营在诸营中间；他们怎样安营，就怎样起行，各按本位，各归本纛。 ###EN### Then the Tent of Meeting shall set out, with the camp of the Levites in the midst of the camps; as they encamp, so shall they set out, every man in his place, by their standards.
Verse_Ch: 2:18 在西边，按着军队是以法莲营的纛；以法莲人的首领是亚米忽的儿子以利沙玛， ###EN### On the west side shall be the standard of the camp of Ephraim according to their companies; and the leader of the children of Ephraim: Elishama the son of Ammihud;
Verse_Ch: 2:19 他军队被数点的，有四万零五百名。 ###EN### And his company, that is, those who were numbered of them: forty thousand five hundred.
Verse_Ch: 2:20 挨着他的是玛拿西支派；玛拿西人的首领是比大蓿的儿子迦玛列， ###EN### And next to him shall be the tribe of Manasseh; and the leader of the children of Manasseh: Gamaliel the son of Pedahzur;
Verse_Ch: 2:21 他军队被数点的，有三万二千二百名。 ###EN### And his company, that is, those who were numbered of them: thirty-two thousand two hundred.
Verse_Ch: 2:22 又有便雅悯支派；便雅悯人的首领是基多尼的儿子亚比但， ###EN### Then the tribe of Benjamin; and the leader of the children of Benjamin: Abidan the son of Gideoni;
Verse_Ch: 2:23 他军队被数点的，有三万五千四百名。 ###EN### And his company, that is, those who were numbered of them: thirty-five thousand four hundred.
Verse_Ch: 2:24 凡属以法莲营，按着军队被数点的，共有十万八千一百名；他们要作第三队起行。 ###EN### All who were numbered of the camp of Ephraim: one hundred eight thousand one hundred, according to their companies. And they shall set out third.
Verse_Ch: 2:25 在北边，按着军队是但营的纛；但人的首领是亚米沙代的儿子亚希以谢， ###EN### On the north side shall be the standard of the camp of Dan according to their companies; and the leader of the children of Dan: Ahiezer the son of Ammishaddai;
Verse_Ch: 2:26 他军队被数点的，有六万二千七百名。 ###EN### And his company, that is, those who were numbered of them: sixty-two thousand seven hundred.
Verse_Ch: 2:27 挨着他安营的是亚设支派；亚设人的首领是俄兰的儿子帕结， ###EN### And those who encamp next to him shall be the tribe of Asher; and the leader of the children of Asher: Pagiel the son of Ochran;
Verse_Ch: 2:28 他军队被数点的，有四万一千五百名。 ###EN### And his company, that is, those who were numbered of them: forty-one thousand five hundred.
Verse_Ch: 2:29 又有拿弗他利支派；拿弗他利人的首领是以南的儿子亚希拉， ###EN### Then the tribe of Naphtali; and the leader of the children of Naphtali: Ahira the son of Enan;
Verse_Ch: 2:30 他军队被数点的，有五万三千四百名。 ###EN### And his company, that is, those who were numbered of them: fifty-three thousand four hundred.
Verse_Ch: 2:31 凡属但营被数点的，共有十五万七千六百名；他们要归本纛作末队起行。 ###EN### All who were numbered of the camp of Dan: one hundred fifty-seven thousand six hundred. They shall set out last by their standards.
Verse_Ch: 2:32 这些就是以色列人，按他们的宗族被数点的；所有在诸营中按军队被数点的，共有六十万三千五百五十名。 ###EN### These are those who were numbered of the children of Israel by their fathers' households. All who were numbered in the camps according to their companies were six hundred three thousand five hundred fifty.
Verse_Ch: 2:33 惟独利未人没有数点在以色列人中，是照耶和华所吩咐摩西的。 ###EN### But the Levites were not numbered among the children of Israel, as Jehovah had commanded Moses.
Verse_Ch: 2:34 以色列人就这样行，各人按他们的家族，照他们的宗族，归于本纛，安营并起行，都是照耶和华所吩咐摩西的。 ###EN### Thus did the children of Israel do. According to all that Jehovah commanded Moses, so they encamped by their standards and so they set out, every one by their families, according to their fathers' households.
Chapter_Header: 3
Verse_Ch: 3:1 耶和华在西乃山对摩西说话的日子，亚伦和摩西的后代如下： ###EN### Now these are the generations of Aaron and Moses at the time when Jehovah spoke with Moses on Mount Sinai.
Verse_Ch: 3:2 亚伦的儿子，长子名叫拿答，还有亚比户、以利亚撒、以他玛。 ###EN### And these are the names of the sons of Aaron: Nadab the firstborn and Abihu, Eleazar and Ithamar;
Verse_Ch: 3:3 这些是亚伦儿子的名字，他们都是受膏的祭司，承接圣职供祭司职分的。 ###EN### These are the names of the sons of Aaron, the anointed priests, whose hands were filled to serve as priests.
Verse_Ch: 3:4 但拿答、亚比户在西乃的旷野，在耶和华面前献凡火的时候，死在耶和华面前；他们没有儿子。因此以利亚撒、以他玛在他们的父亲亚伦面前供祭司 的职分。 ###EN### But Nadab and Abihu died before Jehovah when they offered strange fire before Jehovah in the wilderness of Sinai, and they had no children. So Eleazar and Ithamar served as priests in the presence of Aaron their father.
Verse_Ch: 3:5 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### And Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 3:6 你使利未支派近前来，站在祭司亚伦面前服事他； ###EN### Bring the tribe of Levi near and set them before Aaron the priest, that they may minister to him.
Verse_Ch: 3:7 他们要在会幕前，守所吩咐亚伦和全会众的，办理帐幕的事。 ###EN### And they shall keep his charge and the charge of the whole assembly before the Tent of Meeting to do the service of the tabernacle.
Verse_Ch: 3:8 他们要看守会幕的一切物件，并守所吩咐以色列人的，办理帐幕的事。 ###EN### And they shall keep all the furnishings of the Tent of Meeting and the charge of the children of Israel to do the service of the tabernacle.
Verse_Ch: 3:9 你要将利未人给亚伦和他的儿子们；他们是从以色列人中选出来，完全给他的。 ###EN### And you shall give the Levites to Aaron and to his sons; they are wholly given to him from among the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 3:10 你要指派亚伦和他的儿子们，使他们谨守自己祭司的职任；但近前来的外人要被处死。 ###EN### And you shall appoint Aaron and his sons, and they shall keep their priesthood; but the stranger who comes near shall be put to death.
Verse_Ch: 3:11 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 3:12 看哪，我从以色列人中选取了利未人，代替以色列人一切头生的；利未人要属我。 ###EN### As for Me, I have now taken the Levites from among the children of Israel instead of every firstborn who opens the womb among the children of Israel. So the Levites shall be Mine.
Verse_Ch: 3:13 因为凡头生的都是我的；我在埃及地击杀一切头生的那日，就把以色列中一切头生的，连人带牲畜都分别为圣归我；他们定要属我。我是耶和华。 ###EN### For all the firstborn are Mine; on the day that I struck all the firstborn in the land of Egypt I sanctified to Myself all the firstborn in Israel, both man and beast. They shall be Mine; I am Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 3:14 耶和华在西乃的旷野对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses in the wilderness of Sinai, saying,
Verse_Ch: 3:15 你要按利未人的宗族、家族数点他们；凡一个月以上的男子，都要数点。 ###EN### Number the children of Levi by their fathers' households, by their families; every male from a month old and upward you shall number.
Verse_Ch: 3:16 于是摩西照耶和华所吩咐他的话，数点他们。 ###EN### And Moses numbered them according to the word of Jehovah, as he was commanded.
Verse_Ch: 3:17 利未众子的名字是革顺、哥辖、米拉利。 ###EN### And these were the sons of Levi by their names: Gershon and Kohath and Merari.
Verse_Ch: 3:18 革顺的儿子，按着家族，名字是立尼、示每。 ###EN### And these are the names of the sons of Gershon according to their families: Libni and Shimei.
Verse_Ch: 3:19 哥辖的儿子，按着家族，是暗兰、以斯哈、希伯伦、乌薛。 ###EN### And the sons of Kohath by their families: Amram and Izhar, Hebron and Uzziel.
Verse_Ch: 3:20 米拉利的儿子，按着家族，是抹利、母示。这些按着宗族，是利未人的家族。 ###EN### And the sons of Merari according to their families: Mahli and Mushi. These are the families of the Levites according to their fathers' households.
Verse_Ch: 3:21 属革顺的，有立尼家族、示每家族；这些是革顺的家族。 ###EN### Of Gershon was the family of the Libnites and the family of the Shimeites; these are the families of the Gershonites.
Verse_Ch: 3:22 其中被数点的，按所有男子的数目，从一个月以上的，有七千五百名。 ###EN### Those who were numbered of them, according to the number of all the males, from a month old and upward, even those who were numbered of them were seven thousand five hundred.
Verse_Ch: 3:23 革顺的家族要在帐幕后面、西边安营。 ###EN### The families of the Gershonites shall encamp behind the tabernacle on the west.
Verse_Ch: 3:24 革顺人宗族的首领是拉伊勒的儿子以利雅萨。 ###EN### And the leader of the father's household of the Gershonites shall be Eliasaph the son of Lael.
Verse_Ch: 3:25 革顺的子孙在会幕中所要看守的，是帐幕和罩棚，罩棚的盖与会幕的门帘， ###EN### And the charge of the sons of Gershon in the Tent of Meeting shall be the tabernacle and the tent, its covering and the screen for the entrance of the Tent of Meeting,
Verse_Ch: 3:26 院子的帷子和门帘，(院子是围着帐幕和祭坛的，)并一切使用的绳子。 ###EN### And the hangings of the court, and the screen for the entrance of the court, which is around the tabernacle and around the altar, and its cords for all its service.
Verse_Ch: 3:27 属哥辖的，有暗兰家族、以斯哈家族、希伯伦家族、乌薛家族；这些是哥辖的家族。 ###EN### And of Kohath was the family of the Amramites and the family of the Izharites and the family of the Hebronites and the family of the Uzzielites; these are the families of the Kohathites.
Verse_Ch: 3:28 按所有男子的数目，从一个月以上的，有八千六百名；他们是看守圣所的。 ###EN### According to the number of all the males, from a month old and upward, there were eight thousand six hundred, keeping the charge of the sanctuary.
Verse_Ch: 3:29 哥辖子孙的家族要在帐幕的南边安营。 ###EN### The families of the sons of Kohath shall encamp on the side of the tabernacle to the south.
Verse_Ch: 3:30 哥辖人家族之宗族的首领是乌薛的儿子以利撒反。 ###EN### And the leader of the father's household of the families of the Kohathites shall be Elizaphan the son of Uzziel.
Verse_Ch: 3:31 他们要看守约柜、桌子、灯台、两座坛、圣所内供职用的器具和帘子，并负责一切有关的事务。 ###EN### And their charge shall be the Ark and the table and the lampstand and the altars and the utensils of the sanctuary with which they minister and the screen and all its service.
Verse_Ch: 3:32 祭司亚伦的儿子以利亚撒是利未人众首领的首领，要监督那些看守圣所的人。 ###EN### And Eleazar the son of Aaron the priest shall be leader of the leaders of the Levites and have the oversight of those who keep the charge of the sanctuary.
Verse_Ch: 3:33 属米拉利的，有抹利家族、母示家族；这些是米拉利的家族。 ###EN### Of Merari was the family of the Mahlites and the family of the Mushites; these are the families of Merari.
Verse_Ch: 3:34 他们被数点的，按所有男子的数目，从一个月以上的，有六千二百名。 ###EN### And those who were numbered of them, according to the number of all the males, from a month old and upward: six thousand two hundred.
Verse_Ch: 3:35 米拉利人家族之宗族的首领是亚比亥的儿子苏列；他们要在帐幕的北边安营。 ###EN### And the leader of the father's household of the families of Merari was Zuriel the son of Abihail. They shall encamp on the side of the tabernacle to the north.
Verse_Ch: 3:36 米拉利的子孙受派看守帐幕的板、闩、柱子、卯座、和一切的器具，负责一切有关的事务， ###EN### And the appointed charge of the sons of Merari shall be the boards of the tabernacle and its bars and its pillars and its sockets and all its equipment and all the service pertaining to it,
Verse_Ch: 3:37 并看守院子四围的柱子、卯座、橛子和绳子。 ###EN### And the pillars around the court and their sockets and their pegs and their cords.
Verse_Ch: 3:38 在帐幕前面、东边，就是会幕前面、向日出之地安营的，是摩西、亚伦和亚伦的儿子。他们看守圣所，守所吩咐以色列人的；近前来的外人要被处死。 ###EN### And those who encamp before the tabernacle to the east, before the Tent of Meeting toward the sunrise, shall be Moses and Aaron and his sons, keeping the charge of the sanctuary for the charge of the children of Israel; and the stranger who comes near shall be put to death.
Verse_Ch: 3:39 凡被数点的利未人，就是摩西、亚伦照耶和华吩咐所数点的，按着家族，从一个月以上所有的男子，有二万二千名。 ###EN### All who were numbered of the Levites, whom Moses and Aaron numbered at the commandment of Jehovah, by their families, all the males from a month old and upward were twenty-two thousand.
Verse_Ch: 3:40 耶和华对摩西说，你要数点以色列人中，一个月以上所有头生的男子，记下他们名字的数目。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to Moses, Number all the firstborn males of the children of Israel from a month old and upward, and take the number of their names.
Verse_Ch: 3:41 我是耶和华，你要选取利未人归我，代替以色列人中所有头生的，也要取利未人的牲畜代替以色列人的牲畜中所有头生的。 ###EN### And you shall take the Levites for Me-I am Jehovah-instead of all the firstborn among the children of Israel, and the cattle of the Levites instead of all the firstborn among the cattle of the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 3:42 摩西就照耶和华所吩咐的，把以色列人中所有头生的都数点了。 ###EN### And Moses numbered, just as Jehovah commanded him, all the firstborn among the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 3:43 按人名的数目，从一个月以上所有头生的男子，被数点的共有二万二千二百七十三名。 ###EN### And all the firstborn males according to the number of names, from a month old and upward, of those who were numbered of them were twenty-two thousand two hundred seventy-three.
Verse_Ch: 3:44 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 3:45 你要选取利未人代替以色列人中所有头生的，也要取利未人的牲畜代替以色列人的牲畜。利未人要属我；我是耶和华。 ###EN### Take the Levites instead of all the firstborn among the children of Israel, and the cattle of the Levites instead of their cattle; and the Levites shall be Mine; I am Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 3:46 以色列人头生的男子比利未人多二百七十三个，必当将他们赎出来； ###EN### And for the redemption of the two hundred seventy-three of the firstborn of the children of Israel over and above the number of the Levites,
Verse_Ch: 3:47 你要按人丁，照圣所的舍客勒，每人取赎银五舍客勒，(一舍客勒是二十季拉，) ###EN### You shall take five shekels apiece per head; according to the shekel of the sanctuary you shall take them. (The shekel is twenty gerahs.)
Verse_Ch: 3:48 把那多出之人的赎银，交给亚伦和他的儿子。 ###EN### And you shall give the money, by which the excess number of them is redeemed, to Aaron and to his sons.
Verse_Ch: 3:49 于是摩西从那些被利未人所赎以外的人取了赎银。 ###EN### So Moses took the redemption money from those who were over and above those who were redeemed by the Levites;
Verse_Ch: 3:50 从以色列人头生的所取之银，按圣所的舍客勒，有一千三百六十五舍客勒。 ###EN### From the firstborn of the children of Israel he took the money, a thousand three hundred sixty-five shekels according to the shekel of the sanctuary.
Verse_Ch: 3:51 摩西照耶和华的话，把这赎银交给亚伦和他的儿子，正如耶和华所吩咐的。 ###EN### And Moses gave the redemption money to Aaron and to his sons, according to the word of Jehovah, as Jehovah had commanded Moses.
Chapter_Header: 4
Verse_Ch: 4:1 耶和华对摩西、亚伦说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses and to Aaron, saying,
Verse_Ch: 4:2 你要从利未子孙中，计算哥辖子孙的总数；按他们的家族、宗族， ###EN### Take the sum of the sons of Kohath from among the sons of Levi, by their families, by their fathers' households,
Verse_Ch: 4:3 从三十岁直到五十岁，凡进来事奉，在会幕里作工的，全都计算。 ###EN### From thirty years old and upward even to fifty years old, all who enter into the service to perform the skilled work in the Tent of Meeting.
Verse_Ch: 4:4 哥辖子孙在会幕里搬运至圣之物，所办的事乃是这样： ###EN### This is the service of the sons of Kohath in the Tent of Meeting concerning the most holy things.
Verse_Ch: 4:5 起营的时候，亚伦和他儿子要进去摘下遮掩柜的幔子，用以蒙盖见证的柜； ###EN### When the camp sets out, Aaron and his sons shall go in, and they shall take down the veil of the screen and cover the Ark of the Testimony with it,
Verse_Ch: 4:6 又放上海狗皮盖，再铺上全蓝色的布，并把杠穿上。 ###EN### And they shall put on it a covering of porpoise skin, and shall spread over it a cloth all of blue strands, and shall put in its poles.
Verse_Ch: 4:7 又要用蓝色布铺在陈设饼的桌子上，将盘子、调羹、奠酒的壶和杯，摆在上头；桌子上也必有常设的饼。 ###EN### And over the table of the bread of the Presence they shall spread a blue cloth, and put on it the plates and the spoons and the bowls and the pitchers of the drink offering; and the continual bread shall be on it.
Verse_Ch: 4:8 又要铺上朱红色布，再蒙上海狗皮盖，并把杠穿上。 ###EN### And they shall spread over them a scarlet cloth, and cover it with a covering of porpoise skin, and shall put in its poles.
Verse_Ch: 4:9 要拿蓝色布，把灯台和灯台上供职用的灯盏、灯剪、灯花盘、并一切盛油的器皿，全都遮盖。 ###EN### And they shall take a blue cloth, and cover the lampstand of the light and its lamps and its tongs and its firepans and all its oil vessels with which they minister to it.
Verse_Ch: 4:10 又要把灯台和灯台的一切器具包在海狗皮里，放在抬架上。 ###EN### And they shall put it and all its utensils within a covering of porpoise skin, and shall put it on the carrying frame.
Verse_Ch: 4:11 在金坛上要铺蓝色布，蒙上海狗皮盖，并把杠穿上。 ###EN### And over the golden altar they shall spread a blue cloth, and cover it with a covering of porpoise skin, and shall put in its poles.
Verse_Ch: 4:12 又要把圣所里供职用的一切器具，包在蓝色布里，蒙上海狗皮盖，放在抬架上。 ###EN### And they shall take all the utensils of ministry with which they minister in the sanctuary, and put them in a blue cloth, and cover them with a covering of porpoise skin, and shall put them on the carrying frame.
Verse_Ch: 4:13 要收去坛上的灰，把紫色布铺在坛上； ###EN### And they shall remove the ashes from the altar, and spread a purple cloth over it.
Verse_Ch: 4:14 又要把坛上供职用的一切器具，就是火盆、肉叉、铲子、盘子，一切属坛的器具都摆在坛上，又铺上海狗皮盖，并把杠穿上。 ###EN### And they shall put upon it all its utensils with which they minister upon it, the firepans, the forks, and the shovels, and the basins-all the utensils of the altar; and they shall spread over it a covering of porpoise skin, and put in its poles.
Verse_Ch: 4:15 亚伦和他儿子把圣所和圣所的一切物件遮盖完了，将要起营的时候，哥辖的子孙就要来抬，只是不可摸圣物，免得他们死亡。会幕里这些物件是哥辖 子孙所当抬的。 ###EN### And when Aaron and his sons have finished covering the sanctuary and all the furnishings of the sanctuary, whenever the camp sets out, then the sons of Kohath shall come to carry them; but they shall not touch the holy things, or they will die. These things are the burden of the sons of Kohath in the Tent of Meeting.
Verse_Ch: 4:16 祭司亚伦的儿子以利亚撒所要照管的是点灯的油与馨香的香，并常献的素祭和膏油，也要照管全帐幕与其中所有的，就是圣所和圣所的器具。 ###EN### And the oversight of Eleazar the son of Aaron the priest shall be the oil for the light and the fragrant incense and the continual meal offering and the anointing oil, the oversight of all the tabernacle and all that is in it, the sanctuary and its furnishings.
Verse_Ch: 4:17 耶和华对摩西、亚伦说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses and to Aaron, saying,
Verse_Ch: 4:18 你们不可将哥辖人家族的支派从利未人中剪除； ###EN### Do not let the tribe of the families of the Kohathites be cut off from among the Levites;
Verse_Ch: 4:19 他们挨近至圣之物的时候，亚伦和他儿子要进去派他们各人所当办的，所当抬的；要这样待他们，好使他们活着，不至死亡； ###EN### But do this to them that they may live and not die when they approach the most holy things: Aaron and his sons shall go in and assign each one of them to his service and to his burden;
Verse_Ch: 4:20 只是他们连片刻都不可进去观看圣所，免得死亡。 ###EN### But the Kohathites shall not go in to see the sanctuary even for a moment; otherwise they will die.
Verse_Ch: 4:21 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 4:22 你也要计算革顺子孙的总数；按他们的宗族、家族， ###EN### Take the sum of the sons of Gershon also, by their fathers' households, by their families;
Verse_Ch: 4:23 从三十岁直到五十岁，凡进来事奉，在会幕里办事的，你都要数点。 ###EN### From thirty years old and upward to fifty years old you shall number them, everyone who enters to carry out the service to do the work in the Tent of Meeting.
Verse_Ch: 4:24 革顺人家族在办事、抬物上的事奉，乃是这样： ###EN### This is the service of the families of the Gershonites, in serving and in bearing burdens:
Verse_Ch: 4:25 他们要抬帐幕的幕幔和会幕，会幕的盖与其上的海狗皮盖，和会幕的门帘， ###EN### They shall carry the curtains of the tabernacle, and the Tent of Meeting, its covering, and the covering of porpoise skin that is on top of it, and the screen for the entrance of the Tent of Meeting,
Verse_Ch: 4:26 院子的帷子和门帘、(院子是围着帐幕和祭坛的、)绳子，并事奉用的一切器具；这些不论该怎么处理，他们都要去办。 ###EN### And the hangings of the court, and the screen for the entrance of the gate of the court, which is around the tabernacle and around the altar, and their cords, and all the equipment for their service; and whatever is to be done with them, so shall they do.
Verse_Ch: 4:27 革顺的子孙在抬物、办事上的一切事奉，都要照亚伦和他儿子的吩咐；他们所当抬的一切，你们要派他们看守。 ###EN### All the service of the sons of the Gershonites shall be at the command of Aaron and his sons, in all their burden and in all their service; and you shall assign to them the charge of all they are to carry.
Verse_Ch: 4:28 这是革顺子孙的家族在会幕里所办的事；他们的职责，要在祭司亚伦的儿子以他玛的管理下。 ###EN### This is the service of the families of the sons of the Gershonites in the Tent of Meeting, and their charge shall be under the direction of Ithamar the son of Aaron the priest.
Verse_Ch: 4:29 至于米拉利的子孙，你要按他们的家族、宗族，数点他们； ###EN### As for the sons of Merari, you shall number them by their families, by their fathers' households;
Verse_Ch: 4:30 从三十岁直到五十岁，凡进来事奉，在会幕里办事的，你都要数点。 ###EN### From thirty years old and upward even to fifty years old you shall number them, everyone who enters into the service to do the work of the Tent of Meeting.
Verse_Ch: 4:31 按他们在会幕里的一切事奉，他们的职责是抬帐幕的板、闩、柱子和卯座， ###EN### And this is the charge of what they are to carry, according to all their service in the Tent of Meeting: the boards of the tabernacle and its bars and its pillars and its sockets,
Verse_Ch: 4:32 院子四围的柱子和卯座、橛子、绳子、和一切的器具，并办理一切有关的事；他们所当抬的器具，你们要按名指定。 ###EN### And the pillars around the court and their sockets and their pegs and their cords, with all their equipment and with all their service; and you shall assign by name the equipment they have been charged to carry.
Verse_Ch: 4:33 这是米拉利子孙的家族，按他们在会幕里的一切事奉，所办的事，都在祭司亚伦的儿子以他玛的管理下。 ###EN### This is the service of the families of the sons of Merari, according to all their service in the Tent of Meeting, under the direction of Ithamar the son of Aaron the priest.
Verse_Ch: 4:34 摩西、亚伦与会众的诸首领将哥辖的子孙，按他们的家族、宗族， ###EN### And Moses and Aaron and the leaders of the assembly numbered the sons of the Kohathites by their families and by their fathers' households,
Verse_Ch: 4:35 从三十岁直到五十岁，凡进来事奉，在会幕里办事的，都数点了。 ###EN### From thirty years old and upward even to fifty years old, everyone who entered into the service for work in the Tent of Meeting.
Verse_Ch: 4:36 他们按家族被数点的，有二千七百五十名。 ###EN### And those who were numbered of them by their families were two thousand seven hundred fifty.
Verse_Ch: 4:37 这些是哥辖人的家族中被数点的，都是在会幕里办事的，就是摩西、亚伦照耶和华藉摩西所吩咐数点的。 ###EN### These are those who were numbered of the families of the Kohathites, all who served in the Tent of Meeting, whom Moses and Aaron numbered according to the commandment of Jehovah through Moses.
Verse_Ch: 4:38 革顺的子孙，按他们家族、宗族被数点的， ###EN### And those who were numbered of the sons of Gershon by their families and by their fathers' households,
Verse_Ch: 4:39 从三十岁直到五十岁，凡进来事奉，在会幕里办事的， ###EN### From thirty years old and upward even to fifty years old, everyone who entered into the service for work in the Tent of Meeting,
Verse_Ch: 4:40 就是他们按家族、宗族被数点的，有二千六百三十名。 ###EN### Even those who were numbered of them, by their families, by their fathers' households were two thousand six hundred thirty.
Verse_Ch: 4:41 这些是革顺子孙的家族中被数点的，都是在会幕里办事的，就是摩西、亚伦照耶和华所吩咐数点的。 ###EN### These were those who were numbered of the families of the sons of Gershon, everyone who served in the Tent of Meeting, whom Moses and Aaron numbered according to the commandment of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 4:42 米拉利子孙的家族中，按他们家族、宗族被数点的， ###EN### And those who were numbered of the families of the sons of Merari, by their families, by their fathers' households,
Verse_Ch: 4:43 从三十岁直到五十岁，凡进来事奉，在会幕里办事的， ###EN### From thirty years old and upward even to fifty years old, everyone who entered into the service for work in the Tent of Meeting,
Verse_Ch: 4:44 就是他们按家族被数点的，有三千二百名。 ###EN### Even those who were numbered of them by their families were three thousand two hundred.
Verse_Ch: 4:45 这些是米拉利子孙的家族中被数点的，就是摩西、亚伦照耶和华藉摩西所吩咐数点的。 ###EN### These were those who were numbered of the families of the sons of Merari, whom Moses and Aaron numbered according to the commandment of Jehovah through Moses.
Verse_Ch: 4:46 凡被数点的利未人，就是摩西、亚伦并以色列众首领，按他们的家族、宗族所数点的， ###EN### All those who were numbered of the Levites, whom Moses and Aaron and the leaders of Israel numbered, by their families and by their fathers' households,
Verse_Ch: 4:47 从三十岁直到五十岁，凡进来供职，在会幕里办事，作抬物之工的， ###EN### From thirty years old and upward even to fifty years old, everyone who entered to do the work of service and the work of bearing burdens in the Tent of Meeting,
Verse_Ch: 4:48 就是那些被数点的，共有八千五百八十名。 ###EN### Even those who were numbered of them were eight thousand five hundred eighty.
Verse_Ch: 4:49 摩西按他们各人所办的事、所抬的物，照耶和华藉他所吩咐的，数点他们；他们这样被摩西数点，正如耶和华所吩咐他的。 ###EN### According to the commandment of Jehovah through Moses they were numbered, everyone according to his service and according to his burden; thus they were numbered by him, just as Jehovah had commanded Moses.
Chapter_Header: 5
Verse_Ch: 5:1 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 5:2 你要吩咐以色列人，把一切患痲疯的，患漏症的，并因死人不洁净的，都送出营外。 ###EN### Command the children of Israel that they send out of the camp every leper and everyone that has a discharge and everyone who is unclean because of a dead person.
Verse_Ch: 5:3 无论男女，都要把他们送到营外去，免得污秽他们的营；这营是我在他们中间所住的。 ###EN### You shall send out both male and female; you shall send them outside the camp so that they will not defile their camp, where I dwell in their midst.
Verse_Ch: 5:4 以色列人就这样行，把他们送到营外去；耶和华对摩西怎样说，以色列人就怎样行了。 ###EN### And the children of Israel did so and sent them outside the camp; just as Jehovah had spoken to Moses, so the children of Israel did.
Verse_Ch: 5:5 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 5:6 你要对以色列人说，无论男女，若犯了人所常犯的罪，以致对耶和华行事不忠实，那人就有了罪过； ###EN### Speak to the children of Israel, When a man or woman commits any sin that men commit, so as to act unfaithfully toward Jehovah, and that person realizes his guilt,
Verse_Ch: 5:7 他要承认所犯的罪，将所亏负人的，全数赔还，另外加上五分之一，给与所亏负的人。 ###EN### Then they shall confess their sin which they have committed, and he shall make restitution according to its principal for his wrong and add to it one-fifth of it and give it to the one whom he has wronged.
Verse_Ch: 5:8 那人若没有亲属可以接受所赔还的，所赔还的就要归与耶和华，就是归与祭司；另外加上遮罪的公绵羊，为他遮罪。 ###EN### But if the man has no kinsman to whom restitution may be made for the wrong, the restitution which is made for the wrong goes to Jehovah for the priest, in addition to the ram of the expiation, by which expiation is made for him.
Verse_Ch: 5:9 以色列人一切圣物中所奉给祭司的举祭，都要归与祭司。 ###EN### And every heave offering of all the holy things of the children of Israel, which they present to the priest, shall be his.
Verse_Ch: 5:10 各人给祭司的圣物，无论是什么，都要归与祭司。 ###EN### And everyone's holy things shall be his; whatever anyone gives to the priest, it becomes his.
Verse_Ch: 5:11 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 5:12 你要对以色列人说，人的妻子若背离丈夫，对他行事不忠实， ###EN### Speak to the children of Israel and say to them, If any man's wife goes astray and acts unfaithfully toward him,
Verse_Ch: 5:13 有人与她同寝交合，事情瞒过她丈夫，而且她被玷污，却未被察觉，又没有作见证的人，因她行淫的时候没有被捉住； ###EN### And a man lies with her and has sexual relations, and it is hidden from the eyes of her husband, and she is undetected, and she is defiled, and there is no witness against her since she was not caught in the act;
Verse_Ch: 5:14 她丈夫有了疑忌的灵，疑忌她，她是玷污了自己，或是她丈夫有了疑忌的灵，疑忌她，她并没有玷污自己， ###EN### And a spirit of jealousy comes upon him, and he is jealous of his wife, and she has defiled herself; or if a spirit of jealousy comes upon him, and he is jealous of his wife, and she has not defiled herself;
Verse_Ch: 5:15 这人就要将妻子送到祭司那里，又为她带着大麦面一伊法的十分之一作供物；不可浇上油，也不可放上乳香；因为这是疑忌的素祭，是思念的素祭， 使人想起罪孽。 ###EN### Then the man shall bring his wife to the priest and bring her offering for her, a tenth of an ephah of barley meal. He shall pour no oil upon it nor put frankincense on it; for it is a meal offering of jealousy, a meal offering of remembrance, bringing iniquity to remembrance.
Verse_Ch: 5:16 祭司要使那妇人近前来，站在耶和华面前。 ###EN### And the priest shall bring her near and set her before Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 5:17 祭司要把圣水盛在瓦器里，又从帐幕的地上取点尘土，放在水中。 ###EN### And the priest shall take holy water in an earthen vessel, and the priest shall take some of the dust that is on the floor of the tabernacle and put it into the water.
Verse_Ch: 5:18 祭司要使那妇人站在耶和华面前，叫她蓬头散发，又要把思念的素祭，就是疑忌的素祭，放在她手中；祭司要手里拿着招致咒诅的苦水， ###EN### And the priest shall set the woman before Jehovah and let the hair of the woman's head go loose and put the meal offering of remembrance in her hands, which is the meal offering of jealousy, and in the hand of the priest shall be the water of bitterness that brings the curse.
Verse_Ch: 5:19 叫妇人起誓，对她说，若没有人与你同寝，你也未曾在丈夫权下的时候，背离他作污秽的事，你就免受这招致咒诅之苦水的灾。 ###EN### And the priest shall make her take an oath and shall say to the woman, If no man has lain with you and if you have not gone astray to uncleanness while under the authority of your husband, be immune to this water of bitterness that brings the curse.
Verse_Ch: 5:20 你若在丈夫权下的时候，背离他玷污了自己，在你丈夫以外有人与你同寝， ###EN### But if you have gone astray while under the authority of your husband and if you have defiled yourself, and a man besides your husband has lain with you -
Verse_Ch: 5:21 (这时祭司要叫妇人发咒起誓，对她说，)愿耶和华叫你大腿消瘦，肚子发胀，使你在你民中成了咒诅，成了誓语； ###EN### Then the priest shall make the woman take an oath with the oath of cursing, and the priest shall say to the woman-Jehovah make you a curse and an oath among your people, when Jehovah makes your thigh waste away and your womb swell;
Verse_Ch: 5:22 并且这招致咒诅的水入你的腹中，要叫你的肚子发胀，大腿消瘦。妇人要说，阿们，阿们。 ###EN### And this water that brings the curse shall go into your bowels and make your womb swell and your thigh waste away. And the woman shall say, Amen, Amen.
Verse_Ch: 5:23 祭司要将这咒诅的话写在书卷上，将所写的字在苦水里抹掉； ###EN### And the priest shall write these curses in a book, and he shall wash them off into the water of bitterness.
Verse_Ch: 5:24 又叫妇人喝这招致咒诅的苦水；这水要进入她里面变苦了。 ###EN### And he shall make the woman drink the water of bitterness that brings the curse; and the water that brings the curse shall enter into her and become bitter.
Verse_Ch: 5:25 祭司要从妇人的手中取那疑忌的素祭，在耶和华面前摇一摇，拿到坛前； ###EN### And the priest shall take the meal offering of jealousy out of the woman's hand, and he shall wave the meal offering before Jehovah and bring it to the altar.
Verse_Ch: 5:26 又要从素祭中取出一把，作为记念的部分，烧在坛上，然后叫妇人喝这水。 ###EN### And the priest shall take a handful of the meal offering as its memorial portion and burn it upon the altar, and afterward he shall make the woman drink the water.
Verse_Ch: 5:27 叫她喝了以后，她若玷污了自己，对丈夫行事不忠实，这招致咒诅的水必进入她里面变苦了，她的肚子就要发胀，大腿就要消瘦；那妇人便要在她民 中成了咒诅。 ###EN### And when he has made her drink the water, then if she has defiled herself and has acted unfaithfully to her husband, the water that brings the curse will enter into her and become bitter, and her womb will swell, and her thigh will waste away; and the woman shall be a curse among her people.
Verse_Ch: 5:28 妇人若没有玷污自己，是洁净的，就要免受这灾，且能怀孕。 ###EN### But if the woman has not defiled herself and is clean, then she will be immune and able to conceive seed.
Verse_Ch: 5:29 妻子在丈夫权下的时候，背离他玷污了自己， ###EN### This is the law of jealousy when a wife, while under the authority of her husband, goes astray and defiles herself,
Verse_Ch: 5:30 或是人有了疑忌的灵，疑忌他的妻子，就有这疑忌的条例。他要叫妇人站在耶和华面前，祭司要在她身上施行这全部的条例。 ###EN### Or when the spirit of jealousy comes upon a man, and he is jealous of his wife. He shall set the woman before Jehovah, and the priest shall apply to her all this law.
Verse_Ch: 5:31 男人可免去罪孽，但妇人必担当自己的罪孽。 ###EN### And the man shall be free from iniquity, but that woman shall bear her iniquity.
Chapter_Header: 6
Verse_Ch: 6:1 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 6:2 你要对以色列人说，无论男女许了特别的愿，就是拿细耳人的愿，要将自己分别出来归给耶和华， ###EN### Speak to the children of Israel and say to them, When a man or a woman makes a special vow, the vow of a Nazarite, to separate himself to Jehovah,
Verse_Ch: 6:3 他就要远离淡酒和浓酒，也不可喝淡酒或浓酒作的醋；不可喝什么葡萄汁，也不可吃鲜葡萄或干葡萄。 ###EN### He shall separate himself from wine and strong drink; he shall drink no vinegar of wine or vinegar of strong drink, nor shall he drink any juice of grapes, nor eat fresh or dried grapes.
Verse_Ch: 6:4 在他分别出来的一切日子，凡葡萄树上结的，自核至皮所作的物，都不可吃。 ###EN### All the days of his separation he shall eat nothing that is produced by the grape vine, from the seeds even to the skin.
Verse_Ch: 6:5 在他许愿分别出来的一切日子，不可用剃刀剃头。他要成为圣别，直到他将自己分别出来归耶和华的日子满了；他要任由发绺长长。 ###EN### All the days of his vow of separation no razor shall pass over his head. He shall be holy until the days are fulfilled for which he separated himself to Jehovah; he shall let the locks of the hair of his head grow long.
Verse_Ch: 6:6 在他将自己分别出来归耶和华的一切日子，不可挨近死人。 ###EN### All the days that he separates himself to Jehovah he shall not come near a dead person.
Verse_Ch: 6:7 他的父母、兄弟、或姊妹死了的时候，他不可因他们使自己不洁净，因为那分别出来归神的凭据在他头上。 ###EN### He shall not make himself unclean for his father or for his mother, for his brother or for his sister, when they die, because his separation to God is upon his head.
Verse_Ch: 6:8 在他分别出来的一切日子，他是归耶和华为圣的。 ###EN### All the days of his separation he is holy to Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 6:9 若有人在他旁边忽然死了，以致玷污了他分别出来的头，他就要在得洁净的日子剃头，就是在第七日剃头。 ###EN### And if anyone dies very suddenly beside him so that he defiles the head of his separation, then he shall shave his head on the day he becomes clean; on the seventh day shall he shave it.
Verse_Ch: 6:10 第八日，他要把两只斑鸠或两只雏鸽带到会幕门口，交给祭司。 ###EN### And on the eighth day he shall bring two turtledoves or two young pigeons to the priest at the entrance of the Tent of Meeting,
Verse_Ch: 6:11 祭司要献一只作赎罪祭，一只作燔祭，为他因死人而有的罪遮罪。 ###EN### And the priest shall offer one for a sin offering and the other for a burnt offering, and make expiation for him because he sinned by reason of the dead person. And he shall sanctify his head that same day.
Verse_Ch: 6:12 他要在当日使自己的头分别为圣；他要将自己分别出来的日子，重新分别出来归给耶和华，又要牵一只一岁的公羊羔来作赎愆祭；那先前的日子要归 徒然，因为他在分别出来的期间被玷污了。 ###EN### And he shall separate to Jehovah the days of his separation and shall bring a male lamb a year old for a trespass offering, but the former days shall be void because his separation was defiled.
Verse_Ch: 6:13 拿细耳人满了分别出来的日子，条例乃是这样：人要领他到会幕门口； ###EN### Now this is the law of the Nazarite when the days of his separation are fulfilled: He shall be brought to the entrance of the Tent of Meeting.
Verse_Ch: 6:14 他要将供物奉给耶和华，就是一只没有残疾、一岁的公羊羔作燔祭，一只没有残疾、一岁的母羊羔作赎罪祭，一只没有残疾的公绵羊作平安祭， ###EN### And he shall present his offering to Jehovah: one male lamb a year old without blemish for a burnt offering, and one female lamb a year old without blemish for a sin offering, and one ram without blemish for a peace offering,
Verse_Ch: 6:15 并一筐子无酵饼，就是细面调油的饼，与抹油的无酵薄饼，并同献的素祭和奠祭。 ###EN### And a basket of unleavened bread, cakes of fine flour mingled with oil, and unleavened wafers anointed with oil, and their meal offering and their drink offerings.
Verse_Ch: 6:16 祭司要将这些奉到耶和华面前，献上那人的赎罪祭和燔祭； ###EN### And the priest shall present them before Jehovah, and shall offer his sin offering and his burnt offering.
Verse_Ch: 6:17 也要把那只公绵羊连同那筐无酵饼，献给耶和华作平安祭，又要将同献的素祭和奠祭献上。 ###EN### And he shall offer the ram for a sacrifice of peace offerings to Jehovah, with the basket of unleavened bread. The priest shall also offer its meal offering and its drink offering.
Verse_Ch: 6:18 拿细耳人要在会幕门口剃他分别出来的头，把分别出来头上的发放在平安祭下的火上。 ###EN### And the Nazarite shall shave the head of his separation at the entrance of the Tent of Meeting, and take the hair of the head of his separation and put it on the fire that is under the sacrifice of peace offerings.
Verse_Ch: 6:19 他剃了以后，祭司就要取那煮了的公绵羊一条前腿，又从筐子里取一个无酵饼，和一个无酵薄饼，都放在他手上； ###EN### And the priest shall take the boiled shoulder of the ram and one unleavened cake out of the basket and one unleavened wafer, and shall put them into the hands of the Nazarite after he has shaved the head of his separation;
Verse_Ch: 6:20 祭司要拿这些作为摇祭，在耶和华面前摇一摇；这与摇祭的胸、举祭的腿，都归祭司为圣。然后拿细耳人可以喝酒。 ###EN### And the priest shall wave them for a wave offering before Jehovah. It is holy for the priest, together with the breast of the wave offering and thigh of the heave offering. And afterward the Nazarite may drink wine.
Verse_Ch: 6:21 许愿的拿细耳人为将自己分别出来，而献供物给耶和华，并献他在这之外所能献的，条例就是这样。他怎样许愿，就当照这分别出来的条例行。 ###EN### This is the law of the Nazarite who vows, that is, of his offering to Jehovah for his separation, in addition to what he can afford; according to his vow which he vows, so he must do according to the law of his separation.
Verse_Ch: 6:22 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 6:23 你要对亚伦和他儿子们说，你们要这样为以色列人祝福，说， ###EN### Speak to Aaron and to his sons, saying, Thus you shall bless the children of Israel; you shall say to them,
Verse_Ch: 6:24 愿耶和华赐福给你，保护你； ###EN### Jehovah bless you and keep you;
Verse_Ch: 6:25 愿耶和华使祂的面光照你，赐恩给你； ###EN### Jehovah make His face shine upon you and be gracious to you;
Verse_Ch: 6:26 愿耶和华向你扬脸，赐你平安。 ###EN### Jehovah lift up His countenance upon you and give you peace.
Verse_Ch: 6:27 他们要如此将我的名赐给以色列人，好使我赐福给他们。 ###EN### So shall they put My name upon the children of Israel, that I Myself may bless them.
Chapter_Header: 7
Verse_Ch: 7:1 摩西立完了帐幕的那日，就把帐幕用膏抹了，使其分别为圣，又把其中的一切物件，并坛与坛的一切器具都抹了，使其分别为圣； ###EN### And on the day that Moses had finished setting up the tabernacle, and had anointed it and sanctified it and all its furnishings and the altar and all its utensils, and had anointed them and sanctified them,
Verse_Ch: 7:2 以色列的众首领，就是各宗族的族长，都来献供物；他们是各支派的首领，管理那些被数点的人。 ###EN### The leaders of Israel, the heads of their fathers' households (they were the leaders of the tribes, who were over those who had been numbered), presented their offering.
Verse_Ch: 7:3 他们把自己的供物送到耶和华面前，就是六辆篷车和十二只公牛；每两个首领献一辆车，每首领献一只牛；他们把这些都奉到帐幕前。 ###EN### And they brought their offering before Jehovah: six covered wagons and twelve oxen, a wagon for every two of the leaders and an ox for each one; and they presented them before the tabernacle.
Verse_Ch: 7:4 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 7:5 你要从他们收下这些，好用以办理会幕的事；要照利未人各人所办的事，交给他们。 ###EN### Take these from them, that they may be used in doing the service of the Tent of Meeting; and you shall give them to the Levites, to each according to his service.
Verse_Ch: 7:6 于是摩西收了车和牛，交给利未人， ###EN### And Moses took the wagons and the oxen, and gave them to the Levites.
Verse_Ch: 7:7 把两辆车，四只牛，照革顺子孙所办的事交给他们， ###EN### Two wagons and four oxen he gave to the sons of Gershon according to their service;
Verse_Ch: 7:8 又把四辆车，八只牛，照米拉利子孙所办的事交给他们；他们都在祭司亚伦的儿子以他玛的管理下。 ###EN### And four wagons and eight oxen he gave to the sons of Merari according to their service, under the direction of Ithamar the son of Aaron the priest.
Verse_Ch: 7:9 只是没有交给哥辖子孙，因为他们办的是圣所的事；他们是在肩头上抬圣物的。 ###EN### But to the sons of Kohath he gave none, because the service of the sanctuary belonged to them; they bore this upon their shoulder.
Verse_Ch: 7:10 用膏抹坛的日子，首领都来献上为坛行奉献之礼的供物；众首领把供物献在坛前。 ###EN### And the leaders presented offerings for the dedication of the altar in the day that it was anointed; that is, the leaders presented their offering before the altar.
Verse_Ch: 7:11 耶和华对摩西说，众首领为行献坛的礼，要每天一个首领来献供物。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to Moses, They shall present their offering, one leader each day, for the dedication of the altar.
Verse_Ch: 7:12 头一日献供物的，是犹大支派亚米拿达的儿子拿顺。 ###EN### And he who presented his offering the first day was Nahshon the son of Amminadab, of the tribe of Judah.
Verse_Ch: 7:13 他的供物是：一个银盘，重一百三十舍客勒；一个银碗，重七十舍客勒；都是按圣所的舍客勒，也都盛满了调油的细面作素祭； ###EN### And his offering was one silver plate; its weight was one hundred thirty shekels; one silver bowl of seventy shekels, according to the shekel of the sanctuary; both of them full of fine flour mingled with oil for a meal offering;
Verse_Ch: 7:14 一个金盂，重十舍客勒，盛满了香； ###EN### One golden spoon of ten shekels, full of incense;
Verse_Ch: 7:15 一只公牛犊，一只公绵羊，一只一岁的公羊羔作燔祭； ###EN### One bull of the herd, one ram, one male lamb a year old, for a burnt offering;
Verse_Ch: 7:16 一只公山羊作赎罪祭； ###EN### One male of the goats for a sin offering;

Verse_Ch: 7:84 用膏抹坛的日子，以色列的众首领为行献坛之礼所献的是：银盘十二个，银碗十二个，金盂十二个； ###EN### This was the dedication of the altar, in the day when it was anointed, by the leaders of Israel: twelve silver plates, twelve silver bowls, twelve golden spoons;
Verse_Ch: 7:85 每银盘重一百三十舍客勒，每碗重七十舍客勒。一切器皿的银子，按圣所的舍客勒，共有二千四百舍客勒。 ###EN### Each silver plate weighing one hundred thirty shekels, and each bowl seventy; all the silver of the vessels was two thousand four hundred shekels, according to the shekel of the sanctuary;
Verse_Ch: 7:86 十二个金盂盛满了香，按圣所的舍客勒，每盂重十舍客勒，所有的金子共一百二十舍客勒。 ###EN### The twelve golden spoons, full of incense, weighing ten shekels each, according to the shekel of the sanctuary; all the gold of the spoons was one hundred twenty shekels;
Verse_Ch: 7:87 作燔祭的牲口，共有公牛十二只，公绵羊十二只，一岁的公羊羔十二只，并同献的素祭；作赎罪祭的，共有公山羊十二只； ###EN### All the livestock for the burnt offering: twelve bulls, twelve rams, twelve male lambs a year old and their meal offering; and twelve males of the goats for a sin offering;
Verse_Ch: 7:88 作平安祭的牲口，共有公牛二十四只，公绵羊六十只，公山羊六十只，一岁的公羊羔六十只。这就是用膏抹坛之后，为行献坛之礼所献的。 ###EN### And all the livestock for the sacrifice of peace offerings: twenty-four bulls, sixty rams, sixty male goats, sixty male lambs a year old. This was the dedication of the altar, after it was anointed.
Verse_Ch: 7:89 摩西进会幕要与耶和华说话的时候，听见见证柜的遮罪盖以上、二基路伯中间，有向他说话的声音，他就向耶和华说话。 ###EN### And when Moses went into the Tent of Meeting to speak with Him, he heard the voice speaking to him from above the expiation cover that was upon the Ark of the Testimony, from between the two cherubim; and he spoke to Him.
Chapter_Header: 8
Verse_Ch: 8:1 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 8:2 你要对亚伦说，你放上灯盏的时候，七盏灯都要向灯台前面发光。 ###EN### Speak to Aaron and say to him, When you set up the lamps, the seven lamps will give light in front of the lampstand.
Verse_Ch: 8:3 亚伦便这样行；他把灯盏放上，使灯向灯台前面发光，正如耶和华所吩咐摩西的。 ###EN### And Aaron did so; he set up its lamps to give light in front of the lampstand, as Jehovah had commanded Moses.
Verse_Ch: 8:4 灯台的作法是用金子锤出来的，连座带花都是锤出来的；摩西制造灯台，是照耶和华所指示他的样式。 ###EN### Now this was the workmanship of the lampstand, beaten work of gold. From its base to its flowers it was beaten work; according to the pattern which Jehovah had shown Moses, so he made the lampstand.
Verse_Ch: 8:5 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 8:6 你要从以色列人中选取利未人，并洁净他们。 ###EN### Take the Levites from among the children of Israel and cleanse them.
Verse_Ch: 8:7 洁净他们当这样行：把洁净水弹在他们身上，又叫他们用剃刀刮全身，洗衣服，洁净自己。 ###EN### And thus you shall do to them to cleanse them: Sprinkle the water of purification upon them, and let them pass a razor over all their flesh and wash their clothes and cleanse themselves.
Verse_Ch: 8:8 然后叫他们取一只公牛犊，并同献的素祭，就是调油的细面；你要另取一只公牛犊作赎罪祭。 ###EN### Then let them take a bull of the herd and its meal offering, fine flour mingled with oil; and a second bull of the herd you shall take for a sin offering.
Verse_Ch: 8:9 你要将利未人奉到会幕前，并招聚以色列全会众； ###EN### And you shall present the Levites before the Tent of Meeting, and gather the whole assembly of the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 8:10 你将利未人奉到耶和华面前，以色列人要按手在他们头上。 ###EN### And you shall present the Levites before Jehovah, and the children of Israel shall lay their hands upon the Levites.
Verse_Ch: 8:11 亚伦要将利未人献在耶和华面前，作为以色列人的摇祭，使他们办耶和华的事。 ###EN### And Aaron shall offer the Levites before Jehovah as a wave offering from the children of Israel, that they may do the service of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 8:12 利未人要按手在那两只牛的头上；你要将一只作赎罪祭，一只作燔祭，献给耶和华，为利未人遮罪。 ###EN### And the Levites shall lay their hands upon the heads of the bulls, and you shall offer the one as a sin offering and the other as a burnt offering to Jehovah to make expiation for the Levites.
Verse_Ch: 8:13 你也要使利未人站在亚伦和他儿子面前，将他们作为摇祭献给耶和华。 ###EN### And you shall set the Levites before Aaron and before his sons, and offer them as a wave offering to Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 8:14 这样，你从以色列人中将利未人分别出来，利未人便是我的。 ###EN### Thus you shall separate the Levites from among the children of Israel, and the Levites shall be Mine.
Verse_Ch: 8:15 此后利未人要进去办会幕的事。你要洁净他们，将他们作为摇祭献上； ###EN### Then after this the Levites may go in to do the service of the Tent of Meeting. So you shall cleanse them and offer them as a wave offering.
Verse_Ch: 8:16 因为他们是从以色列人中全然给我的，我选取他们归我，代替以色列人中一切首胎头生的。 ###EN### For they are wholly given to Me from among the children of Israel; I have taken them for Myself instead of everyone who opens the womb, the firstborn of all the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 8:17 以色列人中一切头生的，连人带牲畜，都是我的。我在埃及地击杀一切头生的那天，将他们分别为圣归我。 ###EN### For all the firstborn among the children of Israel are Mine, both human and animal. On the day that I struck down all the firstborn in the land of Egypt I sanctified them for Myself.
Verse_Ch: 8:18 我已选取利未人代替以色列人中一切头生的。 ###EN### And I have taken the Levites instead of all the firstborn among the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 8:19 我从以色列人中将利未人赐给亚伦和他的子孙，在会幕中办以色列人的事，又为以色列人遮罪，免得他们挨近圣所，有灾殃临到他们中间。 ###EN### And I have given the Levites as a gift to Aaron and to his sons from among the children of Israel, to do the service of the children of Israel in the Tent of Meeting, and to make expiation for the children of Israel, that there may be no plague among the children of Israel, when the children of Israel come near to the sanctuary.
Verse_Ch: 8:20 摩西、亚伦、并以色列人的全会众便向利未人如此行；凡耶和华指着利未人所吩咐摩西的，以色列人就向他们照样行。 ###EN### Thus did Moses and Aaron and the whole assembly of the children of Israel do to the Levites; according to all that Jehovah had commanded Moses concerning the Levites, so the children of Israel did to them.
Verse_Ch: 8:21 于是利未人洁净了自己的罪，洗了衣服；亚伦将他们作为摇祭献在耶和华面前，又为他们遮罪，洁净他们。 ###EN### And the Levites purified themselves from sin and washed their clothes. Then Aaron offered them as a wave offering before Jehovah, and Aaron made expiation for them to cleanse them.
Verse_Ch: 8:22 然后利未人进去，在亚伦和他儿子面前，在会幕中办事；耶和华指着利未人怎样吩咐摩西，以色列人就怎样向他们行。 ###EN### And after this the Levites went in to do their service in the Tent of Meeting before Aaron and before his sons; as Jehovah had commanded Moses concerning the Levites, so they did to them.
Verse_Ch: 8:23 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 8:24 关于利未人的事奉，乃是这样：从二十五岁以上，他们要进来事奉，办会幕的事， ###EN### This is what applies to the Levites: From twenty-five years old and upward they shall go in to perform the service in the work of the Tent of Meeting.
Verse_Ch: 8:25 到了五十岁，他们要从事奉的工作上退去，不再办事； ###EN### And from the age of fifty years they shall retire from the service in the work and shall serve no more.
Verse_Ch: 8:26 他们可以在会幕里，帮助他们的弟兄，谨守所吩咐的，但自己不再办事了。关于所吩咐利未人的，你要这样向他们行。 ###EN### But they may minister to their brothers in the Tent of Meeting, to keep the charge, but they themselves shall do no service. Thus you shall do with the Levites concerning their charges.
Chapter_Header: 9
Verse_Ch: 9:1 以色列人出埃及地以后，第二年正月，耶和华在西乃的旷野对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses in the wilderness of Sinai in the first month of the second year after they had come out of the land of Egypt, saying,
Verse_Ch: 9:2 以色列人应当在所定的日期守逾越节。 ###EN### Let the children of Israel keep the passover at its appointed time.
Verse_Ch: 9:3 本月十四日黄昏的时候，你们要在所定的日期守这节，要按这节的一切律例和一切典章而守。 ###EN### On the fourteenth day of this month at twilight, you shall keep it at its appointed time; according to all its statutes and according to all its ordinances you shall keep it.
Verse_Ch: 9:4 于是摩西告诉以色列人要守逾越节。 ###EN### Thus Moses told the children of Israel to keep the passover.
Verse_Ch: 9:5 他们就在西乃的旷野，正月十四日黄昏的时候，守逾越节；凡耶和华所吩咐摩西的，以色列人都照样行了。 ###EN### And they kept the passover in the first month, on the fourteenth day of the month, at twilight, in the wilderness of Sinai; according to all that Jehovah commanded Moses, so the children of Israel did.
Verse_Ch: 9:6 有几个人因接触死人不洁净，以致不能在那日守逾越节；当日他们来到摩西、亚伦面前， ###EN### And there were certain men who were unclean through contact with a dead person, so that they could not keep the passover on that day; so they came before Moses and before Aaron on that day.
Verse_Ch: 9:7 说，我们虽因接触死人不洁净，为何被阻止，不得在以色列人中间，在所定的日期献耶和华的供物呢？ ###EN### And those men said to him, Although we are unclean through contact with a dead person, why must we be kept from presenting the offering of Jehovah at its appointed time among the children of Israel?
Verse_Ch: 9:8 摩西对他们说，你们暂且等候，我可以去听耶和华指着你们有什么吩咐。 ###EN### And Moses said to them, Stay here, so I may hear what Jehovah will command concerning you.
Verse_Ch: 9:9 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 9:10 你要对以色列人说，你们和你们后代中，若有人因接触死人不洁净，或在远方旅途上，他仍要向耶和华守逾越节。 ###EN### Speak to the children of Israel, saying, Any one of you or your descendants who becomes unclean through contact with a dead person or is on a distant journey shall still keep the passover to Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 9:11 他们要在二月十四日黄昏的时候，守逾越节；要用无酵饼与苦菜，和逾越节的羊羔同吃。 ###EN### In the second month on the fourteenth day at twilight they shall keep it; they shall eat it with unleavened bread and bitter herbs.
Verse_Ch: 9:12 羊羔一点不可留到早晨，骨头一根也不可折断；他们要照逾越节的一切律例而守。 ###EN### They shall not leave any of it until the morning, nor break a bone of it; according to every statute of the passover they shall keep it.
Verse_Ch: 9:13 那洁净且不在旅途上的人若不守逾越节，那人要从民中剪除，因为他在所定的日期不献耶和华的供物；那人必担当自己的罪。 ###EN### But the man who is clean and is not on a journey, yet refrains from keeping the passover, that person shall be cut off from his people, because he did not present Jehovah's offering at its appointed time; that man shall bear his sin.
Verse_Ch: 9:14 若有外人寄居在你们中间，愿向耶和华守逾越节，他要照逾越节的律例和典章行。无论是寄居的或是本地人，同归一例。 ###EN### And if a stranger sojourns with you and keeps the passover to Jehovah; according to the statute of the passover and according to its ordinance, so shall he do. You shall have one statute, both for the sojourner and for the native born in the land.
Verse_Ch: 9:15 立起帐幕的那日，有云彩遮盖帐幕，就是见证的帐幕；从晚上到早晨，云彩在其上，形状如火。 ###EN### And on the day that the tabernacle was set up, the cloud covered the tabernacle, the Tent of the Testimony; and in the evening it was like the appearance of fire over the tabernacle until morning.
Verse_Ch: 9:16 常是这样；白昼云彩遮盖帐幕，夜间形状如火。 ###EN### So it was always; the cloud covered it by day, and the appearance of fire by night.
Verse_Ch: 9:17 云彩几时从帐幕收上去，以色列人就几时起行；云彩在那里停住，以色列人就在那里安营。 ###EN### And whenever the cloud was taken up from over the tent, then after that the children of Israel set out; and in the place where the cloud settled, there the children of Israel encamped.
Verse_Ch: 9:18 以色列人遵耶和华的吩咐起行，也遵耶和华的吩咐安营； ###EN### At the commandment of Jehovah the children of Israel set out, and at the commandment of Jehovah they encamped; as long as the cloud settled upon the tabernacle, they remained encamped.
Verse_Ch: 9:19 云彩在帐幕上停住几时，他们就住营几时。云彩在帐幕上停留许多日子，以色列人就遵耶和华的吩咐不起行。 ###EN### Even when the cloud extended its time over the tabernacle for many days, the children of Israel kept the charge of Jehovah and did not set out.
Verse_Ch: 9:20 有时云彩在帐幕上几天，他们就照耶和华的吩咐住营，然后照耶和华的吩咐起行。 ###EN### If sometimes the cloud was upon the tabernacle a few days, according to the commandment of Jehovah they remained encamped; then at the commandment of Jehovah they set out.
Verse_Ch: 9:21 有时从晚上到早晨，这云彩停着；早晨云彩收上去的时候，他们就起行。或者白昼夜间云彩都停着；云彩收上去的时候，他们就起行。 ###EN### If sometimes the cloud remained from evening until morning, when the cloud was taken up in the morning, they set out; or if it remained in the daytime and at night, when the cloud was taken up, they set out.
Verse_Ch: 9:22 云彩住留在帐幕上，无论是两天，或是一个月，或是更长时日，以色列人就住营不起行；但云彩收上去的时候，他们就起行。 ###EN### Whether it was two days or a month or a longer time that the cloud extended its time over the tabernacle and settled above it, the children of Israel remained encamped and did not set out; but when it was taken up, they set out.
Verse_Ch: 9:23 他们遵耶和华的吩咐安营，也遵耶和华的吩咐起行。他们守耶和华所吩咐的，都是照耶和华藉摩西所吩咐的。 ###EN### At the commandment of Jehovah they encamped, and at the commandment of Jehovah they set out. They kept the charge of Jehovah according to the commandment of Jehovah through Moses.
Chapter_Header: 10
Verse_Ch: 10:1 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 10:2 你要作两枝银号，都要锤出来的，用以招聚会众，并叫众营起行。 ###EN### Make yourself two trumpets of silver; of beaten work you shall make them; and you shall use them for summoning the assembly and for the setting out of the camps.
Verse_Ch: 10:3 吹这两枝号的时候，全会众要到你那里，聚集在会幕门口。 ###EN### And when they blow them, all the assembly shall gather themselves to you at the entrance of the Tent of Meeting.
Verse_Ch: 10:4 若单吹一枝，众首领，就是以色列军中的统领，要聚集到你那里。 ###EN### But if they blow only one, then the leaders, the heads of the thousands of Israel, shall gather themselves to you.
Verse_Ch: 10:5 吹出大声的时候，那安在东边的营都要起行。 ###EN### And when you blow an alarm, the camps that are encamped on the east side shall set out.
Verse_Ch: 10:6 第二次吹出大声的时候，那安在南边的营都要起行。吹出大声，是要叫他们起行。 ###EN### And when you blow an alarm the second time, the camps that are encamped on the south side shall set out. They shall blow an alarm for them to set out.
Verse_Ch: 10:7 但招聚会众的时候，你们要吹号，却不要吹出大声。 ###EN### But when the congregation is to be gathered together, you shall blow, but you shall not sound an alarm.
Verse_Ch: 10:8 亚伦子孙作祭司的要吹这两枝号；这要作你们世世代代永远的定例。 ###EN### And the sons of Aaron, the priests, shall blow the trumpets; and this shall be for you a perpetual statute throughout your generations.
Verse_Ch: 10:9 你们在自己的地，与欺压你们的敌人打仗，就要用号吹出大声，使你们在耶和华你们的神面前得蒙记念，也蒙拯救脱离仇敌。 ###EN### And when you go to war in your land against the adversary who oppresses you, then you shall sound an alarm with the trumpets, so that you may be remembered before Jehovah your God and be saved from your enemies.
Verse_Ch: 10:10 在你们欢乐的日子和所定的节期，并月朔，你们献燔祭和平安祭的时候，也要吹号；这都要在你们的神面前作为记念；我是耶和华你们的神。 ###EN### Also on your days of rejoicing and at your appointed feasts and at the beginnings of your months, you shall blow the trumpets over your burnt offerings and over the sacrifices of your peace offerings; and they shall be a reminder on your behalf before your God; I am Jehovah your God.
Verse_Ch: 10:11 第二年二月二十日，云彩从见证的帐幕收上去。 ###EN### Now it was in the second year, in the second month, on the twentieth day of the month, that the cloud was taken up from over the Tabernacle of the Testimony.
Verse_Ch: 10:12 以色列人就从西乃的旷野按站往前行；云彩停住在巴兰的旷野。 ###EN### And the children of Israel set out on their journeys from the wilderness of Sinai. Then the cloud settled down in the wilderness of Paran.
Verse_Ch: 10:13 他们照耶和华藉摩西所吩咐的，初次往前行。 ###EN### And they set out for the first time according to the commandment of Jehovah through Moses.
Verse_Ch: 10:14 犹大营的纛，按着军队首先往前行；统领军队的，是亚米拿达的儿子拿顺。 ###EN### And the standard of the camp of the children of Judah set out first according to their companies; and over the entire company was Nahshon the son of Amminadab.
Verse_Ch: 10:15 统领以萨迦支派军队的，是苏押的儿子拿坦业。 ###EN### And over the company of the tribe of the children of Issachar was Nethanel the son of Zuar.
Verse_Ch: 10:16 统领西布伦支派军队的，是希伦的儿子以利押。 ###EN### And over the company of the tribe of the children of Zebulun was Eliab the son of Helon.
Verse_Ch: 10:17 帐幕拆卸，革顺的子孙和米拉利的子孙就抬着帐幕往前行。 ###EN### And the tabernacle was taken down; and the sons of Gershon and the sons of Merari, who carried the tabernacle, set out.
Verse_Ch: 10:18 流便营的纛，按着军队往前行；统领军队的，是示丢珥的儿子以利蓿。 ###EN### And the standard of the camp of Reuben set out according to their companies; and over the entire company was Elizur the son of Shedeur.
Verse_Ch: 10:19 统领西缅支派军队的，是苏利沙代的儿子示路蔑。 ###EN### And over the company of the tribe of the children of Simeon was Shelumiel the son of Zurishaddai.
Verse_Ch: 10:20 统领迦得支派军队的，是丢珥的儿子以利雅萨。 ###EN### And over the company of the tribe of the children of Gad was Eliasaph the son of Deuel.
Verse_Ch: 10:21 哥辖人抬着圣物往前行；他们到达以前，帐幕已经支搭好了。 ###EN### And the Kohathites, who carried the holy things, set out; and the tabernacle was set up before their arrival.
Verse_Ch: 10:22 以法莲营的纛，按着军队往前行；统领军队的，是亚米忽的儿子以利沙玛。 ###EN### And the standard of the camp of the children of Ephraim set out according to their companies; and over the entire company was Elishama the son of Ammihud.
Verse_Ch: 10:23 统领玛拿西支派军队的，是比大蓿的儿子迦玛列。 ###EN### And over the company of the tribe of the children of Manasseh was Gamaliel the son of Pedahzur.
Verse_Ch: 10:24 统领便雅悯支派军队的，是基多尼的儿子亚比但。 ###EN### And over the company of the tribe of the children of Benjamin was Abidan the son of Gideoni.
Verse_Ch: 10:25 但营的纛是诸营的后队，按着军队往前行；统领军队的，是亚米沙代的儿子亚希以谢。 ###EN### And the standard of the camp of the children of Dan, which was the rear guard of all the camps, set out according to their companies; and over the entire company was Ahiezer the son of Ammishaddai.
Verse_Ch: 10:26 统领亚设支派军队的，是俄兰的儿子帕结。 ###EN### And over the company of the tribe of the children of Asher was Pagiel the son of Ochran.
Verse_Ch: 10:27 统领拿弗他利支派军队的，是以南的儿子亚希拉。 ###EN### And over the company of the tribe of the children of Naphtali was Ahira the son of Enan.
Verse_Ch: 10:28 以色列人按着军队往前行，次序就是这样。 ###EN### This was the order in which the children of Israel set out according to their companies, when they set out.
Verse_Ch: 10:29 摩西对他岳父米甸人流珥的儿子何巴说，我们要往前行，到耶和华所说之地去；祂曾说，我要将这地赐给你们。现在求你和我们同去，我们必善待 你，因为耶和华已经应许给以色列人好处。 ###EN### And Moses said to Hobab the son of Reuel the Midianite, Moses' father-in-law, We are setting out to the place concerning which Jehovah said, I will give it to you. Come with us, and we will treat you well, for Jehovah has promised good to Israel.
Verse_Ch: 10:30 何巴回答说，我不去；我要往我本地本族那里去。 ###EN### But he said to him, I will not go; but rather I will go to my own land and to my relatives.
Verse_Ch: 10:31 摩西说，求你不要离开我们，因为你知道我们在旷野能安营的地方，你可以作我们的眼目。 ###EN### So Moses said, Please do not leave us, for you know where we can encamp in the wilderness, and you will be eyes for us.
Verse_Ch: 10:32 你若和我们同去，将来耶和华有什么好处待我们，我们也必以什么好处待你。 ###EN### And if you go with us, whatever good Jehovah does for us, we will do for you.
Verse_Ch: 10:33 以色列人从耶和华的山往前行，走了三天的路程；在这三天的路程中，耶和华的约柜在他们前头往前行，为他们寻找安歇的地方。 ###EN### So they set out from the mountain of Jehovah three days' journey, with the Ark of the Covenant of Jehovah setting out before them three days' journey, to seek out a resting place for them.
Verse_Ch: 10:34 他们拔营往前行，日间有耶和华的云彩在他们以上。 ###EN### And the cloud of Jehovah was over them by day when they set out from the camp.
Verse_Ch: 10:35 约柜往前行的时候，摩西就说，耶和华阿，求你兴起，愿你的仇敌四散；愿恨你的人从你面前逃跑。 ###EN### And when the Ark set out, Moses said, Rise up, O Jehovah, and let Your enemies be scattered; And let those who hate You flee before You.
Verse_Ch: 10:36 约柜停住的时候，他就说，耶和华阿，求你回到以色列的千万人中。 ###EN### And when it came to rest, he said, Return, O Jehovah, to the ten thousands of the thousands of Israel.
Chapter_Header: 11
Verse_Ch: 11:1 百姓因艰苦发怨言，声音达到耶和华的耳中；耶和华听见了就怒气发作，耶和华的火便在他们中间焚烧，烧灭了在营边界的一些人。 ###EN### And the people became like those who murmur about their misfortune in the ears of Jehovah; and when Jehovah heard it, His anger was kindled, and the fire of Jehovah burned among them and consumed some at the outskirts of the camp.
Verse_Ch: 11:2 百姓向摩西哀求，摩西祈求耶和华，火就熄了。 ###EN### And the people cried to Moses; and Moses prayed to Jehovah, and the fire abated.
Verse_Ch: 11:3 那地方便名叫他备拉，因为耶和华的火烧在他们中间。 ###EN### And the name of that place was called Taberah, because the fire of Jehovah had burned among them.
Verse_Ch: 11:4 他们中间的闲杂人大起贪欲；以色列人又哭号说，谁给我们肉吃呢？ ###EN### And the mixed multitude that was among them lusted exceedingly; and the children of Israel also wept again and said, Who shall give us meat to eat?
Verse_Ch: 11:5 我们记得，在埃及的时候不花钱就有鱼吃，还有黄瓜、西瓜、韭菜、葱、蒜。 ###EN### We remember the fish which we used to eat in Egypt for nothing, the cucumbers and the melons and the leeks and the onions and the garlic;
Verse_Ch: 11:6 现在我们的胃口都没有了，我们眼前除了这吗哪以外，什么也没有。 ###EN### But now our appetite has gone; there is nothing at all but this manna to look at.
Verse_Ch: 11:7 这吗哪仿佛芫荽子，样子好像珍珠。 ###EN### Now the manna was like coriander seed, and its appearance like the appearance of bdellium.
Verse_Ch: 11:8 百姓周围行走，把吗哪收起来，或用磨碾，或用臼捣，在锅里煮，又作成饼；滋味好像烤的油饼。 ###EN### The people went about and gathered it and ground it between two millstones or beat it in a mortar; then they boiled it in pots and made cakes of it; and its taste was like the taste of cakes baked in oil.
Verse_Ch: 11:9 夜间露水降在营中的时候，吗哪也随着降下。 ###EN### And when the dew fell on the camp at night, the manna would fall with it.
Verse_Ch: 11:10 摩西听见百姓各在各家的帐棚门口哭号；耶和华的怒气便大发作，摩西也不喜悦。 ###EN### And Moses heard the people weeping family by families, each at the entrance of his tent; and the anger of Jehovah was kindled greatly, and Moses was displeased.
Verse_Ch: 11:11 摩西对耶和华说，你为何苦待仆人？我为何不在你眼前蒙恩，你竟把照管这百姓的重担加在我身上？ ###EN### And Moses said to Jehovah, Why have You treated Your servant badly, and why have I not found favor in Your sight, that You have put the burden of all this people upon me?
Verse_Ch: 11:12 这百姓岂是我怀的胎，岂是我生下来的呢？你竟对我说，把他们抱在怀里，如养育之父抱吃奶的孩子，直抱到你起誓要赐给他们祖宗的地去。 ###EN### Did I conceive all this people? Or did I bring them forth, so that You should say to me, Carry them in your bosom, as a nurse carries the nursing child, to the land which You swore to give to their fathers?
Verse_Ch: 11:13 我从那里得肉给这百姓吃呢？他们都向我哭号说，你给我们肉吃罢！ ###EN### From where should I get meat to give to all this people? For they weep before me, saying, Give us meat, so that we may eat!
Verse_Ch: 11:14 管这百姓的担子太重了，我独自担当不起。 ###EN### I am not able to bear all this people alone, for it is too heavy for me.
Verse_Ch: 11:15 你这样待我，我若在你眼前蒙恩，求你立时将我杀了，不叫我看见自己的苦楚。 ###EN### And if this is the way You deal with me, please kill me at once-if I have found favor in Your sight-and do not let me see my wretchedness.
Verse_Ch: 11:16 耶和华对摩西说，你从以色列的长老中招聚七十个人，就是你所知道作百姓的长老和官长的，到我这里来，领他们到会幕前，使他们和你一同站立。 ###EN### So Jehovah said to Moses, Gather to Me seventy, each one from the elders of Israel, whom you know are the elders of the people and their officers, and bring them to the Tent of Meeting, and have them stand there with you.
Verse_Ch: 11:17 我要在那里降临，与你说话；我要把你身上的灵，也放在他们身上，他们就要和你同担这照管百姓的担子，免得你独自担当。 ###EN### Then I will come down and talk with you there, and I will take of the Spirit who is upon you and will put Him upon them; and they shall bear the burden of the people with you, so that you do not bear it alone.
Verse_Ch: 11:18 又要对百姓说，你们应当将自己分别为圣，预备明天吃肉，因为你们哭号说，谁给我们肉吃？我们在埃及很好。这声音达到了耶和华的耳中，所以祂 必给你们肉吃。 ###EN### And you shall say to the people, Sanctify yourselves for tomorrow, and you shall eat meat; for you have wept in the ears of Jehovah, saying, Who will give us meat to eat? For it was well with us in Egypt. Therefore Jehovah will give you meat, and you shall eat.
Verse_Ch: 11:19 你们不是吃一天、两天、五天、十天、二十天， ###EN### You shall eat not one day, nor two days, nor five days, nor ten days, nor twenty days,
Verse_Ch: 11:20 乃是要吃整个月，直到肉从你们鼻孔里喷出来，使你们厌恶了，因为你们弃绝那在你们中间的耶和华，在祂面前哭号说，我们为何出了埃及呢？ ###EN### But a whole month, until it comes out from your nostrils, and becomes loathsome to you, because you have rejected Jehovah who is among you, and have wept before Him, saying, Why did we ever come out of Egypt?
Verse_Ch: 11:21 但摩西说，这与我同住的百姓，步行的男丁有六十万，你还说，我要把肉给他们，使他们可以吃整个月。 ###EN### But Moses said, The people, among whom I am, are six hundred thousand on foot; and You have said, I will give them meat so that they may eat a whole month.
Verse_Ch: 11:22 难道为他们宰羊群牛群，就够他们吃么？或是为他们聚拢海中所有的鱼，就够他们吃么？ ###EN### Will flocks and herds be slain for them, to satisfy them? Or will all the fish of the sea be gathered together for them, to satisfy them?
Verse_Ch: 11:23 耶和华对摩西说，耶和华的手臂岂是缩短了么？现在你要看我的话向你应验不应验。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to Moses, Has Jehovah's hand become short? Now you will see whether My word will come to pass for you or not.
Verse_Ch: 11:24 于是摩西出去，将耶和华的话告诉百姓，又招聚百姓的长老中七十个人来，使他们站在会幕的四围。 ###EN### So Moses went out and told the people the words of Jehovah, and he gathered seventy, each one from the elders of the people, and set them around the tent.
Verse_Ch: 11:25 耶和华在云中降临，对摩西说话，并且把他身上的灵，也放在那七十个长老身上。灵停歇在他们身上的时候，他们就申言，以后却没有再申言。 ###EN### And Jehovah came down in the cloud and spoke to him, and He took of the Spirit who was upon him, and put Him upon the seventy elders. And when the Spirit rested upon them, they prophesied, but they did not do so again.
Verse_Ch: 11:26 但有两个人仍留在营里，一个名叫伊利达，一个名叫米达。他们本是在那些登录的人中，却没有到会幕那里去。灵停歇在他们身上，他们就在营里 申言。 ###EN### But two men had remained in the camp, the name of the one was Eldad, and the name of the other Medad. And the Spirit rested upon them. (Now they were among those who were registered, but they had not gone out to the tent.) And they prophesied in the camp.
Verse_Ch: 11:27 有个少年人跑来告诉摩西说，伊利达和米达在营里申言。 ###EN### And a certain young man ran and told Moses and said, Eldad and Medad are prophesying in the camp.
Verse_Ch: 11:28 摩西的帮手，嫩的儿子约书亚，就是摩西所拣选的一个人，说，请我主摩西禁止他们。 ###EN### And Joshua the son of Nun, the attendant of Moses, one of his chosen men, answered and said, My lord Moses, restrain them!
Verse_Ch: 11:29 摩西对他说，你为我的缘故嫉妒人么？惟愿耶和华的百姓都是申言者，愿耶和华把祂的灵放在他们身上！ ###EN### But Moses said to him, Are you jealous for my sake? Oh that all Jehovah's people were prophets, that Jehovah would put His Spirit upon them!
Verse_Ch: 11:30 于是，摩西和以色列的长老都回到营里去。 ###EN### And Moses returned to the camp, he and the elders of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 11:31 有风从耶和华那里刮起，把鹌鹑由海面刮来，散落在营边；这边约有一天的路程，那边约有一天的路程，布满营的四围，离地面约有二肘。 ###EN### And a wind went forth from Jehovah and brought quails from the sea, and let them fall beside the camp, about a day's journey on this side and a day's journey on the other side, all around the camp, and about two cubits above the surface of the earth.
Verse_Ch: 11:32 百姓起来，终日终夜，并次日一整天，捕取鹌鹑；至少的也捕取了十贺梅珥，为自己摆在营的四围。 ###EN### And the people rose up all that day and all the night and all the next day, and they gathered the quail. He who gathered least gathered ten homers. And they spread them out for themselves all around the camp.
Verse_Ch: 11:33 肉在他们牙齿之间尚未嚼烂，耶和华的怒气就向他们发作，用极重的灾殃击杀了他们。 ###EN### While the meat was still between their teeth, before it was chewed, the anger of Jehovah was kindled against the people, and Jehovah struck the people with a very severe plague.
Verse_Ch: 11:34 那地方便名叫基博罗哈他瓦，因为他们在那里葬埋了那些起贪欲的人。 ###EN### And the name of that place was called Kibroth-hattaavah, because there they buried the people who lusted.
Verse_Ch: 11:35 百姓从基博罗哈他瓦往前行，到了哈洗录，就住在哈洗录。 ###EN### From Kibroth-hattaavah the people journeyed to Hazeroth, and they remained at Hazeroth.
Chapter_Header: 12
Verse_Ch: 12:1 米利暗和亚伦因摩西所娶的古实女子就毁谤他，(因为摩西娶了一个古实女子，) ###EN### And Miriam and Aaron spoke against Moses because of the Cushite woman whom he had married (for he had married a Cushite woman).
Verse_Ch: 12:2 他们说，难道耶和华只借着摩西说话，祂不也借着我们说话么？这话耶和华听见了。 ###EN### And they said, Has Jehovah indeed spoken only through Moses? Has He not also spoken through us? And Jehovah heard it.
Verse_Ch: 12:3 摩西这人极其谦和，胜过地上的众人。 ###EN### Now the man Moses was very meek, more than anyone else who was on the surface of the earth.
Verse_Ch: 12:4 耶和华忽然对摩西、亚伦、米利暗说，你们三个人都出来，到会幕这里。他们三个人就出来。 ###EN### And suddenly Jehovah spoke to Moses and to Aaron and to Miriam, You three come out to the Tent of Meeting. So the three of them came out.
Verse_Ch: 12:5 耶和华在云柱中降临，站在会幕门口，召亚伦和米利暗；二人出来了， ###EN### Then Jehovah came down in a pillar of cloud and stood at the entrance of the tent, and called Aaron and Miriam. And when they had both come forward,
Verse_Ch: 12:6 耶和华就说，你们且听我的话：你们中间若有申言者，我耶和华必在异象中使他认识我，我要在梦中与他说话。 ###EN### He said, Hear now My words: If there is a prophet among you, I, Jehovah, will make Myself known to him in a vision, I will speak with him in a dream.
Verse_Ch: 12:7 我的仆人摩西不是这样；他在我全家是忠信的。 ###EN### My servant Moses is not so; He is faithful in all My house.
Verse_Ch: 12:8 我与他面对面说话，乃是明说，不用谜语，他也看见我耶和华的形像。你们毁谤我的仆人摩西，为何不惧怕呢？ ###EN### With him I speak face to face, even openly, and not in riddles; And he beholds the form of Jehovah. Why then were you not afraid to speak against My servant, against Moses?
Verse_Ch: 12:9 耶和华向他们二人发怒，就离开了。 ###EN### And the anger of Jehovah was kindled against them, and He departed.
Verse_Ch: 12:10 云彩从会幕上挪开了，不料，米利暗患了痲疯，像雪那样白。亚伦转向米利暗，见她患了痲疯， ###EN### And when the cloud had departed from over the tent; there Miriam was, leprous, as white as snow. And Aaron turned toward Miriam, and there she was, leprous.
Verse_Ch: 12:11 就对摩西说，我主阿，求你不要将我们愚昧所犯的这罪，加在我们身上。 ###EN### And Aaron said to Moses, Oh, my lord, please do not lay this sin upon us that we have so foolishly committed.
Verse_Ch: 12:12 求你不要使她像那出母腹，肉已半烂的死胎。 ###EN### Please do not let her be like one dead, whose flesh is half consumed when he comes out of his mother's womb.
Verse_Ch: 12:13 于是摩西哀求耶和华说，神阿，求你医治她。 ###EN### And Moses cried to Jehovah, saying, Please heal her, O God, please.
Verse_Ch: 12:14 耶和华对摩西说，她父亲若吐唾沫在她脸上，她岂不蒙羞七天么？现在要把她在营外隔离七天，然后才可以领她进来。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to Moses, If her father had just spat in her face, would she not bear her shame seven days? Let her be shut up outside the camp seven days, and after that she may be brought in again.
Verse_Ch: 12:15 于是米利暗被隔离在营外七天。百姓没有往前行，直到把米利暗领进来。 ###EN### So Miriam was shut up outside the camp seven days, and the people did not set out until Miriam had been brought in again.
Verse_Ch: 12:16 以后百姓从哈洗录起行，在巴兰的旷野安营。 ###EN### After that the people set out from Hazeroth and encamped in the wilderness of Paran.
Chapter_Header: 13
Verse_Ch: 13:1 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
