Verse_Ch: 13:2 你打发人去窥探我所赐给以色列人的迦南地，他们每宗族支派中要打发一个人，都要作首领的。 ###EN### Send men to spy out the land of Canaan, which I am giving to the children of Israel; one man from each of their fathers' tribes you shall send, every one a leader among them.
Verse_Ch: 13:3 摩西就照耶和华的吩咐，从巴兰的旷野打发他们去；他们都是以色列人的首领。 ###EN### So Moses sent them from the wilderness of Paran according to the commandment of Jehovah, all of them leading men among the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 13:4 他们的名字如下：属流便支派的，是撒刻的儿子沙母亚； ###EN### And these were their names: from the tribe of Reuben, Shammua the son of Zaccur;
Verse_Ch: 13:5 属西缅支派的，是何利的儿子沙法； ###EN### From the tribe of Simeon, Shaphat the son of Hori;
Verse_Ch: 13:6 属犹大支派的，是耶孚尼的儿子迦勒； ###EN### From the tribe of Judah, Caleb the son of Jephunneh;
Verse_Ch: 13:7 属以萨迦支派的，是约色的儿子以迦； ###EN### From the tribe of Issachar, Igal the son of Joseph;
Verse_Ch: 13:8 属以法莲支派的，是嫩的儿子何西阿； ###EN### From the tribe of Ephraim, Hoshea the son of Nun;
Verse_Ch: 13:9 属便雅悯支派的，是拉孚的儿子帕提； ###EN### From the tribe of Benjamin, Palti the son of Raphu;
Verse_Ch: 13:10 属西布伦支派的，是梭底的儿子迦叠； ###EN### From the tribe of Zebulun, Gaddiel the son of Sodi;
Verse_Ch: 13:11 属约瑟支派的，就是属玛拿西支派的，是稣西的儿子迦底； ###EN### From the tribe of Joseph, that is, from the tribe of Manasseh, Gaddi the son of Susi;
Verse_Ch: 13:12 属但支派的，是基玛利的儿子亚米利； ###EN### From the tribe of Dan, Ammiel the son of Gemalli;
Verse_Ch: 13:13 属亚设支派的，是米迦勒的儿子西帖； ###EN### From the tribe of Asher, Sethur the son of Michael;
Verse_Ch: 13:14 属拿弗他利支派的，是缚西的儿子拿比； ###EN### From the tribe of Naphtali, Nahbi the son of Vophsi;
Verse_Ch: 13:15 属迦得支派的，是玛基的儿子臼利。 ###EN### From the tribe of Gad, Geuel the son of Machi.
Verse_Ch: 13:16 这些就是摩西打发去窥探那地之人的名字。摩西称嫩的儿子何西阿为约书亚。 ###EN### These are the names of the men whom Moses sent to spy out the land. And Moses called Hoshea the son of Nun Joshua.
Verse_Ch: 13:17 摩西打发他们去窥探迦南地，对他们说，你们从这里上南地，然后上山地去， ###EN### And when Moses sent them to spy out the land of Canaan, he said to them, Go up this way into the Negev, and go up into the hill country;
Verse_Ch: 13:18 看那地如何，其中所住的民是强是弱，是多是少， ###EN### And see what the land is like; and whether the people who live in it are strong or weak, whether they are few or many;
Verse_Ch: 13:19 他们所住之地是好是坏，所住之处是营盘是坚城， ###EN### And whether the land in which they dwell is good or bad; and whether the cities that they live in are like camps or with fortifications;
Verse_Ch: 13:20 那地是肥美是贫瘠，其中有树木没有。你们要壮胆，把那地的果子带些来。那时正是葡萄初熟的时候。 ###EN### And whether the land is fat or lean; whether there are trees in it or not. Therefore strengthen yourselves and bring some of the fruit of the land. Now the time was the time of the first ripe grapes.
Verse_Ch: 13:21 他们就上去窥探那地，从寻的旷野到利合，靠近哈马口。 ###EN### So they went up and spied out the land from the wilderness of Zin to Rehob, near the entrance of Hamath.
Verse_Ch: 13:22 他们从南地上去，到了希伯仑；在那里有亚衲人的后代亚希幔、示筛、挞买。(原来希伯仑城比埃及的锁安城早建七年。) ###EN### And when they had gone up through the Negev, they came to Hebron; and Ahiman, Sheshai, and Talmai, the descendants of Anak, were there. (Now Hebron was built seven years before Zoan in Egypt.)
Verse_Ch: 13:23 他们到了以实各谷，从那里砍了葡萄树的一枝，上头有一挂葡萄，两个人用杠抬着，又带了些石榴和无花果来。 ###EN### Then they came to the Valley of Eshcol, and from there they cut down a branch with a single cluster of grapes; and they carried it on a pole between two of them. They also cut off some of the pomegranates and some of the figs.
Verse_Ch: 13:24 因为以色列人从那里砍来的那挂葡萄，所以那地方叫作以实各谷。 ###EN### That place was called the Valley of Eshcol, because of the cluster which the children of Israel cut down from there.
Verse_Ch: 13:25 过了四十天，他们窥探那地回来， ###EN### And they returned from spying out the land at the end of forty days.
Verse_Ch: 13:26 到了巴兰旷野的加低斯，来见摩西、亚伦、并以色列人全会众，回报摩西、亚伦、并全会众，又把那地的果子给他们看； ###EN### And they proceeded to come to Moses and to Aaron and to the whole assembly of the children of Israel, to the wilderness of Paran, to Kadesh; and brought back word to them and to the whole assembly, and showed them the fruit of the land.
Verse_Ch: 13:27 又告诉摩西说，我们到了你所打发我们去的那地，果然是流奶与蜜之地；这就是那地的果子。 ###EN### And they told him and said, We came to the land into which you sent us; and it indeed flows with milk and honey, and this is its fruit.
Verse_Ch: 13:28 然而住那地的民强壮，城邑也坚固宽大，并且我们在那里看见了亚衲人的后代。 ###EN### However, the people who dwell in the land are strong, and the cities are fortified and very large; and we also saw the descendants of Anak there.
Verse_Ch: 13:29 亚玛力人住在南地，赫人、耶布斯人、亚摩利人住在山地，迦南人住在海边并约但河沿岸。 ###EN### The Amalekites dwell in the land of the Negev, and the Hittites and the Jebusites and the Amorites dwell in the hill country, and the Canaanites dwell by the sea and along the Jordan.
Verse_Ch: 13:30 迦勒在摩西面前使百姓安静，说，我们立刻上去得那地罢，因为我们足能得胜。 ###EN### But Caleb quieted the people before Moses and said, Let us go up at once and possess it; for we are well able to overcome it.
Verse_Ch: 13:31 但那些和他同去的人说，我们不能上去攻击那民，因为他们比我们强壮。 ###EN### But the men who went up with him said, We are not able to go up against the people, for they are stronger than we.
Verse_Ch: 13:32 那些探子论到所窥探之地，向以色列人报恶信，说，我们所经过、窥探之地，是吞吃居民之地，我们在那里所看见的人民都身量高大。 ###EN### And they brought to the children of Israel an evil report of the land which they had spied out, saying, The land, through which we have gone to spy it out, is a land that eats up its inhabitants; and all the people that we saw in it are men of great size.
Verse_Ch: 13:33 我们在那里看见拿非利人；(亚衲人的子孙就是拿非利人的一支；)我们看自己就如蚱蜢一样，他们看我们也是如此。 ###EN### And there we saw the Nephilim (the descendants of Anak are part of the Nephilim); and we were like grasshoppers in our own sight, and so we were in their sight.
Chapter_Header: 14
Verse_Ch: 14:1 当下全会众放声喧嚷；那夜百姓都哭号。 ###EN### Then the whole assembly lifted up their voice and cried, and the people wept that night.
Verse_Ch: 14:2 以色列众人向摩西、亚伦发怨言；全会众对他们说，巴不得我们早死在埃及地，或是死在这旷野。 ###EN### And all the children of Israel murmured against Moses and against Aaron; and the whole assembly said to them, If only we had died in the land of Egypt! Or if only we had died in this wilderness!
Verse_Ch: 14:3 耶和华为什么把我们领到这地，使我们倒在刀下？我们的妻子和孩子必被掳掠。我们回埃及去，岂不更好么？ ###EN### And why does Jehovah bring us into this land, to fall by the sword? Our wives and our little ones will become plunder. Would it not be better for us to return to Egypt?
Verse_Ch: 14:4 众人彼此说，我们不如立一个首领，回埃及去罢。 ###EN### And they said one to another, Let us appoint a captain, and let us return to Egypt.
Verse_Ch: 14:5 摩西、亚伦就在以色列人全会众前，面伏于地。 ###EN### Then Moses and Aaron fell on their faces before the whole congregation of the assembly of the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 14:6 窥探那地的人中，嫩的儿子约书亚和耶孚尼的儿子迦勒，撕裂衣服， ###EN### And Joshua the son of Nun and Caleb the son of Jephunneh, who were among those who spied out the land, tore their clothes;
Verse_Ch: 14:7 对以色列人全会众说，我们所经过、窥探之地是极美之地。 ###EN### And they spoke to the whole assembly of the children of Israel, saying, The land through which we passed to spy out is an exceedingly good land.
Verse_Ch: 14:8 耶和华若喜悦我们，就必领我们进入那地，把那地赐给我们；那地乃是流奶与蜜之地。 ###EN### If Jehovah is pleased with us, then He will bring us into this land and give it to us; a land which flows with milk and honey.
Verse_Ch: 14:9 只是你们不可背叛耶和华，也不要怕那地的民；因为他们是我们的食物。荫庇他们的已经离开他们，有耶和华与我们同在；不要怕他们。 ###EN### Only do not rebel against Jehovah, nor should you fear the people of the land, for they are our bread. Their protection has been removed from them, and Jehovah is with us; do not fear them.
Verse_Ch: 14:10 但全会众说要拿石头打死他们二人。这时，耶和华的荣光在会幕中向以色列众人显现。 ###EN### But the whole assembly said to stone them with stones. Then the glory of Jehovah appeared in the Tent of Meeting to all the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 14:11 耶和华对摩西说，这百姓藐视我，要到几时呢？我在他们中间行了这一切神迹，他们还不信我，要到几时呢？ ###EN### And Jehovah said to Moses, How long will this people despise Me? And how long will they not believe in Me, in spite of all the signs that I have done among them?
Verse_Ch: 14:12 我要用瘟疫击杀他们，使他们不得承受那地；我要使你成为大国，比他们强盛。 ###EN### I will strike them with pestilence and disposses them, and I will make you into a nation greater and mightier than they.
Verse_Ch: 14:13 摩西对耶和华说，这样，埃及人必听见这事；因为你曾用大能，将这百姓从他们中间领上来。 ###EN### But Moses said to Jehovah, Then the Egyptians will hear of it, for by Your might You brought up this people from their midst,
Verse_Ch: 14:14 埃及人必将这事告诉这地的居民；他们已经听见，你耶和华是在这百姓中间；因为耶和华阿，你面对面被人看见，你的云彩停在他们以上；你日间 在云柱中，夜间在火柱中，在他们前面行。 ###EN### And they will tell the inhabitants of this land. They have heard that You, Jehovah, are in the midst of this people; for You, O Jehovah, are seen eye to eye, and Your cloud stands over them, and You go before them in a pillar of cloud by day and in a pillar of fire by night.
Verse_Ch: 14:15 如今你若把这百姓杀了，如杀一人，那些听见你名声的列国必议论说， ###EN### Now if You put this people to death as one man, then the nations that have heard the report about You will speak, saying,
Verse_Ch: 14:16 耶和华因为不能把这百姓领进祂起誓要赐给他们之地，所以在旷野把他们杀了。 ###EN### Because Jehovah was not able to bring this people into the land which He swore to give them, He has therefore slaughtered them in the wilderness.
Verse_Ch: 14:17 现在求主大显能力，照你所说过的话说， ###EN### And now, I pray, let the power of the Lord be great, just as You have spoken, saying,
Verse_Ch: 14:18 耶和华不轻易发怒，并有丰盛的慈爱，赦免罪孽和过犯；但祂绝不以有罪的为无罪，必追讨他的罪孽，自父及子，直到三四代。 ###EN### Jehovah is slow to anger and abundant in lovingkindness, forgiving iniquity and transgression; but He will by no means clear the guilty, visiting the iniquity of the fathers upon the children to the third and the fourth generations.
Verse_Ch: 14:19 求你照你的大慈爱，饶恕这百姓的罪孽，好像你从埃及到如今，常赦免他们一样。 ###EN### Pardon, I pray, the iniquity of this people according to the greatness of Your lovingkindness, just as You have forgiven this people from Egypt even until now.
Verse_Ch: 14:20 耶和华说，我照着你的话饶恕了他们。 ###EN### Then Jehovah said, I have pardoned them according to your word;
Verse_Ch: 14:21 然而我指着我的生存起誓，并指着遍地要充满耶和华的荣耀起誓， ###EN### But as surely as I live, and as all the earth will be filled with the glory of Jehovah,
Verse_Ch: 14:22 这些人虽然看见我的荣耀，和我在埃及与旷野所行的神迹，仍然试探我这十次，不听从我的话， ###EN### None of those men who have seen My glory and My signs, which I did in Egypt and in the wilderness, yet have tried Me these ten times and have not listened to My voice,
Verse_Ch: 14:23 他们断不得看见我起誓要赐给他们祖宗之地；凡藐视我的，一个也不得看见。 ###EN### Shall see the land which I swore to give to their fathers, nor shall any of those who despised Me see it.
Verse_Ch: 14:24 惟独我的仆人迦勒，因他另有一个灵，专一跟从我，我就要把他领进他所去过的那地；他的后裔也必得那地为业。 ###EN### Only My servant Caleb, because he had a different spirit and has fully followed Me, will I bring into the land which he entered; and his descendants shall take possession of it.
Verse_Ch: 14:25 如今亚玛力人和迦南人既住在谷中，明天你们要转回，从通往红海的路往前行，到旷野去。 ###EN### Now since the Amalekites and the Canaanites dwell in the valleys, turn tomorrow, and set out into the wilderness by the way that leads to the Red Sea.
Verse_Ch: 14:26 耶和华对摩西、亚伦说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses and to Aaron, saying,
Verse_Ch: 14:27 这恶会众向我发怨言，我忍耐他们要到几时呢？以色列人向我所发的怨言，我都听见了。 ###EN### How long shall I bear with this evil assembly, which murmurs against Me? I have heard the murmurings of the children of Israel, which they are making against Me.
Verse_Ch: 14:28 你们告诉他们，耶和华宣示说，我指着我的生存起誓，我必要照你们达到我耳中的话待你们。 ###EN### Say to them, As I live, declares Jehovah, just as you have spoken in My ears, so will I do to you.
Verse_Ch: 14:29 你们的尸首必倒在这旷野，并且你们中间凡被数点的，就是按所计算的数目，从二十岁以上，向我发过怨言的， ###EN### Your corpses shall fall in this wilderness, and none of you who were numbered, according to the number you counted from twenty years old and upward, who have murmured against Me,
Verse_Ch: 14:30 必不得进我起誓要赐给你们居住的那地；惟有耶孚尼的儿子迦勒和嫩的儿子约书亚，才能进去。 ###EN### Shall come into the land, in which I swore to settle you, except Caleb the son of Jephunneh and Joshua the son of Nun.
Verse_Ch: 14:31 但你们的孩子，就是你们所说，要被掳掠的，我必把他们领进去，他们必得知你们所弃绝的那地。 ###EN### But your little ones, whom you said would become plunder, I will bring in, and they will know the land which you have rejected.
Verse_Ch: 14:32 至于你们，你们的尸首必倒在这旷野； ###EN### But as for you, your corpses shall fall in this wilderness.
Verse_Ch: 14:33 你们的儿女必在旷野飘流四十年，担当你们淫行的罪，直到你们的尸首在旷野消灭了。 ###EN### And your children shall wander in the wilderness forty years, and they shall suffer for your unfaithfulness until your corpses have been consumed in the wilderness.
Verse_Ch: 14:34 按你们窥探那地的日数共四十日，一年顶一日，你们要担当罪孽四十年，就知道我不喜悦你们了。 ###EN### According to the number of the days which you spied out the land, forty days, a year for every day, you shall bear your iniquities, forty years; and you shall know My displeasure.
Verse_Ch: 14:35 我耶和华说了，我必要这样待这一切聚集攻击我的恶会众；他们必在这旷野消灭，在这里死亡。 ###EN### I, Jehovah, have spoken; surely I will do this to all this evil assembly who are gathered together against Me. In this wilderness they shall be consumed, and there they shall die.
Verse_Ch: 14:36 摩西打发去窥探那地的人回来，报那地的恶信，叫全会众向摩西发怨言， ###EN### And the men whom Moses sent to spy out the land, who returned and made the whole assembly to murmur against him by bringing up an evil report against the land,
Verse_Ch: 14:37 这些报那地恶信的人都遭瘟疫，死在耶和华面前。 ###EN### That is, those men who brought up an evil report of the land, died by the plague before Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 14:38 去窥探那地的人中，惟有嫩的儿子约书亚和耶孚尼的儿子迦勒，仍然存活。 ###EN### Only Joshua the son of Nun and Caleb the son of Jephunneh remained alive out of those men who went to spy out the land.
Verse_Ch: 14:39 摩西将这些话告诉以色列众人，百姓就甚悲哀。 ###EN### And when Moses spoke these words to all the children of Israel, the people mourned greatly.
Verse_Ch: 14:40 他们清早起来，上山顶去，说，我们在这里；我们有罪了，现在我们情愿上耶和华所说的地方去。 ###EN### And they rose up early in the morning to go up to the top of the mountain, saying, Here we are; now we will go up to the place which Jehovah has spoken of, for we have sinned.
Verse_Ch: 14:41 摩西说，你们为何违背耶和华的命令？这事必不成功。 ###EN### But Moses said, Why now do you continue to transgress the commandment of Jehovah? This will not succeed.
Verse_Ch: 14:42 你们不要上去，免得你们在仇敌面前被击杀，因为耶和华不在你们中间。 ###EN### Do not go up-for Jehovah is not among you-so that you are not struck down before your enemies.
Verse_Ch: 14:43 亚玛力人和迦南人都在那里，在你们面前，你们必倒在刀下；因为你们退回不跟从耶和华，所以耶和华必不与你们同在。 ###EN### For the Amalekites and the Canaanites are there before you, and you shall fall by the sword. Because you have turned back from following Jehovah, therefore Jehovah will not be with you.
Verse_Ch: 14:44 他们却擅自上山顶去，然而耶和华的约柜和摩西都没有出营。 ###EN### But they presumed to go up to the top of the mountain, even though neither the Ark of the Covenant of Jehovah nor Moses had departed out of the midst of the camp.
Verse_Ch: 14:45 那时住在那山地的亚玛力人和迦南人，都下来击打他们，把他们击退了，直到何珥玛。 ###EN### Then the Amalekites and the Canaanites who dwelt in that hill country came down and struck them and beat them back as far as Hormah.
Chapter_Header: 15
Verse_Ch: 15:1 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 15:2 你要对以色列人说，你们进了我所赐给你们居住的地， ###EN### Speak to the children of Israel and say to them, When you come into the land that you are to inhabit, which I am giving you,
Verse_Ch: 15:3 若从牛群羊群中取牛羊作火祭，献给耶和华，无论是燔祭或是别的祭，为要许特别的愿，或是作甘心祭，或是在所定节期献的，都要奉给耶和华为怡 爽的香气； ###EN### And you make an offering by fire to Jehovah, a burnt offering or a sacrifice, to make a special vow or as a freewill offering or at your appointed feasts, to make a satisfying fragrance to Jehovah, from the herd or from the flock,
Verse_Ch: 15:4 那献供物的，就要将细面一伊法的十分之一，并油一欣的四分之一，调和作素祭，献给耶和华。 ###EN### The one who presents his offering shall present to Jehovah a meal offering of a tenth of an ephah of fine flour mingled with a fourth of a hin of oil.
Verse_Ch: 15:5 无论是燔祭或是别的祭，你要为每只绵羊羔，一同预备奠祭的酒一欣的四分之一。 ###EN### And you shall prepare wine for the drink offering, a fourth of a hin, with the burnt offering or for the sacrifice, for each lamb.
Verse_Ch: 15:6 或是为公绵羊，你要预备细面一伊法的十分之二，并油一欣的三分之一，调和作素祭； ###EN### Or for a ram you shall prepare as a meal offering two-tenths of an ephah of fine flour mingled with a third of a hin of oil;
Verse_Ch: 15:7 又用酒一欣的三分之一作奠祭，献给耶和华为怡爽的香气。 ###EN### And for the drink offering you shall present a third of a hin of wine, a satisfying fragrance to Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 15:8 你预备公牛犊作燔祭，或是作别的祭，为要许特别的愿，或是作平安祭，献给耶和华， ###EN### And when you prepare a herd animal for a burnt offering or for a sacrifice, to make a special vow or for peace offerings to Jehovah,
Verse_Ch: 15:9 就要把细面一伊法的十分之三，并油半欣，调和作素祭，和公牛犊一同献上； ###EN### Then you shall offer with the herd animal a meal offering of three-tenths of an ephah of fine flour mingled with half a hin of oil;
Verse_Ch: 15:10 又用酒半欣作奠祭，献给耶和华为怡爽香气的火祭。 ###EN### And you shall present for the drink offering half a hin of wine, an offering by fire, a satisfying fragrance to Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 15:11 献公牛、公绵羊、公绵羊羔、或山羊羔，每只都要这样办理。 ###EN### Thus shall it be done for each ox or for each ram or for each of the male lambs or goats.
Verse_Ch: 15:12 照你们所预备的数目，按着只数，每只都要这样办理。 ###EN### According to the number that you prepare, so you shall do for every one according to their number.
Verse_Ch: 15:13 凡本地人将怡爽香气的火祭献给耶和华，都要这样办理。 ###EN### All who are native shall do these things in this way, in presenting an offering by fire, a satisfying fragrance to Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 15:14 在你们那里寄居的外人，或世世代代在你们中间的人，若愿意将怡爽香气的火祭献给耶和华，你们怎样办理，他也要照样办理。 ###EN### And if a stranger sojourns with you, or one who may be among you throughout your generations, and he wants to make an offering by fire, a satisfying fragrance to Jehovah; just as you do, so he shall do.
Verse_Ch: 15:15 至于会众，你们和寄居的外人都归一例，作为你们世世代代永远的定例；在耶和华面前，你们怎样，寄居的也要怎样。 ###EN### For the congregation there shall be one statute for you and for the stranger who sojourns with you, a perpetual statute throughout your generations; as you are, so shall the sojourner be before Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 15:16 你们和在你们那里寄居的外人，当有一样的条例，一样的典章。 ###EN### One law and one ordinance shall be for you and for the stranger who sojourns with you.
Verse_Ch: 15:17 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 15:18 你要对以色列人说，你们到了我所领你们进去的那地， ###EN### Speak to the children of Israel and say to them, When you come into the land into which I am bringing you,
Verse_Ch: 15:19 吃那地粮食的时候，要把举祭献给耶和华。 ###EN### Whenever you eat of the bread of the land, you shall offer up a heave offering to Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 15:20 你们要用初熟的麦子磨面作饼，当举祭献上；你们举上，好像举禾场的举祭一样。 ###EN### From the first of your dough you shall offer up a cake for a heave offering; as the heave offering of the threshing floor, so shall you offer it up.
Verse_Ch: 15:21 你们世世代代要用初熟的麦子磨面，作为举祭献给耶和华。 ###EN### From the first of your dough you shall give to Jehovah a heave offering throughout your generations.
Verse_Ch: 15:22 你们若是无意中犯了罪，没有遵行耶和华所告诉摩西的这一切命令， ###EN### And if you sin unintentionally and do not observe all these commandments which Jehovah has spoken to Moses,
Verse_Ch: 15:23 就是耶和华藉摩西所吩咐你们的一切事，从耶和华吩咐的那日起，直到你们的世世代代， ###EN### That is, everything that Jehovah has commanded you through Moses, from the day that Jehovah gave commandment and onward throughout your generations,
Verse_Ch: 15:24 若是无意中所犯，是会众没有觉察到的，后来全会众就要将一只公牛犊作燔祭，并照典章把素祭和奠祭，一同献给耶和华为怡爽的香气，又献一只 公山羊作赎罪祭。 ###EN### Then, if it was done unintentionally, without the knowledge of the assembly, the whole assembly shall offer one bull of the herd for a burnt offering, for a satisfying fragrance to Jehovah, with its meal offering and its drink offering, according to the ordinance, and one male goat for a sin offering.
Verse_Ch: 15:25 祭司要为以色列人全会众遮罪，他们就必蒙赦免；因为这是无意的，而且他们为自己的过错，已经把供物，就是向耶和华献的火祭，和赎罪祭，奉 到耶和华面前。 ###EN### And the priest shall make expiation for the whole assembly of the children of Israel, and they shall be forgiven; for it was unintentional, and they have brought their offering, an offering by fire to Jehovah, and their sin offering before Jehovah for their error.
Verse_Ch: 15:26 以色列人全会众，和寄居在他们中间的外人，就必蒙赦免，因为就众百姓说，这罪是无意中涉及的。 ###EN### And the whole assembly of the children of Israel shall be forgiven, and the stranger who sojourns among them; for all the people were involved unintentionally.
Verse_Ch: 15:27 若有一个人无意中犯了罪，他就要献一只一岁的母山羊作赎罪祭。 ###EN### And if one person sins unintentionally, then he shall present a female goat a year old for a sin offering.
Verse_Ch: 15:28 那无意中犯罪的人，既是无意中犯的，祭司就要在耶和华面前为他遮罪，他就必蒙赦免。 ###EN### And the priest shall make expiation before Jehovah for the person who sinned unintentionally, when he sins unintentionally, to make expiation for him; and he shall be forgiven.
Verse_Ch: 15:29 以色列人中的本地人和寄居在他们中间的外人，若是无意中行了什么事，必归一样的条例， ###EN### You shall have one law for the one who does anything unintentionally, for one who is a native among the children of Israel and for the stranger who sojourns among them.
Verse_Ch: 15:30 但那胆大妄为的，无论是本地人或是寄居的，他亵渎了耶和华，必从民中剪除。 ###EN### But the person who does anything with a high hand, whether a native or a sojourner, that one reviles Jehovah; and that person shall be cut off from among his people.
Verse_Ch: 15:31 因他藐视耶和华的言语，干犯耶和华的命令，那人总要剪除；他的罪孽要归到他身上。 ###EN### Because he has despised the word of Jehovah and has broken His commandment, that person shall be completely cut off; his iniquity shall be upon him.
Verse_Ch: 15:32 以色列人在旷野的时候，有人遇见一个人在安息日捡柴。 ###EN### Now while the children of Israel were in the wilderness, they found a man gathering sticks on the Sabbath day.
Verse_Ch: 15:33 遇见他捡柴的人，就把他带到摩西、亚伦、并全会众那里。 ###EN### And those who found him gathering sticks brought him to Moses and Aaron and to the whole assembly.
Verse_Ch: 15:34 他们将他拘禁起来，因为当怎样办他，还没有指明。 ###EN### And they put him in custody, because it had not been declared what should be done to him.
Verse_Ch: 15:35 耶和华对摩西说，那人必要被处死；全会众要在营外用石头把他打死。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to Moses, The man shall surely be put to death; the whole assembly shall stone him with stones outside the camp.
Verse_Ch: 15:36 于是全会众将他带到营外，用石头打死他，是照耶和华所吩咐摩西的。 ###EN### So the whole assembly brought him outside the camp and stoned him to death with stones, just as Jehovah had commanded Moses.
Verse_Ch: 15:37 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 15:38 你要告诉以色列人，叫他们世世代代在衣服边上作繸子，又在衣边的繸子上钉一根蓝细带子。 ###EN### Speak to the children of Israel and tell them to make for themselves fringes on the borders of their garments throughout their generations and to put on the fringe of each border a cord of blue.
Verse_Ch: 15:39 这繸子是要叫你们一看见，就记念并遵行耶和华一切的命令，不随从自己的心意、眼目行邪淫，像你们素常一样； ###EN### And it shall be a fringe for you, so that when you see it you will remember all the commandments of Jehovah and do them; so that you do not seek after your own heart and your own eyes, according to which you committed fornication.
Verse_Ch: 15:40 使你们记念并遵行我一切的命令，成为圣别，归与你们的神。 ###EN### And that you shall remember and do all My commandments and be holy to your God.
Verse_Ch: 15:41 我是耶和华你们的神，曾把你们从埃及地领出来，要作你们的神；我是耶和华你们的神。 ###EN### I am Jehovah your God who brought you out of the land of Egypt to be your God; I am Jehovah your God.
Chapter_Header: 16
Verse_Ch: 16:1 利未的曾孙，哥辖的孙子，以斯哈的儿子可拉，和流便子孙中以利押的儿子大坍、亚比兰，与比勒的儿子安，带着人来； ###EN### Now Korah the son of Izhar, the son of Kohath, the son of Levi, with Dathan and Abiram the sons of Eliab, and On the son of Peleth, the sons of Reuben, took men
Verse_Ch: 16:2 他们同以色列人会众中的二百五十个首领，就是有名望被选召到会中的人，在摩西面前起来， ###EN### And rose up before Moses, with certain of the children of Israel, two hundred fifty leaders of the assembly, who were summoned to the meeting, well-known men.
Verse_Ch: 16:3 聚集攻击摩西、亚伦，说，你们太过分了；全会众个个既是圣别的，耶和华也在他们中间，你们为什么高抬自己，超过耶和华的会众呢？ ###EN### And they assembled themselves together against Moses and against Aaron, and said to them, You take too much upon yourselves, for all the assembly are holy, every one of them, and Jehovah is among them. Why then do you exalt yourselves above the congregation of Jehovah?
Verse_Ch: 16:4 摩西听见了，就面伏于地。 ###EN### And when Moses heard this, he fell on his face.
Verse_Ch: 16:5 他对可拉和可拉一党的人说，到了早晨，耶和华必指示谁是属祂的，谁是圣别的，就叫谁亲近祂；祂所拣选的是谁，必叫谁亲近祂。 ###EN### And he spoke to Korah and to all his company, saying, In the morning Jehovah will make known who is His and who is holy, and will bring him near to Himself; even the one whom He will choose He will bring near to Himself.
Verse_Ch: 16:6 你们要这样行：可拉和你一党的人，你们要拿香炉来， ###EN### Do this: Take censers for yourselves, Korah and all your company,
Verse_Ch: 16:7 明日，在耶和华面前，把火盛在炉中，把香放在上面；耶和华拣选谁，谁就是圣别的。利未的子孙哪，是你们太过分了！ ###EN### And put fire in them, and put incense on them before Jehovah tomorrow; and the man whom Jehovah chooses, he shall be holy. It is you who take too much upon yourselves, O sons of Levi!
Verse_Ch: 16:8 摩西又对可拉说，利未的子孙哪，你们听我说， ###EN### And Moses said to Korah, Hear now, O sons of Levi:
Verse_Ch: 16:9 以色列的神从以色列会中将你们分别出来，使你们亲近祂，办耶和华帐幕的事，并站在会众面前供职服事他们； ###EN### Is it a small thing for you that the God of Israel has separated you from the assembly of Israel to bring you near to Himself to do the service of the tabernacle of Jehovah and to stand before the assembly to minister to them?
Verse_Ch: 16:10 耶和华又使你和你一切弟兄利未的子孙一同亲近祂，这岂为小事？你们还要求祭司的职任么？ ###EN### Or that He has brought you near, and all your brothers the sons of Levi with you? And do you seek the priesthood also?
Verse_Ch: 16:11 所以你和你一党的人聚集，是要攻击耶和华；亚伦算什么，你们竟向他发怨言？ ###EN### Therefore you and all your company are gathered together against Jehovah; but Aaron, what is he that you murmur against him?
Verse_Ch: 16:12 摩西打发人去召以利押的儿子大坍、亚比兰；但他们说，我们不上去！ ###EN### Then Moses sent word to call Dathan and Abiram the sons of Eliab; but they said, We will not come up!
Verse_Ch: 16:13 你将我们从流奶与蜜之地领上来，要叫我们死在旷野，这岂为小事？你还要自立为王辖管我们么？ ###EN### Is it not enough that you have brought us up out of a land flowing with milk and honey to have us die in the wilderness, but must you also exercise leadership over us?
Verse_Ch: 16:14 你实在并没有将我们领进流奶与蜜之地，也没有把田地和葡萄园给我们为业。难道你要剜这些人的眼睛么？我们不上去！ ###EN### Indeed, you have not brought us into a land flowing with milk and honey, nor have you given us an inheritance of fields and vineyards. Will you put out the eyes of these men? We will not come up!
Verse_Ch: 16:15 摩西就甚发怒，对耶和华说，求你不要垂顾他们的供物。我并没有夺过他们一匹驴，也没有害过他们一个人。 ###EN### Then Moses became very angry and said to Jehovah, Do not regard their offering. I have not taken a single donkey from them, nor have I done harm to any of them.
Verse_Ch: 16:16 摩西对可拉说，明天，你和你一党的人，并亚伦，都要站在耶和华面前； ###EN### And Moses said to Korah, You and all your company be present before Jehovah, both you and they along with Aaron, tomorrow.
Verse_Ch: 16:17 各人要拿自己的香炉，把香放在上面，各人把香炉，共二百五十个，拿到耶和华面前；你和亚伦也各拿自己的香炉。 ###EN### And let each of you take his censer and put incense on them, and each of you present his censer before Jehovah, two hundred fifty censers; you also and Aaron shall each present his censer.
Verse_Ch: 16:18 于是他们各人拿自己的香炉，盛上火，加上香，同摩西、亚伦站在会幕门前。 ###EN### So each took his censer and put fire on them and laid incense on them, and they stood at the entrance of the Tent of Meeting with Moses and Aaron.
Verse_Ch: 16:19 可拉招聚全会众到会幕门前，要攻击摩西、亚伦；耶和华的荣光就向全会众显现。 ###EN### Thus Korah gathered the whole assembly against them at the entrance of the Tent of Meeting, and the glory of Jehovah appeared to the whole assembly.
Verse_Ch: 16:20 耶和华对摩西、亚伦说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses and to Aaron, saying,
Verse_Ch: 16:21 你们与这会众分开，我好在片刻之间把他们灭绝。 ###EN### Separate yourselves from among this assembly, so that I may consume them in a moment.
Verse_Ch: 16:22 摩西、亚伦却面伏于地，说，神阿，万人之灵的神阿，一人犯罪，你就要向全会众发怒么？ ###EN### But they fell on their faces and said, O God, the God of the spirits of all flesh, will one man sin and You be angry with the whole assembly?
Verse_Ch: 16:23 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 16:24 你要对会众说，你们离开可拉、大坍、亚比兰住处的四围。 ###EN### Speak to the assembly, saying, Get away from around the dwellings of Korah, Dathan, and Abiram.
Verse_Ch: 16:25 摩西起来，往大坍、亚比兰那里去；以色列的众长老也随着他去。 ###EN### Then Moses rose up and went to Dathan and Abiram, and the elders of Israel followed him.
Verse_Ch: 16:26 他对会众说，你们离开这些恶人的帐棚罢，凡属他们的，什么都不可触摸，恐怕你们与他们一切的罪同被除灭。 ###EN### And he spoke to the assembly, saying, Depart now from the tents of these wicked men, and touch nothing which belongs to them, or you will be swept away with all their sins.
Verse_Ch: 16:27 于是众人离开可拉、大坍、亚比兰住处的四围；大坍、亚比兰带着妻子、儿女、小孩子，都出来，站在自己的帐棚门口。 ###EN### So they got away from around the dwellings of Korah, Dathan, and Abiram, and Dathan and Abiram came out, and stood at the entrance of their tents, with their wives and their children and their little ones.
Verse_Ch: 16:28 摩西说，你们要凭这证据知道，这一切事是耶和华差遣我行的，并不是出于我自己的心意。 ###EN### And Moses said, By this you shall know that Jehovah has sent me to do all these works, for it is not of myself.
Verse_Ch: 16:29 这些人死若是与众人无异，或是他们所遭的与众人相同，就不是耶和华差遣我来的。 ###EN### If these people die as all human beings die, or if what befalls all human beings befalls them, then Jehovah has not sent me.
Verse_Ch: 16:30 倘若耶和华创作一件新事，使地开口，把他们和一切属他们的都吞下去，叫他们活活的坠落阴间，你们就明白这些人是藐视耶和华了。 ###EN### But if Jehovah brings about a new thing, and the ground opens its mouth and swallows them up with all that belongs to them, and they descend alive into Sheol, then you will understand that these men have despised Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 16:31 摩西刚说完了这一切话，他们脚下的地就裂开； ###EN### And as soon as he finished speaking all these words, the ground that was under them was split open.
Verse_Ch: 16:32 地开了口，把他们和他们的家眷，并一切属可拉的人和财物，都吞下去。 ###EN### So the earth opened its mouth and swallowed them up, along with their households and everyone who belonged to Korah and all their possessions.
Verse_Ch: 16:33 这样，他们和一切属他们的，都活活的坠落阴间；地在他们上面合闭，他们就从会众中灭亡。 ###EN### So they and all that belonged to them descended alive into Sheol; and the earth closed over them, and they perished from the midst of the congregation.
Verse_Ch: 16:34 在他们四围的以色列众人听他们呼号，就都逃跑，说，恐怕地也把我们吞下去。 ###EN### And all Israel who were around them fled at their outcry, for they said, The earth may swallow us up too!
Verse_Ch: 16:35 又有火从耶和华那里出来，烧灭了那献香的二百五十个人。 ###EN### And fire came forth from Jehovah and consumed the two hundred fifty men who presented the incense.
Verse_Ch: 16:36 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 16:37 你告诉祭司亚伦的儿子以利亚撒，从火烬中捡起那些香炉来，把火撒在别处，因为那些香炉是圣的。 ###EN### Tell Eleazar the son of Aaron the priest to take the censers up out of the burning and scatter the fire about; for they are holy.
Verse_Ch: 16:38 那些犯罪、自害己命之人的香炉，要锤成片，用以包坛；那些香炉本是他们在耶和华面前献过的，是成为圣的，可以给以色列人作警戒。 ###EN### The censers of those who have sinned against their own lives, let them be made into beaten plates for a covering of the altar, for they presented them before Jehovah and they became holy. So they shall be a sign to the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 16:39 于是祭司以利亚撒将被烧之人所献的铜香炉拿来；人就锤出来，用以包坛， ###EN### And Eleazar the priest took the bronze censers which those who were burned had offered; and they beat them out as a covering of the altar,
Verse_Ch: 16:40 给以色列人作记念，好叫那不是亚伦后裔的外人，不得近前来在耶和华面前烧香，免得他遭遇可拉和他一党所遭遇的；这乃是照耶和华借着摩西对 以利亚撒所说的。 ###EN### As a reminder to the children of Israel that no stranger who is not of the seed of Aaron may come near to burn incense before Jehovah, so that he does not become like Korah and his company, just as Jehovah had spoken to him through Moses.
Verse_Ch: 16:41 第二天，以色列人全会众都向摩西、亚伦发怨言说，你们害死耶和华的百姓了。 ###EN### But on the next day the whole assembly of the children of Israel murmured against Moses and against Aaron, saying, You have caused the people of Jehovah to die.
Verse_Ch: 16:42 会众聚集攻击摩西、亚伦的时候，他们向会幕观看，不料，有云彩遮盖会幕，耶和华的荣光显现出来。 ###EN### But when the assembly gathered against Moses and against Aaron, they looked toward the Tent of Meeting, and there the cloud was, covering it; and the glory of Jehovah appeared.
Verse_Ch: 16:43 摩西、亚伦就来到会幕前。 ###EN### And Moses and Aaron came to the front of the Tent of Meeting.
Verse_Ch: 16:44 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 16:45 你们从这会众中间离开，我好在片刻之间把他们灭绝。他们二人就面伏于地。 ###EN### Get away from the midst of this assembly that I might consume them in a moment. And they fell upon their faces.
Verse_Ch: 16:46 摩西对亚伦说，拿你的香炉，把坛上的火盛在其中，又加上香，快快带到会众那里，为他们遮罪；因为有忿怒从耶和华面前出来，瘟疫已经发作了。 ###EN### And Moses said to Aaron, Take the censer and put fire on it from the altar, and lay incense on it, and carry it quickly to the assembly, and make expiation for them. For wrath has gone forth from Jehovah; the plague has begun.
Verse_Ch: 16:47 亚伦照着摩西所说的拿来，奔到会众中间；看哪，瘟疫在百姓中已经发作了。他就加上香，为百姓遮罪。 ###EN### And Aaron took it as Moses had said and ran into the midst of the assembly. And indeed the plague had begun among the people. So he put on the incense and made expiation for the people.
Verse_Ch: 16:48 他站在死人与活人中间，瘟疫就止住了。 ###EN### And he stood between the dead and the living, and the plague was stopped.
Verse_Ch: 16:49 除了因可拉事情死的以外，遭瘟疫死的，有一万四千七百人。 ###EN### Now those who died by the plague were fourteen thousand seven hundred, besides those who died on account of Korah.
Verse_Ch: 16:50 亚伦回到会幕门口，到摩西那里，瘟疫已经止住了。 ###EN### So Aaron returned to Moses at the entrance of the Tent of Meeting when the plague had been stopped.
Chapter_Header: 17
Verse_Ch: 17:1 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 17:2 你要告诉以色列人，从他们取杖，每宗族一根；从他们所有的首领，按着宗族，共取十二根；你要将各人的名字写在各人的杖上， ###EN### Speak to the children of Israel, and take from them rods, one for each father's house, twelve rods from all their leaders according to their fathers' houses; you shall write everyone's name upon his rod.
Verse_Ch: 17:3 并要将亚伦的名字写在利未的杖上，因为各宗族的族长必有一根杖。 ###EN### And you shall write Aaron's name upon the rod of Levi, for there shall be one rod for the head of each of their fathers' houses.
Verse_Ch: 17:4 你要把这些杖放在会幕内见证柜前，我与你们相会之处。 ###EN### And you shall place them in the Tent of Meeting before the testimony, where I meet with you.
Verse_Ch: 17:5 我拣选的那人，他的杖必发芽；这样，我必使以色列人向你们所发、对我的怨言止息。 ###EN### And the rod of the man whom I choose shall bud, and I will put a stop to the murmurings of the children of Israel against Me, which they murmur against you.
Verse_Ch: 17:6 于是摩西告诉以色列人。他们的首领就把杖交给他，按着宗族，每首领一根，共有十二根；亚伦的杖也在其中。 ###EN### So Moses spoke to the children of Israel. And every one of their leaders gave him a rod, one rod for each leader according to their fathers' houses, twelve rods, with the rod of Aaron among their rods.
Verse_Ch: 17:7 摩西就把杖放在见证的会幕内，在耶和华面前。 ###EN### And Moses placed the rods before Jehovah in the Tent of the Testimony.
Verse_Ch: 17:8 第二天，摩西进见证的会幕去；看哪，利未家亚伦的杖已经发了芽，甚至生了花苞，开了花，结了熟杏。 ###EN### And on the next day Moses went into the Tent of the Testimony, and there was the rod of Aaron for the house of Levi: it had budded; it even put forth buds and produced blossoms and bore ripe almonds.
Verse_Ch: 17:9 摩西就把所有的杖从耶和华面前拿出来，给以色列众人看；他们看见了，各首领就把自己的杖拿去。 ###EN### And Moses brought out all the rods from before Jehovah to all the children of Israel, and they looked; and each one took his rod.
Verse_Ch: 17:10 耶和华对摩西说，把亚伦的杖放回见证柜前，给这些背叛之子留作记号；这样，你就使他们向我发的怨言止息，免得他们死亡。 ###EN### Then Jehovah said to Moses, Put back the rod of Aaron before the testimony to be kept as a sign against the rebels, so that you may put an end to their murmurings against Me, and they not die.
Verse_Ch: 17:11 摩西就这样行；耶和华怎样吩咐他，他就怎样行。 ###EN### And Moses did so; just as Jehovah commanded him, so he did.
Verse_Ch: 17:12 以色列人对摩西说，我们死啦，我们灭亡啦，我们都灭亡啦！ ###EN### And the children of Israel spoke to Moses, saying, Alas, we die out; we perish; all of us perish.
Verse_Ch: 17:13 凡挨近耶和华帐幕的是必死的。难道我们都要死么？ ###EN### Everyone who comes near, who comes near to the tabernacle of Jehovah, dies. Are we to completely die out?
Chapter_Header: 18
Verse_Ch: 18:1 耶和华对亚伦说，你和你的儿子，并你宗族的人，要一同担当干犯圣所的罪孽；你和你的儿子，也要一同担当干犯祭司职任的罪孽。 ###EN### Then Jehovah said to Aaron, You and your sons and your father's household with you shall bear the iniquity of the sanctuary; and you and your sons with you shall bear the iniquity of your priesthood.
Verse_Ch: 18:2 你要带你弟兄利未支派，就是你祖宗支派的人前来，使他们与你联合，服事你；只是你和你的儿子，要一同在见证的会幕前供职。 ###EN### And your brothers also, the tribe of Levi, the tribe of your father, bring near with you, so that they may be joined to you and minister to you, while you and your sons with you are before the Tent of the Testimony.
Verse_Ch: 18:3 他们要守所吩咐你的，并看守全帐幕，只是不可挨近圣所的物件和坛，免得他们和你们都死亡。 ###EN### And they shall keep your charge and the charge of all the tent, but they shall not come near to the furnishings of the sanctuary and to the altar, so that they do not die, neither they nor you.
Verse_Ch: 18:4 他们要与你联合，也要看守会幕，办理帐幕一切的事，只是外人不可挨近你们。 ###EN### And they shall be joined to you and keep the charge of the Tent of Meeting for all the service of the tent, but a stranger shall not come near to you.
Verse_Ch: 18:5 你们要看守圣所和坛，免得忿怒再临到以色列人。 ###EN### And you shall keep the charge of the sanctuary and the charge of the altar, so that there may be no more wrath upon the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 18:6 我已将你们的弟兄利未人从以色列人中选取出来，当作礼物给你们，归与耶和华，为要办理会幕的事。 ###EN### And I Myself have taken your brothers the Levites from among the children of Israel. They are a gift to you, given to Jehovah, to do the service of the Tent of Meeting.
Verse_Ch: 18:7 你和你的儿子们要为一切属坛和幔内的事，一同守祭司的职任；你们要这样供职。我将祭司的职任当作礼物给你们，使你们事奉我。凡挨近的外人要 被处死。 ###EN### But you and your sons with you shall attend to your priesthood for everything concerning the altar and within the veil, and you shall carry out your service. I give you the priesthood as a service of gift, but the unauthorized person who comes near shall be put to death.
Verse_Ch: 18:8 耶和华对亚伦说，我已将我的举祭，就是以色列人一切分别为圣的物，交给你经管；因你受过膏，我把这些都赐给了你和你的子孙；这要作永远的定 例。 ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Aaron, And I Myself have given you charge of My heave offerings, even all the holy things of the children of Israel; I have given them to you because of the anointing, and to your sons, as a perpetual statute.
Verse_Ch: 18:9 至圣之物中不经过火的，都是你的；以色列人给我的一切供物，就是一切的素祭、赎罪祭、赎愆祭，都是至圣的，要归给你和你的子孙。 ###EN### This shall be yours of the most holy things, kept from the fire. Every offering of theirs, even every meal offering of theirs and every sin offering of theirs and every trespass offering of theirs, which they shall render to Me, shall be most holy for you and for your sons.
Verse_Ch: 18:10 你要拿这些当至圣物吃；凡男丁都可以吃；你当以此物为圣。 ###EN### As the most holy things you shall eat it; every male shall eat it; it shall be holy to you.
Verse_Ch: 18:11 以色列人礼物中的举祭，并一切的摇祭，也都是你的，我已赐给你和你的儿女；这要作永远的定例；凡在你家中洁净的人都可以吃。 ###EN### This also is yours, the heave offering of their gift, even all the wave offerings of the children of Israel. I have given them to you and to your sons and to your daughters with you, as a perpetual statute; everyone who is clean in your house may eat it.
Verse_Ch: 18:12 凡油中至好的，凡新酒和五谷中至好的，就是以色列人所献给耶和华的初熟之物，我都赐给你。 ###EN### All the best of the oil, and all the best of new wine and of the grain, their firstfruits that they give to Jehovah, I have given to you.
Verse_Ch: 18:13 凡从他们地上所带来给耶和华的初熟之物，也都要归与你；凡在你家中洁净的人都可以吃。 ###EN### The firstfruits of all that is in their land, which they bring to Jehovah, shall be yours; everyone who is clean in your house may eat it.
Verse_Ch: 18:14 以色列中一切永献的都必归与你。 ###EN### Everything devoted in Israel shall be yours.
Verse_Ch: 18:15 他们所奉给耶和华的，连人带牲畜，一切血肉所生，凡头胎的，都要归给你；只是人中头生的，总要赎出来；不洁净牲畜头生的，也要赎出来。 ###EN### Everything that opens the womb of all flesh, which they present to Jehovah, whether human or animal, shall be yours; nevertheless the firstborn of human beings you shall surely redeem, and the firstborn of unclean animals you shall redeem.
Verse_Ch: 18:16 其中从一个月以上所当赎的，要照你所估定的价，按圣所的舍客勒，(一舍客勒是二十季拉，)用银子五舍客勒赎出来。 ###EN### And those who are to be redeemed from a month old you shall redeem, according to your estimation, for five shekels of silver, according to the shekel of the sanctuary, which is twenty gerahs.
Verse_Ch: 18:17 只是头生的牛、头生的绵羊、或头生的山羊，必不可赎；它们都是圣的。你要把它们的血洒在坛上，把它们的脂油焚烧，当作怡爽香气的火祭献给 耶和华。 ###EN### But the firstborn of a cow or the firstborn of a sheep or the firstborn of a goat you shall not redeem; they are holy. You shall sprinkle their blood upon the altar and burn their fat as an offering by fire for a satisfying fragrance to Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 18:18 它们的肉必归与你，像摇祭的胸、举祭的右腿归与你一样。 ###EN### But their flesh shall be yours; like the breast of the wave offering and like the right thigh, it shall be yours.
Verse_Ch: 18:19 凡以色列人所献给耶和华圣物中的举祭，我都赐给你和你的儿女；这要作永远的定例。这是给你和你的后裔，在耶和华面前作为永远的盐约。 ###EN### All the heave offerings of the holy things, which the children of Israel offer to Jehovah, I have given to you and to your sons and your daughters with you, as a perpetual statute. It is a covenant of salt forever before Jehovah for you and for your descendants with you.
Verse_Ch: 18:20 耶和华对亚伦说，你在以色列人的地上不可有产业，在他们中间也不可有分；在他们中间，我就是你的分，是你的产业。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to Aaron, You shall have no inheritance in their land, nor shall you have any portion among them; I am your portion and your inheritance among the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 18:21 凡以色列中出产的十分之一，我已赐给利未的子孙为业，为他们所办理的事，就是会幕的事，酬报他们。 ###EN### And to the children of Levi I have now given every tithe in Israel for an inheritance in return for their service which they carry out, the service of the Tent of Meeting.
Verse_Ch: 18:22 从今以后，以色列人不可挨近会幕，免得他们担罪而死。 ###EN### From now on the children of Israel shall not come near the Tent of Meeting, so that they do not incur sin and die.
Verse_Ch: 18:23 惟独利未人要办理会幕的事，担当罪孽；这要作你们世世代代永远的定例。他们在以色列人中不可有产业； ###EN### But the Levites shall do the service of the Tent of Meeting, and they shall bear their iniquity; it shall be a perpetual statute throughout your generations. And among the children of Israel they shall have no inheritance.
Verse_Ch: 18:24 因为以色列人中出产的十分之一，就是献给耶和华为举祭的，我已赐给利未人为业；所以我对他们说，在以色列人中他们不可有产业。 ###EN### For the tithe of the children of Israel, which they offer as a heave offering to Jehovah, I have given to the Levites for an inheritance; therefore I have said to them, Among the children of Israel they shall have no inheritance.
Verse_Ch: 18:25 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 18:26 你要对利未人说，当你们从以色列人取十分之一，就是我从他们所取来给你们为业的，你们就要从那十分之一中，再取十分之一作为举祭献给耶和 华。 ###EN### Moreover you shall speak to the Levites and say to them, When you take from the children of Israel the tithe which I have given you from them as your inheritance, then you shall offer up a heave offering from it for Jehovah, a tithe of the tithe.
Verse_Ch: 18:27 这举祭要算为你们禾场上的谷，又如满酒醡的酒。 ###EN### And your heave offering shall be reckoned to you as though it were the grain of the threshing floor and the fullness of the wine press.
Verse_Ch: 18:28 这样，你们从以色列人所得的十分之一，其中也要取一分作举祭献给耶和华；从这十分之一中，你们要将所献给耶和华的举祭归给祭司亚伦。 ###EN### Thus you shall also offer a heave offering to Jehovah from all your tithes, which you receive from the children of Israel; and from it you shall give Jehovah's heave offering to Aaron the priest.
Verse_Ch: 18:29 所奉给你们的一切礼物，要从其中将至好的，就是分别为圣的部分，献给耶和华为举祭。 ###EN### Out of all your gifts you shall offer every heave offering of Jehovah, from all the best of it, the sanctified portion of it from them.
Verse_Ch: 18:30 所以你要对利未人说，你们从其中将至好的举起，这就算为你们禾场上的出产，又如酒醡的出产。 ###EN### Therefore you shall say to them, When you heave from it the best of it, then it shall be reckoned to the Levites as though it were the produce of the threshing floor and the produce of the wine press.
Verse_Ch: 18:31 你们和你们的家属随处可以吃，因为这是你们的赏赐，作你们在会幕里办事的报酬。 ###EN### And you may eat it in every place, you and your households, for it is your reward in return for your service in the Tent of Meeting.
Verse_Ch: 18:32 你们从其中将至好的举起，就不至因这物担罪。你们不可亵渎以色列人的圣物，免得死亡。 ###EN### And you shall bear no sin by reason of it, when you have heaved from it the best of it. But you shall not profane the holy things of the children of Israel, so that you do not die.
Chapter_Header: 19
Verse_Ch: 19:1 耶和华对摩西、亚伦说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses and to Aaron, saying,
Verse_Ch: 19:2 耶和华所吩咐律法中的律例，乃是这样说，你要告诉以色列人，把一只纯全无残疾，未曾负轭的红母牛牵到你这里来， ###EN### This is the statute of the law which Jehovah has commanded, saying, Tell the children of Israel to bring you a red heifer without defect, in which is no blemish and upon which a yoke has never come.
Verse_Ch: 19:3 交给祭司以利亚撒；他要牵到营外，人就把牛宰在他面前。 ###EN### And you shall give it to Eleazar the priest, and he shall bring it outside the camp, and one shall slaughter it in his presence.
Verse_Ch: 19:4 祭司以利亚撒要用指头蘸些牛血，向会幕前面弹七次。 ###EN### And Eleazar the priest shall take some of its blood with his finger and sprinkle its blood toward the front of the Tent of Meeting seven times.
Verse_Ch: 19:5 人要在他眼前把这母牛焚烧；牛的皮、肉、血、连粪，都要焚烧。 ###EN### And the heifer shall be burned in his sight; its skin and its flesh and its blood, with its dung, shall be burned.
Verse_Ch: 19:6 祭司要把香柏木、牛膝草、朱红色线，都丢在烧牛的火中。 ###EN### And the priest shall take cedar wood and hyssop and scarlet strands, and cast them into the midst of the burning of the heifer.
Verse_Ch: 19:7 祭司要洗衣服，用水洗身，然后可以进营；但他必不洁净到晚上。 ###EN### Then the priest shall wash his clothes and bathe his flesh in water, and afterward he shall come into the camp; but the priest shall be unclean until the evening.
Verse_Ch: 19:8 烧牛的人也要洗衣服，用水洗身，并且不洁净到晚上。 ###EN### And he who burns the heifer shall wash his clothes in water and bathe his body in water, and shall be unclean until the evening.
Verse_Ch: 19:9 要有一个洁净的人收起母牛灰，放在营外洁净的地方，为以色列人会众留着，用以作除污秽的水；这是赎罪祭。 ###EN### And a man who is clean shall gather up the ashes of the heifer and place them outside the camp in a clean place, and it shall be kept for the assembly of the children of Israel as water for impurity; it is a sin offering.
Verse_Ch: 19:10 收起母牛灰的人要洗衣服，并且不洁净到晚上。这要作以色列人和寄居在他们中间的外人永远的定例。 ###EN### And he who gathers the ashes of the heifer shall wash his clothes and be unclean until the evening. And it shall be a perpetual statute to the children of Israel and to the stranger who sojourns among them.
Verse_Ch: 19:11 触着人死尸的，就必不洁净七天。 ###EN### One who touches the dead body of any human being shall be unclean seven days.
Verse_Ch: 19:12 那人要在第三天和第七天用这水洁净自己，就必洁净了；他若在第三天和第七天不洁净自己，就仍不洁净。 ###EN### He shall purify himself with it on the third day and on the seventh day, and then he shall be clean; but if he does not purify himself on the third day and on the seventh day, he shall not be clean.
Verse_Ch: 19:13 凡触着死人，就是触着死人身体，而不洁净自己的，就玷污了耶和华的帐幕，这人必从以色列中剪除；因为那除污秽的水没有洒在他身上，他就为 不洁净，污秽还在他身上。 ###EN### Whoever touches a dead person, the body of a human being who has died, and does not purify himself, defiles the tabernacle of Jehovah; and that person shall be cut off from Israel. Because the water for impurity was not sprinkled upon him, he shall be unclean; his uncleanness is still on him.
Verse_Ch: 19:14 人死在帐棚里的条例乃是这样：凡进那帐棚的，和一切在帐棚里的，都必不洁净七天。 ###EN### This is the law when a man dies in a tent: Anyone who comes into the tent and everyone who is in the tent shall be unclean seven days.
Verse_Ch: 19:15 凡敞口的器皿，就是没有扎上盖的，也是不洁净的。 ###EN### And every open vessel, which has no covering tied down on it, is unclean.
Verse_Ch: 19:16 无论何人在田野里触着被刀杀的，或是尸首，或是人的骨头，或是坟墓，就必不洁净七天。 ###EN### And whoever in the open field touches one who has been slain with a sword or a dead body or a human bone or a grave, shall be unclean seven days.
Verse_Ch: 19:17 要为这不洁净的人拿些赎罪祭烧成的灰，放在器皿里，倒上活水。 ###EN### And for the unclean they shall take of the ashes of the burning of the sin offering, and running water shall be added to them in a vessel;
Verse_Ch: 19:18 要有一个洁净的人，拿牛膝草蘸在这水中，把水洒在帐棚上，和一切物件并帐棚内的众人身上，又洒在触着骨头，或触着被杀的，或触着自死的， 或触着坟墓的那人身上。 ###EN### And a clean person shall take hyssop, and dip it in the water, and sprinkle it on the tent and on all the furnishings and on the persons who were there, or on the one who touched the bone or the one slain or the one who died or the grave.
Verse_Ch: 19:19 第三天和第七天，洁净的人要洒水在不洁净的人身上，第七天就使他成为洁净。那人要洗衣服，用水洗澡，到晚上就洁净了。 ###EN### And the clean person shall sprinkle on the unclean on the third day and on the seventh day, and on the seventh day he shall purify him. And he shall wash his clothes and bathe himself in water and shall be clean in the evening.
Verse_Ch: 19:20 但那污秽而不洁净自己的，这人要从会众中剪除，因为他玷污了耶和华的圣所；除污秽的水没有洒在他身上，他是不洁净的。 ###EN### But the man who shall be unclean and does not purify himself, that person shall be cut off from the midst of the congregation, because he has defiled the sanctuary of Jehovah; the water for impurity has not been sprinkled on him; he is unclean.
Verse_Ch: 19:21 这要作他们永远的定例。那洒除污秽水的人要洗衣服；凡触着除污秽水的，必不洁净到晚上。 ###EN### So it shall be a perpetual statute for them. And he who sprinkles the water for impurity shall wash his clothes, and he who touches the water for impurity shall be unclean until evening.
Verse_Ch: 19:22 不洁净的人所触着的一切物就不洁净；触着这物的人必不洁净到晚上。 ###EN### And whatever the unclean person touches shall be unclean; and the person who touches it shall be unclean until evening.
Chapter_Header: 20
Verse_Ch: 20:1 正月间，以色列人全会众到了寻的旷野，百姓就住在加低斯；米利暗死在那里，就葬在那里。 ###EN### Then the children of Israel, the whole assembly, came to the wilderness of Zin in the first month, and the people stayed at Kadesh; and Miriam died there and was buried there.
Verse_Ch: 20:2 会众没有水喝，就聚集攻击摩西、亚伦。 ###EN### And there was no water for the assembly, and they gathered themselves together against Moses and against Aaron.
Verse_Ch: 20:3 百姓向摩西争闹说，巴不得我们的弟兄死在耶和华面前的时候，我们也死了！ ###EN### And the people contended with Moses and spoke, saying, If only we had expired when our brothers expired before Jehovah!
Verse_Ch: 20:4 你们为何把耶和华的会众领到这旷野，使我们和牲畜都死在这里？ ###EN### Why then have you brought the congregation of Jehovah into this wilderness for us and our livestock to die there?
Verse_Ch: 20:5 你们为何把我们从埃及带上来，领我们到这坏地方？这地方不好撒种，也没有无花果树、葡萄树、石榴树，甚至没有水喝。 ###EN### Why then did you bring us up out of Egypt, to bring us to this wretched place? It is not a place of grain or figs or vines or pomegranates, and there is not even water to drink.
Verse_Ch: 20:6 摩西、亚伦离开会众，到会幕门口，面伏于地；耶和华的荣光向他们显现。 ###EN### And Moses and Aaron went from before the congregation to the entrance of the Tent of Meeting and fell upon their faces, and the glory of Jehovah appeared to them.
Verse_Ch: 20:7 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 20:8 你拿着杖，和你的哥哥亚伦招聚会众，在他们眼前吩咐磐石发出水来；这样，你就为他们使水从磐石中流出来，给会众和他们的牲畜喝。 ###EN### Take the rod, and gather the assembly, you and Aaron your brother, and speak to the rock before their eyes, so that it yields its water. Thus you shall bring forth water for them out of the rock and give the assembly and their livestock a drink.
Verse_Ch: 20:9 于是摩西照耶和华所吩咐的，从耶和华面前取了杖去。 ###EN### And Moses took the rod from before Jehovah, as He had commanded him.
Verse_Ch: 20:10 摩西、亚伦就招聚会众到磐石前；摩西对他们说，你们这些背叛的人听我说，我们要为你们使水从这磐石中流出来么？ ###EN### And Moses and Aaron gathered the congregation together before the rock, and he said to them, Listen now, you rebels: Shall we bring forth water for you out of this rock?
Verse_Ch: 20:11 摩西举手，用杖击打磐石两下，就有许多水流出来，会众和他们的牲畜都喝了。 ###EN### Then Moses lifted up his hand and struck the rock with his rod twice; and abundant water came forth, and the assembly and their livestock drank.
Verse_Ch: 20:12 耶和华对摩西、亚伦说，因为你们不信我，不在以色列人眼前尊我为圣，所以你们必不得领这会众进我所赐给他们的地去。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to Moses and Aaron, Because you did not believe in Me, to sanctify Me in the sight of the children of Israel, therefore you shall not bring this congregation into the land which I have given them.
Verse_Ch: 20:13 这就是米利巴水；以色列人在那里向耶和华争闹，耶和华就在他们中间显为圣。 ###EN### These are the waters of Meribah, where the children of Israel contended with Jehovah, and He was sanctified among them.
Verse_Ch: 20:14 摩西从加低斯差遣使者去见以东王，说，你的弟兄以色列人这样说，你知道我们所遭遇的一切艰难， ###EN### Now Moses sent messengers from Kadesh to the king of Edom: Thus says your brother Israel, You know all the hardship that has befallen us;
Verse_Ch: 20:15 就是我们的列祖如何下到埃及，我们在埃及久住；埃及人如何苦待我们和我们的列祖， ###EN### How our fathers went down to Egypt, and we dwelt in Egypt a long time; and the Egyptians ill-treated us and our fathers;
Verse_Ch: 20:16 我们哀求耶和华的时候，祂听了我们的声音，差遣一位使者把我们从埃及领出来。如今，我们在你边界上的城加低斯。 ###EN### And when we cried to Jehovah, He heard our voice and sent an Angel and brought us forth out of Egypt; and now we are in Kadesh, a city on the edge of your border.
Verse_Ch: 20:17 求你让我们从你的地经过。我们不走田间和葡萄园，也不喝井里的水，只走王道，不偏左右，直到过了你的境界。 ###EN### Please let us pass through your land. We will not pass through field or through vineyard, nor will we drink water from any well; we will go along the King's Highway, not turning aside to the right or to the left, until we pass through your territory.
Verse_Ch: 20:18 以东王说，你不可从我的地经过，不然我要带刀出去攻击你。 ###EN### But Edom said to him, You shall not pass through my territory, or else I will come out against you with the sword.
Verse_Ch: 20:19 以色列人说，我们要走大道上去；我们和牲畜若喝你的水，必给你价值。不求别的，只求你让我们步行过去。 ###EN### Then the children of Israel said to him, We will go up by the highway, and if I and my livestock drink some of your water, then I will pay its price. Allow me only this one thing, to pass through on foot.
Verse_Ch: 20:20 以东王说，你们不可经过；就率领许多人出来，要用强硬的手攻击以色列人。 ###EN### However he said, You shall not pass through. And Edom came out against him with a large number of people and with a mighty hand.
Verse_Ch: 20:21 这样，以东王不肯让以色列人从他的境界过去；于是他们转去，离开他。 ###EN### So Edom refused to give Israel passage through his territory, and Israel turned away from him.
Verse_Ch: 20:22 以色列人全会众从加低斯起行，到了何珥山。 ###EN### Now when they journeyed from Kadesh, the children of Israel, the whole assembly, came to Mount Hor.
Verse_Ch: 20:23 耶和华在以东地边界的何珥山上对摩西、亚伦说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses and to Aaron at Mount Hor, on the border of the land of Edom, saying,
Verse_Ch: 20:24 亚伦要归到他本民那里，他必不得进我所赐给以色列人的地，因为在米利巴水的事上，你们违背了我的话。 ###EN### Aaron shall be gathered to his people, for he shall not enter into the land which I have given to the children of Israel, because you rebelled against My word at the waters of Meribah.
Verse_Ch: 20:25 你带亚伦和他的儿子以利亚撒上何珥山， ###EN### Take Aaron and Eleazar his son, and bring them up Mount Hor;
Verse_Ch: 20:26 把亚伦的圣衣脱下来，给他儿子以利亚撒穿上；亚伦必死在那里，归他本民。 ###EN### And strip Aaron of his garments and put them upon Eleazar his son; so Aaron will be gathered to his people, and will die there.
Verse_Ch: 20:27 摩西就照耶和华所吩咐的行，三人当着全会众的眼前上了何珥山。 ###EN### So Moses did just as Jehovah had commanded, and they went up Mount Hor in the sight of the whole assembly.
Verse_Ch: 20:28 摩西把亚伦的圣衣脱下来，给他的儿子以利亚撒穿上，亚伦就死在山顶那里。于是摩西和以利亚撒下了山。 ###EN### And when Moses had stripped Aaron of his garments and put them on Eleazar his son, Aaron died there on the top of the mountain. Then Moses and Eleazar came down from the mountain.
Verse_Ch: 20:29 全会众见亚伦已经死了，以色列全家便为亚伦哀哭了三十天。 ###EN### And when the whole assembly saw that Aaron had expired, all the house of Israel wept for Aaron thirty days.
Chapter_Header: 21
Verse_Ch: 21:1 住南地的迦南人亚拉得王，听说以色列人从亚他林路来，就和以色列人争战，掳了他们几个人。 ###EN### And when the Canaanite, the king of Arad, who dwelt in the Negev, heard that Israel was coming by the way of Atharim, he fought against Israel and took some of them captive.
Verse_Ch: 21:2 以色列人向耶和华许愿说，你若将这民交付我们手里，我们就要把他们的城邑尽行毁灭。 ###EN### And Israel made a vow to Jehovah and said, If You will indeed deliver this people into my hand, then I will utterly destroy their cities.
Verse_Ch: 21:3 耶和华听了以色列人的呼声，把迦南人交付他们，他们就把迦南人和迦南人的城邑尽行毁灭。那地方的名便叫何珥玛。 ###EN### And Jehovah listened to the voice of Israel and delivered up the Canaanites, and they utterly destroyed them and their cities. Thus the name of the place was called Hormah.
Verse_Ch: 21:4 他们从何珥山起行，沿着通往红海的路走，要绕过以东地。百姓在这路上，心中烦躁， ###EN### Then they journeyed from Mount Hor by the way to the Red Sea, to go around the land of Edom; and the people became impatient on the way.
Verse_Ch: 21:5 就毁谤神和摩西说，你们为什么把我们从埃及领上来，使我们死在旷野？这里没有粮，没有水，我们的心厌恶这淡薄的食物。 ###EN### And the people spoke against God and against Moses, Why have you brought us up out of Egypt to die in the wilderness? For there is no food and there is no water; and our soul loathes this light bread.
Verse_Ch: 21:6 于是耶和华打发火蛇进入百姓中间，蛇就咬他们，以致以色列中死了许多人。 ###EN### Then Jehovah sent fiery serpents among the people, and they bit the people, so that many people of Israel died.
Verse_Ch: 21:7 百姓到摩西那里，说，我们有罪了，因为我们毁谤了耶和华和你；求你向耶和华祷告，叫这些蛇离开我们。于是摩西为百姓祷告。 ###EN### And the people came to Moses and said, We have sinned, because we have spoken against Jehovah and against you; pray to Jehovah, that He may take away the serpents from us. So Moses prayed for the people.
Verse_Ch: 21:8 耶和华对摩西说，你制造一条火蛇，挂在杆上；凡被咬的，一看这蛇，就必得活。 ###EN### Then Jehovah said to Moses, Make a fiery serpent, and set it on a pole; and everyone who is bitten, when he sees it, shall live.
Verse_Ch: 21:9 摩西便制造一条铜蛇，挂在杆上；蛇若咬了什么人，那人一望这铜蛇就活了。 ###EN### And Moses made a bronze serpent and set it on the pole; and if a serpent had bitten any man, when he looked at the bronze serpent, he lived.
Verse_Ch: 21:10 以色列人起行，安营在阿伯。 ###EN### And the children of Israel journeyed and encamped at Oboth.
Verse_Ch: 21:11 又从阿伯起行，安营在以耶亚巴琳，与摩押相对的旷野，向着日出之地。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Oboth and encamped at Iye-abarim in the wilderness which faces Moab toward the sunrise.
Verse_Ch: 21:12 从那里起行，安营在撒烈谷。 ###EN### From there they journeyed and encamped in the valley of Zered.
Verse_Ch: 21:13 从那里起行，安营在亚嫩河的那一边；这亚嫩河是在旷野，从亚摩利的境界流出来的；原来亚嫩河是摩押的边界，在摩押和亚摩利人交界的地方。 ###EN### From there they journeyed and encamped on the other side of the Arnon, which is in the wilderness that comes out of the border of the Amorites; for the Arnon is the border of Moab, between Moab and the Amorites.
Verse_Ch: 21:14 所以耶和华的战记上说，苏法的哇哈伯与亚嫩河的众谷， ###EN### Therefore it is said in the Book of the Wars of Jehovah, Waheb in Suphah, And the valleys of the Arnon,
Verse_Ch: 21:15 并众谷的斜坡，向亚珥城座落之处伸展，靠近摩押的境界。 ###EN### And the slope of the valleys That inclines toward the seat of Ar And leans toward the border of Moab.
Verse_Ch: 21:16 以色列人从那里起行，到了比珥；从前耶和华对摩西说，招聚百姓，我好给他们水喝，说的就是这井。 ###EN### And from there they journeyed to Beer; that is the well where Jehovah said to Moses, Gather the people together, and I will give them water.
Verse_Ch: 21:17 当时，以色列人唱这歌说，井阿，涌上水来！你们要向这井歌唱！ ###EN### Then Israel sang this song: Spring up, O well! Sing to it!
Verse_Ch: 21:18 这井是众首领和民中的尊贵人，用权杖用扶杖所挖所掘的。以色列人从旷野往玛他拿去， ###EN### The well, which the leaders sank, Which the nobles of the people dug, With the scepter, with their staffs. And from the wilderness they journeyed to Mattanah;
Verse_Ch: 21:19 从玛他拿到拿哈列，从拿哈列到巴末， ###EN### And from Mattanah to Nahaliel, and from Nahaliel to Bamoth;
Verse_Ch: 21:20 从巴末到摩押地的谷，又到那下望旷野之毗斯迦的山顶。 ###EN### And from Bamoth to the valley that is in the land of Moab, to the top of Pisgah, which looks down upon the desert.
Verse_Ch: 21:21 以色列人差遣使者去见亚摩利人的王西宏，说， ###EN### And Israel sent messengers to Sihon the king of the Amorites, saying,
Verse_Ch: 21:22 求你让我们从你的地经过；我们不偏入田间和葡萄园，也不喝井里的水，只走王道，直到过了你的境界。 ###EN### Let me pass through your land. We will not turn aside into field or into vineyard; we will not drink water from any well. We will go by the King's Highway, until we have passed through your territory.
Verse_Ch: 21:23 西宏不准以色列人从他的境界经过，就招聚他的众民出到旷野，攻击以色列人；他到了雅杂，与以色列人争战。 ###EN### But Sihon would not allow Israel to pass through his territory. And Sihon gathered all his people together and went out against Israel into the wilderness, and he came to Jahaz and fought against Israel.
Verse_Ch: 21:24 以色列人用刀击杀他，得了他的地，从亚嫩河到雅博河，直到亚扪人那里；因为亚扪人的边界很坚固。 ###EN### And Israel struck him with the edge of the sword and took possession of his land from the Arnon to the Jabbok, as far as the children of Ammon; for the border of the children of Ammon was strong.
Verse_Ch: 21:25 以色列人夺取这一切的城邑，也在亚摩利人的一切城邑，就是希实本与希实本的一切乡村住下。 ###EN### And Israel took all these cities, and Israel settled in all the cities of the Amorites, in Heshbon and in all her villages.
Verse_Ch: 21:26 这希实本是亚摩利人的王西宏的京城；西宏曾与摩押先前的王争战，从他手中夺取了他一切的地，直到亚嫩河。 ###EN### For Heshbon was the city of Sihon the king of the Amorites, who had fought against the former king of Moab and taken all his land out of his hand, as far as the Arnon.
Verse_Ch: 21:27 所以那些作诗歌的说，你们来到希实本；愿西宏的城被修造，得坚立。 ###EN### Therefore those who speak in proverbs say, Come to Heshbon; let it be built, And let the city of Sihon be established.
Verse_Ch: 21:28 因为有火从希实本发出，有火焰出于西宏的城，烧尽摩押的亚珥，并吞灭亚嫩河的高处。 ###EN### For fire has gone forth from Heshbon, A flame from the city of Sihon; It has consumed Ar of Moab, And swallowed up the high places of the Arnon.
Verse_Ch: 21:29 摩押阿，你有祸了！基抹的民哪，你们灭亡了；基抹使自己的男子逃奔，女子被掳，交付亚摩利人的王西宏。 ###EN### Woe to you, O Moab! You have perished, O people of Chemosh; He has given his sons as fugitives, And his daughters have gone into captivity, To an Amorite king, Sihon.
Verse_Ch: 21:30 我们射了他们；希实本尽皆毁灭，直到底本；我们使地荒凉，直到挪法；有火直烧到米底巴。 ###EN### We have shot at them; Heshbon is ruined as far as Dibon, And we have laid waste as far as Nophah, Fire spreads as far as Medeba.
Verse_Ch: 21:31 这样，以色列人就在亚摩利人之地住下。 ###EN### Thus Israel settled in the land of the Amorites.
Verse_Ch: 21:32 摩西打发人去窥探雅谢，以色列人就占了雅谢的乡村，赶出那里的亚摩利人。 ###EN### And Moses sent some to spy out Jazer. And they captured its villages and dispossessed the Amorites who were there.
Verse_Ch: 21:33 以色列人转回，由通往巴珊的路上去；巴珊王噩和他的众民都出来，在以得来与他们交战。 ###EN### And they turned and went up on the way that leads to Bashan; and Og the king of Bashan went out against them, he and all his people, for battle at Edrei.
Verse_Ch: 21:34 耶和华对摩西说，不要怕他，因我已将他和他的众民，并他的地，都交在你手中；你要对待他像对待住希实本之亚摩利人的王西宏一般。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to Moses, Do not fear him, for I have given him and all his people and his land into your hand; and you shall do to him as you did to Sihon the king of the Amorites, who was dwelling at Heshbon.
Verse_Ch: 21:35 于是他们击杀了他和他的众子，并他的众民，没有留下一个，就得了他的地。 ###EN### So they struck him and his sons and all his people until there was no remnant left to him, and they possessed his land.
Chapter_Header: 22
Verse_Ch: 22:1 以色列人起行，在约但河东的摩押平原，对着耶利哥安营。 ###EN### And the children of Israel journeyed and encamped in the plains of Moab beyond the Jordan at Jericho.
Verse_Ch: 22:2 以色列人向亚摩利人所行的一切事，西拨的儿子巴勒都看见了。 ###EN### And Balak the son of Zippor saw all that Israel had done to the Amorites.
Verse_Ch: 22:3 摩押人因以色列民甚多，就极其惧怕，心内忧急， ###EN### And Moab was very afraid of the people because they were many, and Moab was distressed because of the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 22:4 对米甸的长老说，现在这群众要把我们四围所有的一概舔尽，就如牛舔尽田间的草一般。那时西拨的儿子巴勒作摩押王。 ###EN### And Moab said to the elders of Midian, This multitude will now lick up all that is around us, as the ox licks up the grass of the field. Now Balak the son of Zippor was king of Moab at that time.
Verse_Ch: 22:5 他差遣使者往大河边的毗夺去，到比珥的儿子巴兰本乡那里，召巴兰来，说，有一民从埃及出来，遮满这地，住在我的对面。 ###EN### And he sent messengers to Balaam the son of Beor, to Pethor, which is by the River, to the land of the children of his people, to call him, saying, There is a people here who have come out from Egypt; now they cover the surface of the land and have settled over against me.
Verse_Ch: 22:6 这民比我强盛，现在求你来为我咒诅他们，或者我能击败他们，把他们赶出此地；因为我知道，你为谁祝福，谁就得福；你咒诅谁，谁就受咒诅。 ###EN### Now, therefore, please come; curse this people for me, since they are mightier than I. Perhaps I may be able to strike them and drive them out of the land, for I know that whomever you bless is blessed and whomever you curse is cursed.
Verse_Ch: 22:7 摩押的长老和米甸的长老，手里拿着占卜的礼金，到了巴兰那里，将巴勒的话告诉他。 ###EN### So the elders of Moab and the elders of Midian departed with fees for divination in their hand, and they came to Balaam and spoke to him the words of Balak.
Verse_Ch: 22:8 巴兰说，你们今夜在这里住宿，我必照耶和华所告诉我的回报你们。摩押的首领就在巴兰那里住下了。 ###EN### And he said to them, Spend tonight here, and I will bring back word to you as Jehovah speaks to me. And the rulers of Moab stayed with Balaam.
Verse_Ch: 22:9 神临到巴兰那里，说，在你这里的人都是谁？ ###EN### And God came to Balaam and said, Who are these men with you?
Verse_Ch: 22:10 巴兰回答说，是摩押王西拨的儿子巴勒打发人到我这里来，说， ###EN### And Balaam said to God, Balak the son of Zippor, the king of Moab, has sent word to me, saying,
Verse_Ch: 22:11 有一民从埃及出来，遮满了这地；现在求你来，为我咒诅他们，或者我能战胜他们，把他们赶出去。 ###EN### There is a people who came out of Egypt, and they cover the surface of the land. Now come; curse them for me; perhaps I will be able to fight against them and drive them out.
Verse_Ch: 22:12 神对巴兰说，你不可同他们去，也不可咒诅那民，因为那民是蒙福的。 ###EN### And God said to Balaam, You shall not go with them; you shall not curse the people, for they are blessed.
Verse_Ch: 22:13 巴兰早晨起来，对巴勒差来的首领说，你们回本地去罢，因为耶和华不许我和你们同去。 ###EN### So Balaam rose up in the morning and said to the rulers from Balak, Go to your land, for Jehovah has refused to let me go with you.
Verse_Ch: 22:14 摩押的首领就起来，回巴勒那里去，说，巴兰不肯和我们同来。 ###EN### And the rulers of Moab rose up and went to Balak and said, Balaam refuses to come with us.
Verse_Ch: 22:15 巴勒又差遣首领，比先前的更多更尊贵。 ###EN### So Balak yet again sent rulers, more numerous and more honorable than these.
Verse_Ch: 22:16 他们到了巴兰那里，对他说，西拨的儿子巴勒这样说，求你不让什么事拦阻你到我这里来， ###EN### And they came to Balaam and said to him, Thus says Balak the son of Zippor, Please let nothing hinder you from coming to me,
Verse_Ch: 22:17 因为我必使你得极大的尊荣；你向我说什么，我就去作；只求你来为我咒诅这民。 ###EN### For I will indeed honor you greatly; and whatever you say to me I will do. Please come therefore; curse this people for me.
Verse_Ch: 22:18 巴兰回答巴勒的臣仆说，即使巴勒将他满屋的金银给我，我也不可越过耶和华我神的话作事，少作多作都不可。 ###EN### And Balaam answered and said to the servants of Balak, Even if Balak were to give me his house full of silver and gold, I could not go beyond the word of Jehovah my God, to do less or more.
Verse_Ch: 22:19 现在请你们今夜也在这里住宿，等我得知耶和华还要对我说什么。 ###EN### Now you therefore please stay here tonight also, so that I may know what more Jehovah might speak to me.
Verse_Ch: 22:20 当夜，神临到巴兰那里，对他说，这些人既来召你，你就起来同他们去，但你只当遵行我对你所说的话。 ###EN### And God came to Balaam at night and said to him, Since the men have come to call you, rise up; go with them, but only what I speak to you shall you do.
Verse_Ch: 22:21 巴兰早晨起来，备上驴，和摩押的首领一同去了。 ###EN### And Balaam rose up in the morning and saddled his donkey and went with the rulers of Moab.
Verse_Ch: 22:22 神因他去就发怒；耶和华的使者站在路上抵挡他。他骑着驴，有两个仆人跟随他。 ###EN### And God's anger was kindled because he was going, and the Angel of Jehovah took His stand in the way as an adversary against him. Now he was riding on his donkey, and his two servants were with him.
Verse_Ch: 22:23 驴看见耶和华的使者站在路上，手里有拔出来的刀，就从路上转开，跨进田间；巴兰便打驴，要叫它转回路上。 ###EN### And when the donkey saw the Angel of Jehovah standing in the way with His drawn sword in His hand, the donkey turned aside out of the way and went into the field. And Balaam struck the donkey to turn her back into the way.
Verse_Ch: 22:24 耶和华的使者就站在葡萄园间的窄路上，这边有墙，那边也有墙。 ###EN### Then the Angel of Jehovah stood in a narrow path between the vineyards, with a wall on this side and a wall on that side.
Verse_Ch: 22:25 驴看见耶和华的使者，就贴靠墙，将巴兰的脚挤伤了；于是巴兰又打驴。 ###EN### And when the donkey saw the Angel of Jehovah, she pressed herself against the wall and crushed Balaam's foot against the wall. So he struck her again.
Verse_Ch: 22:26 耶和华的使者又往前去，站在狭窄之处，左右都无路可以转折。 ###EN### And the Angel of Jehovah went further and stood in a narrow place, where there was no way to turn either to the right or to the left.
Verse_Ch: 22:27 驴看见耶和华的使者，就卧在巴兰底下；巴兰就发怒，用杖打驴。 ###EN### And when the donkey saw the Angel of Jehovah, she lay down under Balaam. Then Balaam's anger was kindled, and he struck the donkey with his staff.
Verse_Ch: 22:28 耶和华开了驴的口，驴对巴兰说，我向你行了什么，你竟打我这三次呢？ ###EN### And Jehovah opened the mouth of the donkey, and she said to Balaam, What have I done to you, that you have struck me these three times?
Verse_Ch: 22:29 巴兰对驴说，因为你戏弄我，我若手中有刀，早就把你杀了。 ###EN### And Balaam said to the donkey, Because you have mocked me! If I had a sword in my hand, I would have killed you by now.
Verse_Ch: 22:30 驴对巴兰说，我不是你从小时直到今日所骑的驴么？我素常向你这样行过么？巴兰说，没有。 ###EN### And the donkey said to Balaam, Am I not your donkey on which you have ridden all your life to this day? Have I ever been accustomed to do so to you? And he said, No.
Verse_Ch: 22:31 当时，耶和华开了巴兰的眼，他就看见耶和华的使者站在路上，手里有拔出来的刀，巴兰便低头，面伏于地。 ###EN### Then Jehovah opened the eyes of Balaam, and he saw the Angel of Jehovah standing in the way with His drawn sword in His hand, and he bowed his head and fell on his face.
Verse_Ch: 22:32 耶和华的使者对他说，你为何这三次打你的驴呢？看哪，我出来抵挡你，因你所行的路，在我面前是邪僻的。 ###EN### And the Angel of Jehovah said to him, Why have you struck your donkey these three times? I am here, having come out as an adversary, because your way was unrestrained before Me.
Verse_Ch: 22:33 驴看见我，就三次从我面前转开；驴若没有从我转开，我必早把你杀了，留它存活。 ###EN### And the donkey saw Me and turned aside before Me these three times. If she had not turned aside from Me, I would surely have killed you just now and let her live.
Verse_Ch: 22:34 巴兰对耶和华的使者说，我有罪了，我不知道你站在路上阻挡我；你若不喜欢我去，我就转回。 ###EN### And Balaam said to the Angel of Jehovah, I have sinned, for I did not know that You were standing in the way against me. Now then, if it displeases You, I will turn back.
Verse_Ch: 22:35 耶和华的使者对巴兰说，你同这些人去罢；你只要说我对你说的话。于是巴兰同着巴勒差来的首领去了。 ###EN### And the Angel of Jehovah said to Balaam, Go with the men; but you shall speak only the word that I shall speak to you. So Balaam went with the rulers from Balak.
Verse_Ch: 22:36 巴勒听见巴兰来了，就往摩押城去迎接他；这城是在边界的尽头，在亚嫩河旁。 ###EN### And when Balak heard that Balaam was coming, he went out to meet him at the city of Moab, which is on the border of the Arnon, at the farthest point of the border.
Verse_Ch: 22:37 巴勒对巴兰说，我不是急急的打发人到你那里去召你么？你为何不到我这里来呢？我岂不能使你得尊荣么？ ###EN### And Balak said to Balaam, Did I not send word urgently to you to call you? Why did you not come to me? Am I not indeed able to honor you?
Verse_Ch: 22:38 巴兰说，我已经到你这里来了；现在我岂能擅自说什么呢？神将什么话放在我口中，我就说什么。 ###EN### And Balaam said to Balak, Here I am; I have come to you now. Am I able to speak anything at all? The word that God puts in my mouth, that I shall speak.
Verse_Ch: 22:39 巴兰和巴勒同行，来到基列胡琐。 ###EN### And Balaam went with Balak, and they came to Kiriath-huzoth.
Verse_Ch: 22:40 巴勒宰献了牛羊，送给巴兰和陪伴的首领。 ###EN### And Balak sacrificed oxen and sheep, and sent them to Balaam and to the rulers who were with him.
Verse_Ch: 22:41 到了早晨，巴勒领巴兰上到巴末巴力；巴兰从那里观看以色列营的边缘。 ###EN### And in the morning Balak took Balaam and brought him up to Bamoth- baal, and he saw from there the edge of the people.
Chapter_Header: 23
Verse_Ch: 23:1 巴兰对巴勒说，你在这里为我筑七座坛，又在这里为我预备七只公牛和七只公绵羊。 ###EN### Then Balaam said to Balak, Build me seven altars here, and have seven bulls and seven rams ready for me here.
Verse_Ch: 23:2 巴勒照巴兰的话行了。巴勒和巴兰在每座坛上献一只公牛和一只公绵羊。 ###EN### And Balak did just as Balaam had spoken. And Balak and Balaam offered up a bull and a ram on each altar.
Verse_Ch: 23:3 巴兰对巴勒说，你站在你的燔祭旁边，我要往前去，或者耶和华会来迎见我；祂指示我什么，我必告诉你。于是巴兰上到一个光秃的高处。 ###EN### And Balaam said to Balak, Stand near your burnt offering, and I will go; perhaps Jehovah will come to meet me; and whatever He shows me I will tell you. And he went to a bare height.
Verse_Ch: 23:4 神迎见巴兰；巴兰说，我预备了七座坛，在每座坛上献了一只公牛和一只公绵羊。 ###EN### And God met Balaam, and he said to Him, I have prepared the seven altars, and I have offered up a bull and a ram on each altar.
Verse_Ch: 23:5 耶和华将话放在巴兰口中，又说，你回到巴勒那里，要如此如此说。 ###EN### And Jehovah put a word in Balaam's mouth and said, Return to Balak, and you shall speak this.
Verse_Ch: 23:6 他就回到巴勒那里，见巴勒同摩押的众首领都站在燔祭旁边。 ###EN### When he returned to him, there he was, standing beside his burnt offering, he and all the rulers of Moab.
Verse_Ch: 23:7 巴兰便题起诗歌说，巴勒引我出亚兰，摩押王引我出东方的山，说，来阿，为我咒诅雅各；来阿，怒骂以色列。 ###EN### And he took up his parable and said, From Aram Balak brought me, The king of Moab from the mountains of the East. Come, curse Jacob for me; And come, denounce Israel!
Verse_Ch: 23:8 神没有咒诅的，我焉能咒诅？耶和华没有怒骂的，我焉能怒骂？ ###EN### How shall I curse whom God has not cursed? And how can I denounce whom Jehovah has not denounced?
Verse_Ch: 23:9 我从高峰看他，从小山望他；这是独居的民，不将自己算在万民中。 ###EN### For from the top of the rocks I see him, And from the hills I behold him. Here is a people who live alone And do not reckon themselves among the nations.
Verse_Ch: 23:10 谁能数算雅各的尘土？谁能数点以色列的四分之一？愿我之死如正直人之死；愿我之终如正直人之终。 ###EN### Who can count the dust of Jacob, Or number the fourth part of Israel? Let me die the death of the upright, And let my latter end be like theirs!
Verse_Ch: 23:11 巴勒对巴兰说，你向我作的是什么事？我领你来咒诅我的仇敌，不料，你竟完全为他们祝福。 ###EN### And Balak said to Balaam, What have you done to me? I took you to curse my enemies, but now you have altogether blessed them.
Verse_Ch: 23:12 他回答说，耶和华放在我口中的话，我能不谨慎讲说么？ ###EN### And he answered and said, Shall I not take care to speak what Jehovah puts in my mouth?
Verse_Ch: 23:13 巴勒说，求你同我往另一处去，你从那里可以看见他们；你不能看见他们全部，只能看见他们营的边缘。你要从那里为我咒诅他们。 ###EN### And Balak said to him, Come now with me to another place from which you may see them. You will see only the outside edge of them and not see them all; then curse them for me from there.
Verse_Ch: 23:14 于是巴勒领巴兰到琐腓田，上毗斯迦山顶，筑了七座坛；每座坛上献一只公牛和一只公绵羊。 ###EN### So he took him into the field of Zophim, to the top of Pisgah, and built seven altars and offered up a bull and a ram on each altar.
Verse_Ch: 23:15 巴兰对巴勒说，你在这里站在你的燔祭旁边，等我往那边去迎见耶和华。 ###EN### And he said to Balak, Stand here near your burnt offering, while I meet Jehovah there.
Verse_Ch: 23:16 耶和华迎见巴兰，将话放在他口中，又说，你回到巴勒那里，要如此如此说。 ###EN### And Jehovah met Balaam and put a word in his mouth and said, Return to Balak, and you shall speak this.
Verse_Ch: 23:17 他就回到巴勒那里，见他站在燔祭旁边；摩押的首领也和他在一起。巴勒问巴兰说，耶和华说了什么话？ ###EN### When he came to him, there he was, standing beside his burnt offering, and the rulers of Moab with him. And Balak said to him, What has Jehovah spoken?
Verse_Ch: 23:18 巴兰便题起诗歌说，巴勒阿，你起来听；西拨的儿子阿，你向我侧耳。 ###EN### And he took up his parable and said, Arise, O Balak, and hear; Listen to me, O son of Zippor:
Verse_Ch: 23:19 神并非人，必不至说谎，也非人子，必不至后悔。祂说话，岂能不作成？祂发言，岂能不立定？ ###EN### God is not a man, that He should lie, Nor a son of man, that He should repent. Has He said, and will He not do it? Or has He spoken, and will He not establish it?
Verse_Ch: 23:20 我奉命祝福；神既已赐福，这事我不能翻转。 ###EN### Now I have received a word to bless; Since He has blessed, then I cannot reverse it.
Verse_Ch: 23:21 祂未见雅各中有罪孽，也未见以色列中有祸患；耶和华他们的神与他们同在，有向王欢呼的声音在他们中间。 ###EN### He has not beheld iniquity in Jacob, Nor has He seen trouble in Israel; Jehovah their God is with them, And the shout of a king is among them.
Verse_Ch: 23:22 神领他们出埃及；他们似乎有野牛之力。 ###EN### God is the One who brought them forth out of Egypt, He has as it were the horns of the wild ox.
Verse_Ch: 23:23 断没有法术可以害雅各，也没有占卜可以害以色列。现在人论到雅各，论到以色列，必说，神行了何等的事！ ###EN### Surely there is no enchantment against Jacob, Nor is there any divination against Israel. Now it shall be said of Jacob And of Israel, What has God wrought!
Verse_Ch: 23:24 看哪，这民起来仿佛母狮，挺身好像公狮；未吃野食，未喝被杀者之血，绝不躺卧。 ###EN### See, a people rises up like a lioness, And like a lion they lift themselves up. They shall not lie down until they eat the prey And drink the blood of the slain.
Verse_Ch: 23:25 巴勒对巴兰说，那么你一点不要咒诅他们，也一点不要为他们祝福。 ###EN### And Balak said to Balaam, Neither curse them at all, nor bless them at all.
Verse_Ch: 23:26 巴兰回答说，我岂不曾告诉你说，凡耶和华所说的，我必须遵行么？ ###EN### But Balaam answered and said to Balak, Did I not tell you, saying, All that Jehovah speaks, that I must do?
Verse_Ch: 23:27 巴勒对巴兰说，来罢，我领你往另一处去；或者神喜欢你从那里为我咒诅他们。 ###EN### And Balak said to Balaam, Come now, I will take you to another place; perhaps it will please God that you may curse them for me from there.
Verse_Ch: 23:28 巴勒就领巴兰到那下望旷野的毗珥山顶上。 ###EN### And Balak took Balaam to the top of Peor, which looks down upon the desert.
Verse_Ch: 23:29 巴兰对巴勒说，你在这里为我筑七座坛，又在这里为我预备七只公牛和七只公绵羊。 ###EN### And Balaam said to Balak, Build me seven altars here, and have seven bulls and seven rams ready for me here.
Verse_Ch: 23:30 巴勒就照巴兰的话行，在每座坛上献一只公牛和一只公绵羊。 ###EN### And Balak did just as Balaam had said, and he offered up a bull and a ram on each altar.
Chapter_Header: 24
Verse_Ch: 24:1 巴兰见耶和华喜欢赐福与以色列，就不像前两次去求法术，却面向旷野。 ###EN### And when Balaam saw that it pleased Jehovah to bless Israel, he did not go as at the other times to meet with enchantments, but he set his face toward the wilderness.
Verse_Ch: 24:2 巴兰举目，看见以色列人按支派居住，神的灵就临到他身上。 ###EN### And Balaam lifted up his eyes and saw Israel dwelling according to their tribes, and the Spirit of God came upon him.
Verse_Ch: 24:3 他便题起诗歌说，比珥的儿子巴兰宣告说，眼目睁开的人宣告说， ###EN### And he took up his parable and said, Balaam the son of Beor declares, And the man whose eye is opened declares;
Verse_Ch: 24:4 得听神的言语，得见全足者的异象，仆倒而眼目得开的人宣告说， ###EN### He declares, he who hears the words of God, Who sees the vision of the All-sufficient One, Falling down, but having his eyes uncovered:
Verse_Ch: 24:5 雅各阿，你的帐棚何其佳美！以色列阿，你的帐幕何其华丽！ ###EN### How fair are your tents, O Jacob, Your tabernacles, O Israel!
Verse_Ch: 24:6 如延展的山谷，如河旁的园子，如耶和华所栽的沉香树，如水边的香柏木。 ###EN### Like valleys they are spread forth, Like gardens beside a river, Like aloes which Jehovah has planted, Like cedars beside water.
Verse_Ch: 24:7 水要从他的桶里流出，他的种子必撒在多水之处；他的王必超过亚甲，他的国必被高举。 ###EN### Water shall flow from his buckets, And his seed shall be in many waters, And his king shall be higher than Agag, And his kingdom shall be exalted.
Verse_Ch: 24:8 神领他出埃及；他似乎有野牛之力。他必吞吃敌国，打碎他们的骨头，用箭射透他们。 ###EN### God is the One who brought him forth out of Egypt; He has as it were the horns of the wild ox. He shall eat up the nations, his adversaries, And shall break their bones in pieces, And shatter them with his arrows.
Verse_Ch: 24:9 他蹲卧如公狮，又如母狮，谁敢惹他？凡给你祝福的，愿他蒙福；凡咒诅你的，愿他受咒诅。 ###EN### He couches; he lies down like a lion And like a lioness; who will rouse him up? Blessed is everyone who blesses you, And cursed is everyone who curses you.
Verse_Ch: 24:10 巴勒向巴兰发怒，就拍掌对他说，我召你来为我咒诅仇敌，不料，你这三次竟完全为他们祝福。 ###EN### Then Balak's anger was kindled against Balaam, and he struck his hands together. And Balak said to Balaam, I called you to curse my enemies, but now you have altogether blessed them these three times.
Verse_Ch: 24:11 如今你快回本地去罢！我说过我要使你得大尊荣，耶和华却不让你得尊荣。 ###EN### Therefore now flee to your place! I said I would greatly honor you, but now Jehovah has kept you away from honor.
Verse_Ch: 24:12 巴兰对巴勒说，我岂不曾告诉你所差遣到我那里的使者说， ###EN### And Balaam said to Balak, Did I not also speak to your messengers whom you sent to me, saying,
Verse_Ch: 24:13 即使巴勒将他满屋的金银给我，我也不能越过耶和华的话，凭自己的心意行好行歹么？耶和华说什么，我就说什么。 ###EN### Even if Balak were to give me his house full of silver and gold, I could not go beyond the word of Jehovah, to do either good or bad from my own heart? What Jehovah speaks, that I will speak.
Verse_Ch: 24:14 现在我要回本族去。你来，我指示你这民日后要怎样待你的民。 ###EN### And now therefore, I am going to my people. Come, let me give you counsel as to what this people will do to your people in the last days.
Verse_Ch: 24:15 他就题起诗歌说，比珥的儿子巴兰宣告说，眼目睁开的人宣告说， ###EN### And he took up his parable and said, Balaam the son of Beor declares, And the man whose eye is opened declares;
Verse_Ch: 24:16 得听神的言语，得知至高者的知识，得见全足者的异象，仆倒而眼目得开的人宣告说， ###EN### He declares, he who hears the words of God And obtains the knowledge of the Most High, Who sees the vision of the All-sufficient One, Falling down, but having his eyes uncovered:
Verse_Ch: 24:17 我看祂，却不在现时；我望祂，却不在近日。必有一星从雅各而出，必有一杖从以色列兴起，祂必打碎摩押的四角，毁坏所有舍特的子孙。 ###EN### I see Him, but not now; I behold Him, but not near. There shall come forth a Star out of Jacob, And a Scepter shall rise out of Israel, And He shall crush the corners of Moab, And break down all the sons of Sheth.
Verse_Ch: 24:18 祂必得以东为基业，又得仇敌之地西珥为产业；以色列必行事勇敢。 ###EN### And Edom shall be dispossessed, Seir, His enemies, shall also be dispossessed; While Israel does valiantly.
Verse_Ch: 24:19 有一位出于雅各的，必掌大权，并除灭城中的余民。 ###EN### And One from Jacob shall have dominion And destroy the remnant from the city.
Verse_Ch: 24:20 巴兰观看亚玛力，就题起诗歌说，亚玛力原为诸国之首，但他终必灭亡。 ###EN### And he looked on Amalek and took up his parable and said, Amalek was the first of the nations, But his latter end shall come to destruction.
Verse_Ch: 24:21 巴兰观看基尼人，就题起诗歌说，你的住处坚固，你的窝巢造在磐石中。 ###EN### And he looked on the Kenites and took up his parable and said, Strong is your dwelling place, And your nest is set in the rock.
Verse_Ch: 24:22 然而基尼必被烧毁；直到亚述把你掳去。 ###EN### Nevertheless Kain shall be burned Until Asshur carry you away captive.
Verse_Ch: 24:23 巴兰又题起诗歌说，哀哉，神行这事，谁能得活？ ###EN### And he took up his parable and said, Alas, who shall live when God does this?
Verse_Ch: 24:24 必有人乘船从基提海岸而来，苦害亚述，苦害希伯；他也必灭亡。 ###EN### But ships shall come from the coast of Kittim, And they shall afflict Asshur and shall afflict Eber; And he also shall come to destruction.
Verse_Ch: 24:25 于是巴兰起来，回他本地去；巴勒也回去了。 ###EN### And Balaam rose up and went back to his place, and Balak also went his way.
Chapter_Header: 25
Verse_Ch: 25:1 以色列人住在什亭，百姓与摩押女子行起淫乱。 ###EN### While Israel dwelt in Shittim, the people began to commit fornication with the daughters of Moab.
Verse_Ch: 25:2 这些女子邀百姓来，给她们的神献祭，百姓就吃她们的祭物，跪拜她们的神。 ###EN### For they invited the people to the sacrifices of their gods, and the people ate and bowed down to their gods.
