Verse_Ch: 25:3 以色列人与巴力毗珥连合，耶和华的怒气就向以色列人发作。 ###EN### And Israel joined itself to Baal-peor, and the anger of Jehovah was kindled against Israel.
Verse_Ch: 25:4 耶和华对摩西说，将百姓中所有的族长，在我耶和华面前对着日头悬挂，使我耶和华的烈怒可以从以色列人转消。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to Moses, Take all the leaders of the people and hang them up to Jehovah before the sun, so that the fierce anger of Jehovah may turn away from Israel.
Verse_Ch: 25:5 于是摩西对以色列的审判官说，凡属你们的人，有与巴力毗珥连合的，你们各人要把他们杀了。 ###EN### And Moses said to the judges of Israel, Each of you slay his men who have joined themselves to Baal-peor.
Verse_Ch: 25:6 摩西和以色列人全会众正在会幕门口哭泣的时候，有以色列人中的一个人，竟然当他们眼前，带着一个米甸女人到他弟兄们那里。 ###EN### Just then one of the children of Israel came and brought a Midianite woman to his brothers in the sight of Moses and in the sight of the whole assembly of the children of Israel, while they were weeping at the entrance of the Tent of Meeting.
Verse_Ch: 25:7 祭司亚伦的孙子，以利亚撒的儿子非尼哈看见了，就从会中起来，手里拿着枪， ###EN### And when Phinehas the son of Eleazar, the son of Aaron the priest, saw it, he rose up from the midst of the assembly, and took a spear in his hand,
Verse_Ch: 25:8 跟随那以色列人进内棚去，将以色列人和那女人由腹中刺透。这样，在以色列人中的瘟疫就止息了。 ###EN### And went after the man of Israel into the tent and pierced both of them, the man of Israel and the woman through her stomach. So the plague among the children of Israel was stopped.
Verse_Ch: 25:9 那时遭瘟疫死的，有二万四千人。 ###EN### And those who died by the plague were twenty-four thousand.
Verse_Ch: 25:10 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 25:11 祭司亚伦的孙子，以利亚撒的儿子非尼哈，使我的怒气从以色列人转消；因他在他们中间，以我的妒忌妒忌他们，使我不在妒忌中把他们除灭。 ###EN### Phinehas the son of Eleazar, the son of Aaron the priest, has turned My wrath away from the children of Israel, in that he was jealous with My jealousy among them, so that I did not consume the children of Israel in My jealousy.
Verse_Ch: 25:12 因此，你要说，我将我平安的约赐给他； ###EN### Therefore say, I now give him My covenant of peace,
Verse_Ch: 25:13 这约要给他和他的后裔，作永远祭司职任的约；因他为神起了妒忌，为以色列人遮罪。 ###EN### And it shall be to him and to his seed after him, the covenant of an everlasting priesthood, because he was jealous for his God and made expiation for the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 25:14 那与米甸女人一同被杀的以色列人，名叫心利，是撒路的儿子，是西缅一个宗族的首领。 ###EN### Now the name of the slain man of Israel, who was slain with the Midianite woman, was Zimri the son of Salu, a leader of a father's household among the Simeonites.
Verse_Ch: 25:15 那被杀的米甸女人，名叫哥斯比，是苏珥的女儿；这苏珥是米甸一个宗族的首领。 ###EN### And the name of the Midianite woman who was slain was Cozbi the daughter of Zur, head of the people of a father's household in Midian.
Verse_Ch: 25:16 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 25:17 你要扰害米甸人，击杀他们； ###EN### Harass the Midianites and strike them;
Verse_Ch: 25:18 因为他们用诡计扰害你们，在毗珥的事上，并在他们的姊妹，米甸首领的女儿哥斯比的事上，用这诡计诱惑了你们；这哥斯比，当瘟疫流行的日子， 因毗珥的事被杀了。 ###EN### For they have harassed you with their deception with which they have deceived you in the matter of Peor and in the matter of Cozbi, the daughter of the prince of Midian, their sister, who was slain on the day of the plague in the matter of Peor.
Chapter_Header: 26
Verse_Ch: 26:1 瘟疫之后，耶和华对摩西和祭司亚伦的儿子以利亚撒说， ###EN### Now after the plague Jehovah spoke to Moses and to Eleazar the son of Aaron the priest, saying,
Verse_Ch: 26:2 你们要将以色列人全会众，按他们的宗族，凡以色列中从二十岁以上能出去打仗的，计算总数。 ###EN### Take the sum of the whole assembly of the children of Israel, from twenty years old and upward, by their fathers' households, all who are able to go forth for military service in Israel.
Verse_Ch: 26:3 于是摩西和祭司以利亚撒，在摩押平原与耶利哥相对的约但河边，向以色列人说， ###EN### So Moses and Eleazar the priest spoke with them in the plains of Moab by the Jordan at Jericho, saying,
Verse_Ch: 26:4 要将你们中间从二十岁以上的，计算总数；这是照耶和华所吩咐摩西的。从埃及地出来的以色列人如下： ###EN### Take the sum of the people, from twenty years old and upward, as Jehovah commanded Moses. Now the children of Israel, who came forth out of the land of Egypt were:
Verse_Ch: 26:5 以色列的长子是流便。流便的众子，属哈诺的，有哈诺家族；属法路的，有法路家族； ###EN### Reuben, the firstborn of Israel; the sons of Reuben: of Hanoch, the family of the Hanochites; of Pallu, the family of the Palluites;
Verse_Ch: 26:6 属希斯伦的，有希斯伦家族；属迦米的，有迦米家族。 ###EN### Of Hezron, the family of the Hezronites; of Carmi, the family of the Carmites.
Verse_Ch: 26:7 这些是流便的各家族；他们中间被数点的，有四万三千七百三十名。 ###EN### These are the families of the Reubenites, and those who were numbered of them were forty-three thousand seven hundred thirty.
Verse_Ch: 26:8 法路的儿子是以利押。 ###EN### And the sons of Pallu: Eliab.
Verse_Ch: 26:9 以利押的众子是尼母利、大坍、亚比兰。这大坍、亚比兰原是会众中选召的，在可拉一党向耶和华争闹的时候，也随伙向摩西、亚伦争闹； ###EN### And the sons of Eliab: Nemuel and Dathan and Abiram. These are the Dathan and Abiram, who were called by the assembly, who contended against Moses and against Aaron in the company of Korah, when they contended against Jehovah;
Verse_Ch: 26:10 地便开口，把他们和可拉一同吞灭，可拉一党就都死了；那时火烧灭了二百五十个人；他们就作了警戒。 ###EN### And the earth opened its mouth and swallowed them up together with Korah, when that company died, when the fire consumed two hundred fifty men; and they became a sign.
Verse_Ch: 26:11 然而可拉的众子没有死亡。 ###EN### But the sons of Korah did not die.
Verse_Ch: 26:12 西缅的众子按着家族，属尼母利的，有尼母利家族；属雅悯的，有雅悯家族；属雅斤的，有雅斤家族； ###EN### The sons of Simeon according to their families: of Nemuel, the family of the Nemuelites; of Jamin, the family of the Jaminites; of Jachin, the family of the Jachinites;
Verse_Ch: 26:13 属谢拉的，有谢拉家族；属扫罗的，有扫罗家族。 ###EN### Of Zerah, the family of the Zerahites; of Shaul, the family of the Shaulites.
Verse_Ch: 26:14 这些是西缅的各家族，共有二万二千二百名。 ###EN### These are the families of the Simeonites, twenty-two thousand two hundred.
Verse_Ch: 26:15 迦得的众子按着家族，属洗分的，有洗分家族；属哈基的，有哈基家族；属书尼的，有书尼家族； ###EN### The sons of Gad according to their families: of Zephon, the family of the Zephonites; of Haggi, the family of the Haggites; of Shuni, the family of the Shunites;
Verse_Ch: 26:16 属阿斯尼的，有阿斯尼家族；属以利的，有以利家族； ###EN### Of Ozni, the family of the Oznites; of Eri, the family of the Erites;
Verse_Ch: 26:17 属亚律的，有亚律家族；属亚列利的，有亚列利家族。 ###EN### Of Arod, the family of the Arodites; of Areli, the family of the Arelites.
Verse_Ch: 26:18 这些是迦得子孙的各家族，照他们中间被数点的，有四万零五百名。 ###EN### These are the families of the sons of Gad according to those who were numbered of them, forty thousand five hundred.
Verse_Ch: 26:19 犹大的儿子是珥和俄南；珥和俄南死在迦南地。 ###EN### The sons of Judah: Er and Onan; but Er and Onan died in the land of Canaan.
Verse_Ch: 26:20 犹大其余的众子按着家族，属示拉的，有示拉家族；属法勒斯的，有法勒斯家族；属谢拉的，有谢拉家族； ###EN### And the sons of Judah according to their families were: of Shelah, the family of the Shelanites; of Perez, the family of the Perezites; of Zerah, the family of the Zerahites.
Verse_Ch: 26:21 法勒斯的儿子，属希斯伦的，有希斯伦家族；属哈母勒的，有哈母勒家族。 ###EN### And the sons of Perez were: of Hezron, the family of the Hezronites; of Hamul, the family of the Hamulites.
Verse_Ch: 26:22 这些是犹大的各家族，照他们中间被数点的，有七万六千五百名。 ###EN### These are the families of Judah according to those who were numbered of them, seventy-six thousand five hundred.
Verse_Ch: 26:23 以萨迦的众子按着家族，属陀拉的，有陀拉家族；属普瓦的，有普瓦家族； ###EN### The sons of Issachar according to their families: of Tola, the family of the Tolaites; of Puvah, the family of the Punites;
Verse_Ch: 26:24 属雅述的，有雅述家族；属伸仑的，有伸仑家族。 ###EN### Of Jashub, the family of the Jashubites; of Shimron, the family of the Shimronites.
Verse_Ch: 26:25 这些是以萨迦的各家族，照他们中间被数点的，有六万四千三百名。 ###EN### These are the families of Issachar according to those who were numbered of them, sixty-four thousand three hundred.
Verse_Ch: 26:26 西布伦的众子按着家族，属西烈的，有西烈家族；属以伦的，有以伦家族；属雅利的，有雅利家族。 ###EN### The sons of Zebulun according to their families: of Sered, the family of the Seredites; of Elon, the family of the Elonites; of Jahleel, the family of the Jahleelites.
Verse_Ch: 26:27 这些是西布伦的各家族，照他们中间被数点的，有六万零五百名。 ###EN### These are the families of the Zebulunites according to those who were numbered of them, sixty thousand five hundred.
Verse_Ch: 26:28 约瑟的儿子按着家族，有玛拿西和以法莲。 ###EN### The sons of Joseph according to their families: Manasseh and Ephraim.
Verse_Ch: 26:29 玛拿西的众子，属玛吉的，有玛吉家族；玛吉生基列；属基列的，有基列家族。 ###EN### The sons of Manasseh: of Machir, the family of the Machirites; and Machir begat Gilead; of Gilead, the family of the Gileadites.
Verse_Ch: 26:30 基列的众子，属伊以谢的，有伊以谢家族；属希勒的，有希勒家族； ###EN### These are the sons of Gilead: of Iezer, the family of the Iezerites; of Helek, the family of the Helekites;
Verse_Ch: 26:31 属亚斯烈的，有亚斯烈家族；属示剑的，有示剑家族； ###EN### And of Asriel, the family of the Asrielites; and of Shechem, the family of the Shechemites;
Verse_Ch: 26:32 属示米大的，有示米大家族；属希弗的，有希弗家族。 ###EN### And of Shemida, the family of the Shemidaites; and of Hepher, the family of the Hepherites.
Verse_Ch: 26:33 希弗的儿子西罗非哈没有儿子，只有女儿；西罗非哈女儿的名字是玛拉、挪阿、曷拉、密迦、得撒。 ###EN### Now Zelophehad the son of Hepher had no sons, but daughters, and the names of the daughters of Zelophehad were Mahlah and Noah, Hoglah, Milcah, and Tirzah.
Verse_Ch: 26:34 这些是玛拿西的各家族；他们中间被数点的，有五万二千七百名。 ###EN### These are the families of Manasseh; and those who were numbered of them were fifty-two thousand seven hundred.
Verse_Ch: 26:35 以法莲的众子按着家族如下：属书提拉的，有书提拉家族；属比结的，有比结家族；属他罕的，有他罕家族。 ###EN### These are the sons of Ephraim according to their families: of Shuthelah, the family of the Shuthelahites; of Becher, the family of the Becherites; of Tahan, the family of the Tahanites.
Verse_Ch: 26:36 书提拉的众子如下：属以兰的，有以兰家族。 ###EN### And these are the sons of Shuthelah: of Eran, the family of the Eranites.
Verse_Ch: 26:37 这些是以法莲子孙的各家族，照他们中间被数点的，有三万二千五百名。按着家族，这些都是约瑟的子孙。 ###EN### These are the families of the sons of Ephraim according to those who were numbered of them, thirty-two thousand five hundred. These are the sons of Joseph according to their families.
Verse_Ch: 26:38 便雅悯的众子按着家族，属比拉的，有比拉家族；属亚实别的，有亚实别家族；属亚希兰的，有亚希兰家族； ###EN### The sons of Benjamin according to their families: of Bela, the family of the Belaites; of Ashbel, the family of the Ashbelites; of Ahiram, the family of the Ahiramites;
Verse_Ch: 26:39 属书反的，有书反家族；属户反的，有户反家族。 ###EN### Of Shephupham, the family of the Shuphamites; of Hupham, the family of the Huphamites.
Verse_Ch: 26:40 比拉的儿子是亚勒和乃幔；属亚勒的，有亚勒家族；属乃幔的，有乃幔家族。 ###EN### And the sons of Bela were Ard and Naaman: of Ard, the family of the Ardites; of Naaman, the family of the Naamites.
Verse_Ch: 26:41 按着家族，这些是便雅悯的子孙；他们中间被数点的，有四万五千六百名。 ###EN### These are the sons of Benjamin according to their families; and those who were numbered of them were forty-five thousand six hundred.
Verse_Ch: 26:42 但的众子按着家族如下：属书含的，有书含家族。按着家族，这些是但的各家族。 ###EN### These are the sons of Dan according to their families: of Shuham, the family of the Shuhamites. These are the families of Dan according to their families.
Verse_Ch: 26:43 书含所有的家族，照他们中间被数点的，有六万四千四百名。 ###EN### All the families of the Shuhamites, according to those who were numbered of them, were sixty-four thousand four hundred.
Verse_Ch: 26:44 亚设的众子按着家族，属音拿的，有音拿家族；属亦施韦的，有亦施韦家族；属比利亚的，有比利亚家族。 ###EN### The sons of Asher according to their families: of Imnah, the family of the Imnites; of Ishvi, the family of the Ishvites; of Beriah, the family of the Berites.
Verse_Ch: 26:45 比利亚的众子，属希别的，有希别家族；属玛结的，有玛结家族。 ###EN### From the sons of Beriah: of Heber, the family of the Heberites; of Malchiel, the family of the Malchielites.
Verse_Ch: 26:46 亚设的女儿名叫西拉。 ###EN### And the name of the daughter of Asher was Serah.
Verse_Ch: 26:47 这些是亚设子孙的各家族，照他们中间被数点的，有五万三千四百名。 ###EN### These are the families of the sons of Asher according to those who were numbered of them, fifty-three thousand four hundred.
Verse_Ch: 26:48 拿弗他利的众子按着家族，属雅薛的，有雅薛家族；属沽尼的，有沽尼家族； ###EN### The sons of Naphtali according to their families: of Jahzeel, the family of the Jahzeelites; of Guni, the family of the Gunites;
Verse_Ch: 26:49 属耶色的，有耶色家族；属示冷的，有示冷家族。 ###EN### Of Jezer, the family of the Jezerites; of Shillem, the family of the Shillemites.
Verse_Ch: 26:50 按着家族，这些是拿弗他利的各家族；他们中间被数点的，有四万五千四百名。 ###EN### These are the families of Naphtali according to their families; and those who were numbered of them were forty-five thousand four hundred.
Verse_Ch: 26:51 这些就是以色列人中被数点的，共有六十万零一千七百三十名。 ###EN### These are those who were numbered of the children of Israel, six hundred one thousand seven hundred thirty.
Verse_Ch: 26:52 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 26:53 你要按着人名的数目，将地分给这些人为业。 ###EN### To these the land shall be divided for an inheritance according to the number of names.
Verse_Ch: 26:54 人数多的，你要把产业多分给他们；人数少的，你要把产业少分给他们；要照被数点的人数，把产业分给各支派。 ###EN### You shall increase the larger group's inheritance, and you shall reduce the smaller group's inheritance. Each shall be given their inheritance according to those who were numbered of them.
Verse_Ch: 26:55 虽是这样，还要拈阄分地；他们要按着祖宗支派的名字，承受为业。 ###EN### But the land shall be apportioned by lot; they shall inherit it according to the names of the tribes of their fathers.
Verse_Ch: 26:56 要按着所拈的阄，看人数多，人数少，把产业分给他们。 ###EN### According to the lot their inheritance shall be apportioned among the larger and the smaller groups.
Verse_Ch: 26:57 利未人按着他们各家族被数点的如下：属革顺的，有革顺家族；属哥辖的，有哥辖家族；属米拉利的，有米拉利家族。 ###EN### And these are those who were numbered of the Levites according to their families: of Gershon, the family of the Gershonites; of Kohath, the family of the Kohathites; of Merari, the family of the Merarites.
Verse_Ch: 26:58 利未的各家族，有立尼家族、希伯伦家族、玛利家族、母示家族、可拉家族。哥辖生暗兰。 ###EN### These are the families of Levi: the family of the Libnites, the family of the Hebronites, the family of the Mahlites, the family of the Mushites, the family of the Korahites. And Kohath begot Amram.
Verse_Ch: 26:59 暗兰的妻子名叫约基别，是利未的女儿，是利未在埃及所生的；她给暗兰生了亚伦、摩西、和他们的姐姐米利暗。 ###EN### And the name of Amram's wife was Jochebed, the daughter of Levi, who was born to Levi in Egypt; and she bore to Amram Aaron and Moses and their sister Miriam.
Verse_Ch: 26:60 亚伦生拿答、亚比户、以利亚撒、以他玛。 ###EN### And to Aaron were born Nadab and Abihu, Eleazar and Ithamar.
Verse_Ch: 26:61 拿答、亚比户在耶和华面前献凡火的时候死了。 ###EN### And Nadab and Abihu died when they offered strange fire before Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 26:62 利未人中，凡一个月以上的男子，被数点的有二万三千名。他们本来没有数点在以色列人中，因为在以色列人中，没有产业给他们。 ###EN### And those who were numbered of them were twenty-three thousand, every male from a month old and upward, for they were not numbered among the children of Israel, because no inheritance was given to them among the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 26:63 这些就是摩西和祭司以利亚撒所数点的；他们在摩押平原与耶利哥相对的约但河边，数点以色列人。 ###EN### These are those who were numbered by Moses and Eleazar the priest, who numbered the children of Israel in the plains of Moab by the Jordan at Jericho.
Verse_Ch: 26:64 但这些人中，没有一个是摩西和祭司亚伦从前在西乃的旷野所数点的以色列人； ###EN### But among these there was not one of those numbered by Moses and Aaron the priest, who numbered the children of Israel in the wilderness of Sinai.
Verse_Ch: 26:65 因为耶和华曾论到他们说，他们必要死在旷野。除了耶孚尼的儿子迦勒和嫩的儿子约书亚以外，连一个人也没有存留。 ###EN### For Jehovah had said of them, They shall surely die in the wilderness. And not one of them was left, except Caleb the son of Jephunneh and Joshua the son of Nun.
Chapter_Header: 27
Verse_Ch: 27:1 属约瑟儿子玛拿西各家族的，有玛拿西的玄孙，玛吉的曾孙，基列的孙子，希弗的儿子西罗非哈的女儿，名叫玛拉、挪阿、曷拉、密迦、得撒；她们 近前来， ###EN### Then the daughters of Zelophehad the son of Hepher, the son of Gilead, the son of Machir, the son of Manasseh, of the families of Manasseh the son of Joseph came near. And these are the names of his daughters: Mahlah, Noah, and Hoglah, and Milcah and Tirzah.
Verse_Ch: 27:2 站在会幕门口，在摩西和祭司以利亚撒，并众首领与全会众面前，说， ###EN### And they stood before Moses and before Eleazar the priest and before the leaders and the whole assembly at the entrance of the Tent of Meeting, saying,
Verse_Ch: 27:3 我们的父亲死在旷野，他没有在可拉一党中，随从他们聚集攻击耶和华，是在自己罪中死的；他也没有儿子。 ###EN### Our father died in the wilderness, and he was not among the company of those who gathered themselves together against Jehovah in the company of Korah; but he died in his own sin, and he had no sons.
Verse_Ch: 27:4 为什么因我们的父亲没有儿子，就把他的名从他家族中除掉呢？求你们在我们父亲的弟兄中，给我们产业。 ###EN### Why should our father's name be taken away from among his family because he had no son? Give us a possession among our father's brothers.
Verse_Ch: 27:5 于是，摩西将她们的案件呈到耶和华面前。 ###EN### And Moses brought their case before Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 27:6 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 27:7 西罗非哈的女儿说得有理。你一定要在她们父亲的弟兄中，把地业给她们作产业；要将她们父亲的产业归给她们。 ###EN### The daughters of Zelophehad speak rightly. You shall surely give them the possession of an inheritance among their father's brothers; and you shall cause the inheritance of their father to pass to them.
Verse_Ch: 27:8 也要对以色列人说，人若死了没有儿子，就要把他的产业归给他的女儿。 ###EN### And you shall speak to the children of Israel, saying, If a man dies and has no son, then you shall cause his inheritance to pass to his daughter.
Verse_Ch: 27:9 他若没有女儿，就要把他的产业给他的弟兄。 ###EN### And if he does not have a daughter, then you shall give his inheritance to his brothers.
Verse_Ch: 27:10 他若没有弟兄，就要把他的产业给他父亲的弟兄。 ###EN### And if he has no brothers, then you shall give his inheritance to his father's brothers.
Verse_Ch: 27:11 他父亲若没有弟兄，就要把他的产业给他家族中最近的亲属，他便要得为业。这要作以色列人判断的律例，是照耶和华所吩咐摩西的。 ###EN### And if his father has no brothers, then you shall give his inheritance to his relative nearest to him among his family, and he shall possess it. And it shall be a statute of judgment for the children of Israel, as Jehovah commanded Moses.
Verse_Ch: 27:12 耶和华对摩西说，你上这亚巴琳山，观看我所赐给以色列人的地。 ###EN### And Jehovah said to Moses, Go up to this mountain of the Abarim and see the land which I have given to the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 27:13 看了以后，你也必归到你本民那里，像你哥哥亚伦一样； ###EN### And when you have seen it, you also shall be gathered to your people, just as Aaron your brother was gathered,
Verse_Ch: 27:14 因为你们在寻的旷野，当会众争闹的时候，违背了我的话，没有在涌水之处，在会众眼前尊我为圣。(这水就是在寻的旷野的加低斯米利巴水。) ###EN### Because you rebelled against My word in the wilderness of Zin, in the strife of the assembly, and failed to sanctify Me at the waters before their eyes. (These are the waters of Meribah-kadesh, in the wilderness of Zin.)
Verse_Ch: 27:15 摩西对耶和华说， ###EN### And Moses spoke to Jehovah, saying,
Verse_Ch: 27:16 愿耶和华万人之灵的神，立一个人治理会众， ###EN### Let Jehovah, the God of the spirits of all flesh, appoint a man over the assembly,
Verse_Ch: 27:17 可以在他们面前出入，也可以引领他们出入，免得耶和华的会众如同没有牧人的羊群一般。 ###EN### Who will go out before them and who will come in before them, and who will lead them out and who will bring them in; so that the assembly of Jehovah will not be like sheep which have no shepherd.
Verse_Ch: 27:18 耶和华对摩西说，你要将嫩的儿子约书亚领来，这人里面有神的灵；你要按手在他头上， ###EN### And Jehovah said to Moses, Take Joshua the son of Nun, a man in whom is the Spirit, and lay your hand upon him;
Verse_Ch: 27:19 使他站在祭司以利亚撒和全会众面前，在他们眼前嘱咐他， ###EN### And set him before Eleazar the priest and before the whole assembly, and give him a charge in their sight.
Verse_Ch: 27:20 又要将你的尊荣给他几分，使以色列人全会众都听从他。 ###EN### And you shall put some of your honor upon him, so that the whole assembly of the children of Israel may obey him.
Verse_Ch: 27:21 他要站在祭司以利亚撒面前，以利亚撒要凭乌陵的判断，在耶和华面前为他求问。他和以色列全会众都要遵以利亚撒的话出入。 ###EN### And he shall stand before Eleazar the priest, and he shall inquire for him by the judgment of the Urim before Jehovah. At his word shall they go out and at his word they shall come in, both he and all the children of Israel with him, even the whole assembly.
Verse_Ch: 27:22 于是摩西照耶和华所吩咐的去行；他将约书亚领来，使他站在祭司以利亚撒和全会众面前， ###EN### And Moses did as Jehovah commanded him, and he took Joshua and set him before Eleazar the priest and before the whole assembly.
Verse_Ch: 27:23 按手在他头上，嘱咐他，正如耶和华藉摩西所说的。 ###EN### And he laid his hands upon him and gave him a charge just as Jehovah had spoken through Moses.
Chapter_Header: 28
Verse_Ch: 28:1 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 28:2 你要吩咐以色列人说，献给我的供物，就是献给我作怡爽香气之火祭的食物，你们要谨慎，在所定的日期献给我。 ###EN### Command the children of Israel and say to them, My offering, My food for My offerings by fire of a satisfying fragrance to Me, you shall be careful to present to Me at its appointed time.
Verse_Ch: 28:3 又要对他们说，你们要献给耶和华的火祭，就是没有残疾、一岁的公羊羔，每日两只，作为常献的燔祭。 ###EN### And you shall say to them, This is the offering by fire which you shall present to Jehovah: two male lambs a year old without blemish each day as a continual burnt offering.
Verse_Ch: 28:4 早晨要献一只，黄昏的时候要献一只； ###EN### One lamb you shall offer in the morning, and the other lamb you shall offer at twilight;
Verse_Ch: 28:5 又用细面一伊法的十分之一，并捣成的油一欣的四分之一，调和作为素祭。 ###EN### Also a tenth of an ephah of fine flour for a meal offering, mingled with the fourth of a hin of beaten oil.
Verse_Ch: 28:6 这是在西乃山所定常献的燔祭，作为献给耶和华怡爽香气的火祭。 ###EN### It is a continual burnt offering, which was set up on Mount Sinai for a satisfying fragrance, an offering by fire to Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 28:7 为这一只羊羔，要同献奠祭的酒一欣的四分之一；在圣所中，你要将浓酒奉给耶和华为奠祭。 ###EN### And its drink offering shall be the fourth of a hin for the one lamb; in the sanctuary you shall pour out a drink offering of strong drink to Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 28:8 黄昏的时候，你要献那一只羊羔，必像早晨一样，与素祭和同献的奠祭献上，作为怡爽香气的火祭献给耶和华。 ###EN### And the other lamb you shall offer at twilight; you shall offer it with the meal offering and its drink offering as in the morning, an offering by fire, a satisfying fragrance to Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 28:9 当安息日，要献两只没有残疾、一岁的公羊羔，并用调油的细面一伊法的十分之二为素祭，又将同献的奠祭献上； ###EN### And on the Sabbath day two male lambs a year old without blemish, and two-tenths of an ephah of fine flour for a meal offering, mingled with oil, and its drink offering -
Verse_Ch: 28:10 这是每安息日献的燔祭，是在常献的燔祭和同献的奠祭以外。 ###EN### This is the burnt offering of every Sabbath, besides the continual burnt offering and its drink offering.
Verse_Ch: 28:11 每月朔，你们要将公牛犊两只，公绵羊一只，没有残疾、一岁的公羊羔七只，献给耶和华为燔祭。 ###EN### And at the beginnings of your months you shall present a burnt offering to Jehovah: two bulls of the herd and one ram, seven male lambs a year old without blemish;
Verse_Ch: 28:12 为每只公牛，要献调油的细面一伊法的十分之三为素祭；为那只公羊，也要献调油的细面一伊法的十分之二为素祭； ###EN### And three-tenths of an ephah of fine flour for a meal offering, mingled with oil, for each bull; and two-tenths of an ephah of fine flour for a meal offering, mingled with oil, for the one ram;
Verse_Ch: 28:13 为每只羊羔，要献调油的细面一伊法的十分之一为素祭；这些都是燔祭，是献给耶和华为怡爽香气的火祭。 ###EN### And a tenth of an ephah of fine flour mingled with oil for a meal offering for each lamb for a burnt offering, a satisfying fragrance, an offering by fire to Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 28:14 与这同献的奠祭，为一只公牛要奠酒半欣，为一只公羊要奠酒一欣的三分之一，为一只羊羔也要奠酒一欣的四分之一。这是每月的燔祭，一年之中 要月月如此。 ###EN### And their drink offerings shall be half a hin of wine for a bull, and a third of a hin for the ram, and a fourth of a hin for a lamb. This is the burnt offering of each month throughout the months of the year.
Verse_Ch: 28:15 又要将一只公山羊献给耶和华为赎罪祭，是在常献的燔祭和同献的奠祭以外。 ###EN### Also one male goat for a sin offering to Jehovah shall be offered in addition to the continual burnt offering and its drink offering.
Verse_Ch: 28:16 正月十四日是耶和华的逾越节。 ###EN### And in the first month on the fourteenth day of the month shall be Jehovah's Passover.
Verse_Ch: 28:17 这月十五日是节期，要吃无酵饼七日。 ###EN### And on the fifteenth day of this month shall be a feast; seven days unleavened bread shall be eaten.
Verse_Ch: 28:18 第一日当有圣会；什么劳碌的工都不可作。 ###EN### On the first day there shall be a holy convocation; you shall do no work of labor;
Verse_Ch: 28:19 只要将公牛犊两只，公绵羊一只，一岁的公羊羔七只，都要你们看为没有残疾的，献为火祭，给耶和华为燔祭。 ###EN### But you shall present an offering by fire, a burnt offering to Jehovah: two bulls of the herd and one ram and seven male lambs a year old; they shall be without blemish for you;
Verse_Ch: 28:20 要用调油的细面作同献的素祭；为一只公牛，要献一伊法的十分之三；为一只公羊，要献一伊法的十分之二； ###EN### And you shall offer their meal offering of fine flour mingled with oil: three-tenths of an ephah for a bull and two-tenths for a ram;
Verse_Ch: 28:21 为那七只羊羔，每只要献一伊法的十分之一。 ###EN### You shall offer one-tenth for each lamb of the seven lambs;
Verse_Ch: 28:22 又要献一只公山羊作赎罪祭，为你们遮罪。 ###EN### And one male goat as a sin offering, to make expiation for you.
Verse_Ch: 28:23 你们献这些，要在早晨常献的燔祭以外。 ###EN### You shall offer these besides the burnt offering of the morning, which is for a continual burnt offering.
Verse_Ch: 28:24 一连七日，每日要这样把怡爽香气之火祭的食物献给耶和华，要在常献的燔祭和同献的奠祭以外献上。 ###EN### In this way you shall offer daily, for seven days, the food of the offering by fire, a satisfying fragrance to Jehovah; it shall be offered besides the continual burnt offering and its drink offering.
Verse_Ch: 28:25 第七日你们当有圣会，什么劳碌的工都不可作。 ###EN### And on the seventh day you shall have a holy convocation; you shall do no work of labor.
Verse_Ch: 28:26 在七七节，庄稼初熟，你们献新素祭给耶和华的日子，当有圣会；什么劳碌的工都不可作。 ###EN### Also in the day of the firstfruits, when you present a new meal offering to Jehovah on your Feast of Weeks, you shall have a holy convocation; you shall do no work of labor;
Verse_Ch: 28:27 只要将公牛犊两只，公绵羊一只，一岁的公羊羔七只，作为怡爽香气的燔祭献给耶和华。 ###EN### But you shall present a burnt offering for a satisfying fragrance to Jehovah: two bulls of the herd, one ram, seven male lambs a year old;
Verse_Ch: 28:28 要用调油的细面作同献的素祭；为每只公牛，要献一伊法的十分之三；为一只公羊，要献一伊法的十分之二； ###EN### And their meal offering of fine flour mingled with oil: three-tenths of an ephah for each bull, two-tenths for one ram,
Verse_Ch: 28:29 为那七只羊羔，每只要献一伊法的十分之一。 ###EN### One-tenth for each lamb of the seven lambs;
Verse_Ch: 28:30 又要献一只公山羊，为你们遮罪。 ###EN### And one male goat, to make expiation for you.
Verse_Ch: 28:31 你们在常献的燔祭和同献的素祭以外，要与同献的奠祭献上这些，都要你们看为没有残疾的。 ###EN### Besides the continual burnt offering and its meal offering, you shall offer them (they shall be without blemish for you) and their drink offerings.
Chapter_Header: 29
Verse_Ch: 29:1 七月初一日，你们当有圣会，什么劳碌的工都不可作；这是你们吹角的日子。 ###EN### Now in the seventh month, on the first day of the month, you shall have a holy convocation; you shall do no work of labor. It is a day of blowing of trumpets for you.
Verse_Ch: 29:2 你们要将公牛犊一只，公绵羊一只，没有残疾、一岁的公羊羔七只，作为怡爽香气的燔祭献给耶和华。 ###EN### And you shall offer a burnt offering for a satisfying fragrance to Jehovah: one bull of the herd, one ram, seven male lambs a year old without blemish;
Verse_Ch: 29:3 要用调油的细面作同献的素祭；为那只公牛，要献一伊法的十分之三；为那只公羊，要献一伊法的十分之二； ###EN### And their meal offering of fine flour mingled with oil: three-tenths of an ephah for the bull, two-tenths for the ram,
Verse_Ch: 29:4 为那七只羊羔，每只要献一伊法的十分之一。 ###EN### And one-tenth for each lamb of the seven lambs;
Verse_Ch: 29:5 又要献一只公山羊作赎罪祭，为你们遮罪。 ###EN### And one male goat as a sin offering, to make expiation for you;
Verse_Ch: 29:6 这些是在月朔的燔祭和同献的素祭，并常献的燔祭与同献的素祭，以及照例同献的奠祭以外，作为怡爽香气的火祭献给耶和华。 ###EN### Besides the burnt offering of the new moon and its meal offering, and the continual burnt offering and its meal offering, and their drink offerings, according to their ordinance, for a satisfying fragrance, an offering by fire to Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 29:7 七月初十日，你们当有圣会；要刻苦己心，什么工都不可作。 ###EN### And on the tenth day of this seventh month you shall have a holy convocation, and you shall afflict your souls; you shall not do any work.
Verse_Ch: 29:8 只要将公牛犊一只，公绵羊一只，一岁的公羊羔七只，都要你们看为没有残疾的，作为怡爽香气的燔祭献给耶和华。 ###EN### And you shall present a burnt offering to Jehovah for a satisfying fragrance: one bull of the herd, one ram, seven male lambs a year old; they shall be without blemish for you;
Verse_Ch: 29:9 要用调油的细面作同献的素祭；为那只公牛，要献一伊法的十分之三；为那只公羊，要献一伊法的十分之二， ###EN### And their meal offering of fine flour mingled with oil: three-tenths of an ephah for the bull, two-tenths for the one ram,
Verse_Ch: 29:10 为那七只羊羔，每只要献一伊法的十分之一。 ###EN### One-tenth for each lamb of the seven lambs;
Verse_Ch: 29:11 又要献一只公山羊为赎罪祭。这些是在遮罪的赎罪祭，并常献的燔祭与同献的素祭，以及同献的奠祭以外。 ###EN### One male goat as a sin offering; besides the sin offering of expiation and the continual burnt offering and its meal offering, and their drink offerings.
Verse_Ch: 29:12 七月十五日，你们当有圣会；什么劳碌的工都不可作，要向耶和华守节七日。 ###EN### And on the fifteenth day of the seventh month you shall have a holy convocation; you shall do no work of labor, and you shall hold a feast to Jehovah seven days.
Verse_Ch: 29:13 又要将公牛犊十三只，公绵羊两只，一岁的公羊羔十四只，都要没有残疾的，献为燔祭，给耶和华为怡爽香气的火祭。 ###EN### And you shall present a burnt offering, an offering by fire, a satisfying fragrance to Jehovah: thirteen bulls of the herd, two rams, fourteen male lambs a year old; they shall be without blemish;
Verse_Ch: 29:14 要用调油的细面作同献的素祭；为那十三只公牛，每只要献一伊法的十分之三；为那两只公羊，每只要献一伊法的十分之二； ###EN### And their meal offering of fine flour mingled with oil: three-tenths of an ephah for each bull of the thirteen bulls, two-tenths of an ephah for each ram of the two rams,
Verse_Ch: 29:15 为那十四只羊羔，每只要献一伊法的十分之一。 ###EN### And one-tenth of an ephah for each lamb of the fourteen lambs;
Verse_Ch: 29:16 又要献一只公山羊为赎罪祭。这些是在常献的燔祭和同献的素祭，并同献的奠祭以外。 ###EN### And one male goat for a sin offering; besides the continual burnt offering, its meal offering, and its drink offering.
Verse_Ch: 29:17 第二日要献公牛犊十二只，公绵羊两只，没有残疾、一岁的公羊羔十四只； ###EN### And on the second day: twelve bulls of the herd, two rams, fourteen male lambs a year old without blemish;
Verse_Ch: 29:18 并为公牛、公羊和羊羔，按数照例，献同献的素祭和同献的奠祭。 ###EN### And their meal offering and their drink offerings for the bulls, for the rams, and for the lambs, by their number according to the ordinance;
Verse_Ch: 29:19 又要献一只公山羊为赎罪祭。这些是在常献的燔祭和同献的素祭，并同献的奠祭以外。 ###EN### And one male goat for a sin offering; besides the continual burnt offering and its meal offering, and their drink offerings.
Verse_Ch: 29:20 第三日要献公牛十一只，公羊两只，没有残疾、一岁的公羊羔十四只； ###EN### And on the third day: eleven bulls, two rams, fourteen male lambs a year old without blemish;
Verse_Ch: 29:21 并为公牛、公羊和羊羔，按数照例，献同献的素祭和同献的奠祭。 ###EN### And their meal offering and their drink offerings for the bulls, for the rams, and for the lambs, by their number according to the ordinance;
Verse_Ch: 29:22 又要献一只公山羊为赎罪祭。这些是在常献的燔祭和同献的素祭，并同献的奠祭以外。 ###EN### And one male goat for a sin offering; besides the continual burnt offering and its meal offering and its drink offering.
Verse_Ch: 29:23 第四日要献公牛十只，公羊两只，没有残疾、一岁的公羊羔十四只； ###EN### And on the fourth day: ten bulls, two rams, fourteen male lambs a year old without blemish;
Verse_Ch: 29:24 并为公牛、公羊和羊羔，按数照例，献同献的素祭和同献的奠祭。 ###EN### Their meal offering and their drink offerings for the bulls, for the rams, and for the lambs, by their number according to the ordinance;
Verse_Ch: 29:25 又要献一只公山羊为赎罪祭。这些是在常献的燔祭和同献的素祭，并同献的奠祭以外。 ###EN### And one male goat for a sin offering; besides the continual burnt offering, its meal offering, and its drink offering.
Verse_Ch: 29:26 第五日要献公牛九只，公羊两只，没有残疾、一岁的公羊羔十四只； ###EN### And on the fifth day: nine bulls, two rams, fourteen male lambs a year old without blemish;
Verse_Ch: 29:27 并为公牛、公羊和羊羔，按数照例，献同献的素祭和同献的奠祭。 ###EN### And their meal offering and their drink offerings for the bulls, for the rams, and for the lambs, by their number according to the ordinance;
Verse_Ch: 29:28 又要献一只公山羊为赎罪祭。这些是在常献的燔祭和同献的素祭，并同献的奠祭以外。 ###EN### And one male goat for a sin offering; besides the continual burnt offering and its meal offering and its drink offering.
Verse_Ch: 29:29 第六日要献公牛八只，公羊两只，没有残疾、一岁的公羊羔十四只； ###EN### And on the sixth day: eight bulls, two rams, fourteen male lambs a year old without blemish;
Verse_Ch: 29:30 并为公牛、公羊和羊羔，按数照例，献同献的素祭和同献的奠祭。 ###EN### And their meal offering and their drink offerings for the bulls, for the rams, and for the lambs, by their number according to the ordinance;
Verse_Ch: 29:31 又要献一只公山羊为赎罪祭。这些是在常献的燔祭和同献的素祭，并同献的奠祭以外。 ###EN### And one male goat for a sin offering; besides the continual burnt offering, its meal offering, and its drink offerings.
Verse_Ch: 29:32 第七日要献公牛七只，公羊两只，没有残疾、一岁的公羊羔十四只； ###EN### And on the seventh day: seven bulls, two rams, fourteen male lambs a year old without blemish;
Verse_Ch: 29:33 并为公牛、公羊和羊羔，按数照例，献同献的素祭和同献的奠祭。 ###EN### And their meal offering and their drink offerings for the bulls, for the rams, and for the lambs, by their number according to the ordinance;
Verse_Ch: 29:34 又要献一只公山羊为赎罪祭。这些是在常献的燔祭和同献的素祭，并同献的奠祭以外。 ###EN### And one male goat for a sin offering; besides the continual burnt offering, its meal offering, and its drink offering.
Verse_Ch: 29:35 第八日你们当有严肃会；什么劳碌的工都不可作； ###EN### On the eighth day you shall have a solemn assembly; you shall do no work of labor,
Verse_Ch: 29:36 只要将公牛一只，公羊一只，没有残疾、一岁的公羊羔七只，献为燔祭，给耶和华为怡爽香气的火祭； ###EN### But you shall present a burnt offering, an offering by fire, a satisfying fragrance to Jehovah: one bull, one ram, seven male lambs a year old without blemish;
Verse_Ch: 29:37 并为公牛、公羊和羊羔，按数照例，献同献的素祭和同献的奠祭。 ###EN### Their meal offering and their drink offerings for the bull, for the ram, and for the lambs by their number according to the ordinance;
Verse_Ch: 29:38 又要献一只公山羊为赎罪祭。这些是在常献的燔祭和同献的素祭，并同献的奠祭以外。 ###EN### And one male goat for a sin offering; besides the continual burnt offering and its meal offering and its drink offering.
Verse_Ch: 29:39 这些祭要在你们所定的节期献给耶和华，都在所许的愿并甘心所献的以外，作为你们的燔祭、素祭、奠祭、和平安祭。 ###EN### These you shall offer to Jehovah in your appointed feasts, besides your vows and your freewill offerings, for your burnt offerings and for your meal offerings and for your drink offerings and for your peace offerings.
Verse_Ch: 29:40 于是，摩西照耶和华所吩咐他的一切，告诉以色列人。 ###EN### And Moses spoke to the children of Israel according to all that Jehovah had commanded Moses.
Chapter_Header: 30
Verse_Ch: 30:1 摩西对以色列人各支派的首领说，耶和华所吩咐的乃是这样： ###EN### And Moses spoke to the heads of the tribes of the children of Israel, saying, This is what Jehovah has commanded:
Verse_Ch: 30:2 人若向耶和华许愿，或起誓约束自己，就不可食言，必要按口中所出的一切话行。 ###EN### When a man vows a vow to Jehovah or swears an oath to bind himself by pledge, he shall not break his word; he shall do according to all that proceeds out of his mouth.
Verse_Ch: 30:3 女子年幼还在父家的时候，若向耶和华许愿，或约束自己， ###EN### But when a woman vows a vow to Jehovah or binds herself by pledge in her father's house in her youth,
Verse_Ch: 30:4 她父亲也听见她所许的愿或约束自己的话，却向她默默不言，她所许的愿，并约束自己的话，就都要为定。 ###EN### And her father hears of her vow or her pledge by which she has bound herself, and her father is silent with respect to her; then all her vows will stand, and any pledge by which she has bound herself will stand.
Verse_Ch: 30:5 但她父亲听见的日子若不应承，她所许的愿和约束自己的话，就都不得为定；耶和华也必赦免她，因为她父亲不应承。 ###EN### But if her father disallows her on the day he hears, none of her vows or of her pledges by which she has bound herself will stand; and Jehovah will forgive her because her father disallowed her.
Verse_Ch: 30:6 她若出了嫁，有愿在身，或是口中出了约束自己的冒失话， ###EN### And if she gets married, while her vows are upon her or the rash utterance of her lips by which she has bound herself,
Verse_Ch: 30:7 她丈夫听见的日子，却向她默默不言，她所许的愿，并约束自己的话，就都要为定。 ###EN### And her husband hears of it and is silent with respect to her on the day he hears it, then her vows will stand and her pledges by which she has bound herself will stand.
Verse_Ch: 30:8 但她丈夫听见的日子若不应承，就把她身上的愿，和她出口约束自己的冒失话废了；耶和华也必赦免她。 ###EN### But if, on the day her husband hears of it, he disallows her, then he makes void her vow which is upon her and the rash utterance of her lips by which she has bound herself; and Jehovah will forgive her.
Verse_Ch: 30:9 寡妇或是被休的妇人所许的愿，凡她所说约束自己的话，对她都要为定。 ###EN### But the vow of a widow or of a divorced woman, everything by which she has bound herself, will stand against her.
Verse_Ch: 30:10 她若在丈夫家里许了愿，或起了誓约束自己， ###EN### And if she vowed in her husband's house or bound herself by a pledge with an oath,
Verse_Ch: 30:11 丈夫听见，却向她默默不言，也没有不应承，凡她所许的愿，并约束自己的话，就都要为定。 ###EN### And her husband heard of it and was silent with respect to her and did not disallow her, then all her vows will stand and any pledge by which she has bound herself will stand.
Verse_Ch: 30:12 丈夫听见的日子，若把这两样全废了，从那妇人口中所出，许愿的话和约束自己的话，就都不得为定；她丈夫已经把这两样废了，耶和华也必赦免 她。 ###EN### But if her husband made them null and void on the day he heard of it, then whatever proceeded out of her lips concerning her vows or concerning the pledging of herself will not stand; her husband has made them void, and Jehovah will forgive her.
Verse_Ch: 30:13 凡她所许的愿，和她为刻苦己心，所起约束自己的誓，她丈夫可以坚定，也可以废去。 ###EN### As for every vow and every binding oath to afflict herself, her husband may establish it or her husband may make it void.
Verse_Ch: 30:14 倘若她丈夫天天向她默默不言，就是坚定她一切所许的愿，和一切约束自己的话；丈夫听见的日子既向她默默不言，就使这两样坚定。 ###EN### But if her husband is completely silent with respect to her from day to day, then he establishes all her vows or all her pledges which are upon her; he has established them because he was silent with respect to her on the day he heard it.
Verse_Ch: 30:15 但她丈夫听见以后，若是过了一些时日才把这两样全废了，他就要担当妇人的罪孽。 ###EN### But if he makes them null and void some time after he has heard of it, then he shall bear her iniquity.
Verse_Ch: 30:16 这些是关于丈夫和妻子，父亲和年幼还在父家的女儿，耶和华所吩咐摩西的律例。 ###EN### These are the statutes which Jehovah commanded Moses, between a man and his wife, and between a father and his daughter while in her youth in her father's house.
Chapter_Header: 31
Verse_Ch: 31:1 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 31:2 你要在米甸人身上报以色列人的仇，然后归到你本民那里。 ###EN### Thoroughly avenge the children of Israel of the Midianites; afterward you will be gathered to your people.
Verse_Ch: 31:3 摩西对百姓说，要从你们中间叫人带兵器出去打仗，攻击米甸，好在米甸人身上为耶和华报仇。 ###EN### And Moses spoke to the people, saying, Arm men from among you for the war, that they may come upon Midian to execute Jehovah's vengeance on Midian.
Verse_Ch: 31:4 从以色列众支派中，每支派要打发一千人去打仗。 ###EN### A thousand from each tribe, of all the tribes of Israel, you shall send to the war.
Verse_Ch: 31:5 于是从以色列千万人中，每支派交出一千人，共一万二千人，带着兵器预备打仗。 ###EN### So out of the thousands of Israel, a thousand for each tribe were committed, twelve thousand armed for war.
Verse_Ch: 31:6 摩西就打发每支派的一千人去打仗，并打发祭司以利亚撒的儿子非尼哈同去；非尼哈手里拿着圣所的器皿和吹大声的号筒。 ###EN### And Moses sent them, a thousand for each tribe, to the war, and Phinehas the son of Eleazar the priest with them, to the war, with the vessels of the sanctuary and the trumpets for the alarm in his hand.
Verse_Ch: 31:7 他们就照耶和华所吩咐摩西的，与米甸人打仗，杀了所有的男丁。 ###EN### And they warred against Midian, just as Jehovah had commanded Moses; and they killed every male.
Verse_Ch: 31:8 在所杀的人以外，还杀了米甸的五王，就是以未、利金、苏珥、户珥、利巴，又用刀杀了比珥的儿子巴兰。 ###EN### And they killed the kings of Midian in addition to the others slain among them: Evi and Rekem and Zur and Hur and Reba, the five kings of Midian; also Balaam the son of Beor they slew with the sword.
Verse_Ch: 31:9 以色列人掳了米甸人的妇女孩子，掠夺了他们所有的牲畜、羊群和财物， ###EN### And the children of Israel took captive the women of Midian and their little ones, and all their cattle and all their livestock and all their goods they plundered.
Verse_Ch: 31:10 又用火焚烧他们所住的城邑和所有的营寨， ###EN### And all their cities in which they had settled and all their encampments, they burned with fire.
Verse_Ch: 31:11 把一切所掠的、所获的，连人带牲畜都带了去， ###EN### And they took all the spoil and all the booty, both of man and of beast.
Verse_Ch: 31:12 将所掳的人，并所获、所掠的牲畜、财物，都带到摩押平原，在约但河边与耶利哥相对的营盘，交给摩西和祭司以利亚撒，并以色列人的会众。 ###EN### And they brought the captives and the booty and the spoil to Moses and to Eleazar the priest and to the assembly of the children of Israel, to the camp in the plains of Moab, which was beside the Jordan at Jericho.
Verse_Ch: 31:13 摩西和祭司以利亚撒，并会众一切的首领，都出到营外迎接他们。 ###EN### And Moses and Eleazar the priest and all the leaders of the assembly went out to meet them outside the camp.
Verse_Ch: 31:14 摩西向打仗回来的军长，就是千夫长、百夫长，发怒， ###EN### And Moses became angry with the officers of the company, the captains of thousands and the captains of hundreds, who came from service in the war.
Verse_Ch: 31:15 对他们说，你们要让这一切妇女存活么？ ###EN### And Moses said to them, Have you kept all the women alive?
Verse_Ch: 31:16 这些妇女因巴兰的计谋，叫以色列人在毗珥的事上，对耶和华行事不忠实，以致瘟疫临到耶和华的会众。 ###EN### It was these who caused the children of Israel, through the counsel of Balaam, to act unfaithfully against Jehovah in the matter of Peor, so that the plague came upon the assembly of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 31:17 所以，你们要把一切的男孩和所有已嫁的女子都杀了。 ###EN### Now therefore kill every male among the little ones, and kill every woman who has known a man by lying with him.
Verse_Ch: 31:18 但女孩子中，凡没有出嫁的，可以让她们存活，归给你们。 ###EN### But all the little ones among the women, who have not known a male by lying with him, keep alive for yourselves.
Verse_Ch: 31:19 你们要在营外驻扎七日；凡杀了人的，和一切触了被杀的，并你们所掳来的人口，都要在第三日和第七日洁净自己； ###EN### And you, encamp outside the camp seven days, everyone who has killed any person and everyone who has touched any slain; purify yourselves on the third day and on the seventh day, you and your captives.
Verse_Ch: 31:20 也要为自己洁净一切的衣服、皮物、山羊毛织的物、和各样的木器。 ###EN### And you shall purify for yourselves every garment and every article of skin and everything made of goats' hair and every article of wood.
Verse_Ch: 31:21 祭司以利亚撒对打仗回来的兵丁说，耶和华所吩咐摩西律法中的律例乃是这样： ###EN### And Eleazar the priest said to the men of war who had gone to the battle, This is the statute of the law which Jehovah has commanded Moses:
Verse_Ch: 31:22 金、银、铜、铁、锡、铅， ###EN### Only the gold and the silver, the bronze, the iron, the tin, and the lead,
Verse_Ch: 31:23 凡能见火的，你们要叫它经火，就洁净了，然而还要用除污秽的水洁净它；凡不能见火的，你们要叫它过水。 ###EN### Everything that can go into the fire, you shall pass through the fire, and it will become clean; but it shall be purified with the water for impurity; and everything that cannot go into the fire you shall pass through the water.
Verse_Ch: 31:24 第七日，你们要洗衣服，就为洁净，然后可以进营。 ###EN### And you shall wash your clothes on the seventh day, and you shall be clean; and afterward you may come into the camp.
Verse_Ch: 31:25 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 31:26 你和祭司以利亚撒，并会众各宗族的族长，要计算所掳获的人口和牲畜的总数； ###EN### You and Eleazar the priest and the heads of the fathers' households of the assembly, take the sum of the booty that was captured, both of man and of beast,
Verse_Ch: 31:27 把所获的分作两半，一半归与出去打仗的精兵，一半归与全会众。 ###EN### And halve the booty between those skilled in war who went out to battle and the whole assembly.
Verse_Ch: 31:28 又要从出去打仗的兵丁所得的人口、牛、驴、羊群中，每五百取一，作为贡物奉给耶和华； ###EN### And levy a tribute to Jehovah from the men of war who went out to battle: one living thing out of five hundred, of the persons and of the cattle and of the donkeys and of the flock;
Verse_Ch: 31:29 从他们所得的这一半之中，取出来交给祭司以利亚撒，作为耶和华的举祭。 ###EN### Take it from their half and give it to Eleazar the priest, for Jehovah's heave offering.
Verse_Ch: 31:30 从以色列人所得的那一半之中，就是从人口、牛、驴、羊群、各样牲畜中，每五十取一，交给看守耶和华帐幕的利未人。 ###EN### And of the children of Israel's half, you shall take one seized out of fifty, of the persons, of the cattle, of the donkeys, and of the flocks, from all the beasts, and give them to the Levites, who keep the charge of the tabernacle of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 31:31 于是摩西和祭司以利亚撒照耶和华所吩咐摩西的行了。 ###EN### And Moses and Eleazar the priest did just as Jehovah commanded Moses.
Verse_Ch: 31:32 兵丁所获的，就是他们所掠得、还留存的，有羊六十七万五千只， ###EN### Now the booty that was left from the spoil which the men of war took was six hundred seventy-five thousand sheep,
Verse_Ch: 31:33 牛七万二千只， ###EN### And seventy-two thousand cattle,
Verse_Ch: 31:34 驴六万一千匹， ###EN### And sixty-one thousand donkeys,
Verse_Ch: 31:35 女人共三万二千口，都是没有出嫁的。 ###EN### And thirty-two thousand persons in all, the women who had not known lying with a male.
Verse_Ch: 31:36 出去打仗之人的分，就是他们所得的那一半，共计羊三十三万七千五百只， ###EN### And the half, which was the portion of those who went out to war, was in number three hundred thirty-seven thousand five hundred sheep.
Verse_Ch: 31:37 从其中归耶和华为贡物的，有六百七十五只； ###EN### And Jehovah's tribute of the sheep was six hundred seventy-five.
Verse_Ch: 31:38 牛三万六千只，从其中归耶和华为贡物的，有七十二只； ###EN### And the cattle were thirty-six thousand, of which Jehovah's tribute was seventy-two.
Verse_Ch: 31:39 驴三万零五百匹，从其中归耶和华为贡物的，有六十一匹； ###EN### And the donkeys were thirty thousand five hundred, of which Jehovah's tribute was sixty-one.
Verse_Ch: 31:40 人一万六千口，从其中归耶和华为贡物的，有三十二口。 ###EN### And the human beings were sixteen thousand, of whom Jehovah's tribute was thirty-two persons.
Verse_Ch: 31:41 摩西把贡物，就是耶和华的举祭，交给祭司以利亚撒，是照耶和华所吩咐摩西的。 ###EN### And Moses gave the tribute, Jehovah's heave offering, to Eleazar the priest, just as Jehovah had commanded Moses.
Verse_Ch: 31:42 以色列人所得的那一半，就是摩西从打仗的人取来分给他们的， ###EN### And of the children of Israel's half, which Moses had separated from the men who had gone to war -
Verse_Ch: 31:43 (会众所得的那一半，有羊三十三万七千五百只， ###EN### That is, the assembly's half was three hundred thirty-seven thousand five hundred sheep,
Verse_Ch: 31:44 牛三万六千只， ###EN### And thirty-six thousand cattle,
Verse_Ch: 31:45 驴三万零五百匹， ###EN### And thirty thousand five hundred donkeys,
Verse_Ch: 31:46 人一万六千口，) ###EN### And sixteen thousand persons -
Verse_Ch: 31:47 从以色列人所得的那一半之中，无论是人口或是牲畜，摩西每五十取一，交给看守耶和华帐幕的利未人，正如耶和华所吩咐摩西的。 ###EN### Now Moses took from the children of Israel's half, one drawn out of every fifty, both of man and of beast, and gave them to the Levites, who kept the charge of the tabernacle of Jehovah, just as Jehovah had commanded Moses.
Verse_Ch: 31:48 统领千军的各军长，就是千夫长、百夫长，都近前来见摩西， ###EN### And the officers who were over the thousands of the army, the captains of thousands and the captains of hundreds, approached Moses.
Verse_Ch: 31:49 对他说，仆人权下的兵已经计算总数，并不短少一人。 ###EN### And they said to Moses, Your servants have taken the sum of the men of war who are under our charge, and not a man is missing from us;
Verse_Ch: 31:50 如今我们将各人所得的金器，就是臂环、手镯、打印的戒指、耳环、项链，都送来为耶和华的供物，好在耶和华面前为我们的性命遮罪。 ###EN### And we have presented Jehovah's offering, what every man has obtained, articles of gold, armlets and bracelets, signet rings, earrings and pendants, to make expiation for our souls before Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 31:51 摩西和祭司以利亚撒就从他们收了金子，都是各样打成的物件。 ###EN### And Moses and Eleazar the priest took the gold from them, all kinds of wrought articles.
Verse_Ch: 31:52 千夫长、百夫长所献给耶和华为举祭的金子，共有一万六千七百五十舍客勒。 ###EN### And all the gold of the heave offering which they offered up to Jehovah, from the captains of thousands and from the captains of hundreds, was sixteen thousand seven hundred fifty shekels.
Verse_Ch: 31:53 各兵丁都为自己获得了财物。 ###EN### The men of war had taken booty, each for himself.
Verse_Ch: 31:54 摩西和祭司以利亚撒从千夫长、百夫长收了金子，就带进会幕，在耶和华面前作为以色列人的记念。 ###EN### So Moses and Eleazar the priest took the gold from the captains of thousands and of hundreds, and brought it into the Tent of Meeting as a memorial for the children of Israel before Jehovah.
Chapter_Header: 32
Verse_Ch: 32:1 流便子孙和迦得子孙的牲畜极其众多；他们看见雅谢地和基列地是可牧放牲畜之地， ###EN### Now the children of Reuben and the children of Gad had a very great abundance of livestock. And when they saw the land of Jazer and the land of Gilead, that the place was indeed a place for livestock,
Verse_Ch: 32:2 就来见摩西和祭司以利亚撒，并会众的首领，说， ###EN### The children of Gad and the children of Reuben came and spoke to Moses and to Eleazar the priest and to the leaders of the assembly, saying,
Verse_Ch: 32:3 亚大录、底本、雅谢、宁拉、希实本、以利亚利、示班、尼波、比稳， ###EN### Ataroth and Dibon and Jazer and Nimrah and Heshbon and Elealeh and Sebam and Nebo and Beon,
Verse_Ch: 32:4 就是耶和华在以色列会众前面所攻取之地，是可牧放牲畜之地，你仆人也有牲畜； ###EN### The land which Jehovah struck before the assembly of Israel, is a land for livestock, and your servants have livestock.
Verse_Ch: 32:5 又说，我们若在你眼前蒙恩，求你把这地给你仆人为业，不要叫我们过约但河。 ###EN### And they said, If we have found favor in your sight, let this land be given to your servants for a possession; do not make us cross over the Jordan.
Verse_Ch: 32:6 摩西对迦得子孙和流便子孙说，难道你们的弟兄去打仗，你们竟坐在这里么？ ###EN### And Moses said to the children of Gad and to the children of Reuben, Shall your brothers go to war, while you stay here?
Verse_Ch: 32:7 你们为何使以色列人灰心丧胆，不过去进入耶和华所赐给他们的那地呢？ ###EN### Now why would you discourage the heart of the children of Israel from crossing over into the land which Jehovah has given them?
Verse_Ch: 32:8 我先前从加低斯巴尼亚打发你们先祖去看那地，那时他们也是这样行。 ###EN### Your fathers did this when I sent them from Kadesh-barnea to see the land.
Verse_Ch: 32:9 他们上到以实各谷，看了那地之后，使以色列人灰心丧胆，不进入耶和华所赐给他们的地。 ###EN### When they went up to the valley of Eshcol and saw the land, they discouraged the heart of the children of Israel from going into the land which Jehovah had given them.
Verse_Ch: 32:10 当日耶和华的怒气发作，就起誓说， ###EN### And Jehovah's anger was kindled in that day, and He swore, saying,
Verse_Ch: 32:11 凡从埃及上来，二十岁以上的人，断不得看见我所起誓要赐给亚伯拉罕、以撒、雅各之地，因为他们没有专心跟从我。 ###EN### Surely none of the men who came up out of Egypt, from twenty years old and upward, shall see the land which I swore to give to Abraham, to Isaac, and to Jacob, because they have not fully followed Me;
Verse_Ch: 32:12 惟有基尼洗人耶孚尼的儿子迦勒，和嫩的儿子约书亚可以看见，因为他们专心跟从耶和华。 ###EN### Except Caleb the son of Jephunneh the Kenizzite and Joshua the son of Nun, because they have fully followed Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 32:13 耶和华的怒气向以色列人发作，使他们在旷野飘流四十年，直到在耶和华眼前行恶的那一代人都消灭了。 ###EN### And Jehovah's anger was kindled against Israel, and He made them wander in the wilderness forty years, until the whole generation which had done evil in the sight of Jehovah was consumed.
Verse_Ch: 32:14 谁知，你们这些罪人的种类起来接替先祖，使耶和华向以色列的烈怒越发加增。 ###EN### And now you have risen up in your fathers' place, a brood of sinful men, to further increase the burning anger of Jehovah toward Israel.
Verse_Ch: 32:15 你们若转离不跟从祂，祂就要再把以色列人撇在旷野；你们便使这众民全都灭亡。 ###EN### For if you turn away from following Him, He will yet again leave them in the wilderness; and you will destroy this entire people.
Verse_Ch: 32:16 两支派的人挨近摩西，说，我们要在这里为牲畜垒圈，为妇人孩子造城； ###EN### And they came near to him and said, We will build sheepfolds here for our livestock and cities for our little ones;
Verse_Ch: 32:17 我们自己要备妥兵器，行在以色列人的前头，直到把他们领到他们的地方；但我们的妇人孩子，因这地居民的缘故，要住在坚固的城内。 ###EN### But we ourselves will be armed and ready to go before the children of Israel until we have brought them to their place, while our little ones dwell in the fortified cities because of the inhabitants of the land.
Verse_Ch: 32:18 我们不回家，直等到以色列人各自承受了产业。 ###EN### We will not return to our houses until each one of the children of Israel has inherited his inheritance.
Verse_Ch: 32:19 我们不和他们在约但河那边一带之地同受产业，因为给我们的产业是在约但河东边这里。 ###EN### For we will not inherit with them on the other side of the Jordan and further on, because our inheritance has come to us on this side of the Jordan eastward.
Verse_Ch: 32:20 摩西对他们说，你们若这样行，在耶和华面前带着兵器出去打仗， ###EN### And Moses said to them, If you will do this thing, if you will arm yourselves before Jehovah for war,
Verse_Ch: 32:21 所有带兵器的人都要在耶和华面前过约但河，直到祂把仇敌从祂面前赶出去， ###EN### And all of your armed men will cross over the Jordan before Jehovah until He has driven out His enemies from before Him,
Verse_Ch: 32:22 那地在耶和华面前被制伏了，然后你们才可以回来，卸下向耶和华和以色列的责任，这地也必在耶和华面前归你们为业。 ###EN### And the land is subdued before Jehovah, then afterward you shall return and be free of obligation toward Jehovah and toward Israel; and this land shall be yours for a possession before Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 32:23 倘若你们不这样行，就得罪耶和华，要知道你们的罪必追上你们。 ###EN### But if you will not do so, then you have sinned against Jehovah; and know that your sin will find you out.
Verse_Ch: 32:24 如今你们口中所出的，只管去行，为你们的妇人孩子造城，为你们的羊群垒圈。 ###EN### Build for yourselves cities for your little ones and folds for your sheep, and do what has proceeded out of your mouth.
Verse_Ch: 32:25 迦得子孙和流便子孙对摩西说，仆人必照我主所吩咐的去行。 ###EN### And the children of Gad and the children of Reuben spoke to Moses, saying, Your servants will do as my lord commands.
Verse_Ch: 32:26 我们的孩子、妻子、羊群、和所有的牲畜，都要留在基列的各城； ###EN### Our little ones, our wives, our livestock, and all our cattle will be there in the cities of Gilead;
Verse_Ch: 32:27 但你的仆人，凡带兵器出去打仗的，都要照我主所说的，在耶和华面前过去打仗。 ###EN### But your servants will cross over, everyone who is armed for war before Jehovah to battle, as my lord says.
Verse_Ch: 32:28 于是，摩西为他们嘱咐祭司以利亚撒和嫩的儿子约书亚，并以色列众支派宗族的族长， ###EN### So Moses gave command concerning them to Eleazar the priest and to Joshua the son of Nun and to the heads of the fathers' houses of the tribes of the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 32:29 对他们说，迦得子孙和流便子孙，凡带兵器在耶和华面前去打仗的，若与你们一同过约但河，那地在你们面前被制伏了，你们就要把基列地给他们 为业。 ###EN### And Moses said to them, If the children of Gad and the children of Reuben cross over the Jordan with you, everyone who is armed to battle before Jehovah, and the land is subdued before you, then you shall give them the land of Gilead as a possession.
Verse_Ch: 32:30 倘若他们不带兵器和你们一同过去，就要在迦南地你们中间得产业。 ###EN### But if they do not cross over armed with you, they shall have possessions among you in the land of Canaan.
Verse_Ch: 32:31 迦得子孙和流便子孙回答说，耶和华对仆人怎样说，仆人就怎样行。 ###EN### And the children of Gad and the children of Reuben answered, saying, As Jehovah has said to your servants, so will we do.
Verse_Ch: 32:32 我们要带兵器，在耶和华面前过去，进入迦南地，只是在约但河这边，我们所得为业之地仍归我们。 ###EN### We will cross over armed before Jehovah into the land of Canaan, and the possession of our inheritance will remain with us beyond the Jordan.
Verse_Ch: 32:33 摩西将亚摩利王西宏的国和巴珊王噩的国，那地和那地四境的城邑，都给了迦得子孙和流便子孙，并约瑟的儿子玛拿西半个支派。 ###EN### And Moses gave to them, to the children of Gad and to the children of Reuben and to the half-tribe of Manasseh the son of Joseph, the kingdom of Sihon the king of the Amorites and the kingdom of Og the king of Bashan, the land according to its cities with their territories, the cities of the surrounding land.
Verse_Ch: 32:34 迦得子孙修建底本、亚他录、亚罗珥、 ###EN### And the children of Gad built Dibon and Ataroth and Aroer
Verse_Ch: 32:35 亚他录朔反、雅谢、约比哈、 ###EN### And Atroth-shophan and Jazer and Jogbehah
Verse_Ch: 32:36 伯宁拉、伯哈兰，都是坚固城；他们又垒羊圈。 ###EN### And Beth-nimrah and Beth-haran as fortified cities, and folds for sheep.
Verse_Ch: 32:37 流便子孙修建希实本、以利亚利、基列亭、 ###EN### And the children of Reuben built Heshbon and Elealeh and Kiriathaim
Verse_Ch: 32:38 尼波、巴力免(这些名字是改了的、)西比玛，并给他们所修建的城起了别的名字。 ###EN### And Nebo and Baal-meon-their names to be changed-and Sibmah, and they gave other names to the cities which they built.
Verse_Ch: 32:39 玛拿西的儿子玛吉，他的子孙往基列去，占了那地，赶出那里的亚摩利人。 ###EN### And the children of Machir the son of Manasseh went to Gilead and took it and dispossessed the Amorites who were in it.
Verse_Ch: 32:40 摩西将基列赐给玛拿西的儿子玛吉，他的子孙就住在那里。 ###EN### And Moses gave Gilead to Machir the son of Manasseh, and he dwelt in it.
Verse_Ch: 32:41 玛拿西的子孙睚珥去占了亚摩利人的村落，就称这些村落为哈倭特睚珥。 ###EN### And Jair the son of Manasseh went and took its villages and called them Havvoth-jair.
Verse_Ch: 32:42 挪巴去占了基纳和基纳的乡村，就按自己的名称基纳为挪巴。 ###EN### And Nobah went and took Kenath and its towns, and called it Nobah after his own name.
Chapter_Header: 33
Verse_Ch: 33:1 以色列人按着军队，在摩西、亚伦的手下出埃及地所行的路程，记在下面。 ###EN### These are the journeys of the children of Israel, when they went forth out of the land of Egypt by their companies under the direction of Moses and Aaron.
Verse_Ch: 33:2 摩西照着耶和华的吩咐记下他们所行路程中的出发地，他们按着出发地所经过的站口如下： ###EN### And Moses wrote down the places that they went out from for their journeys according to the commandment of Jehovah; and these are their stages according to the places they went out from.
Verse_Ch: 33:3 正月十五日，就是逾越节的次日，以色列人从兰塞起行，在所有的埃及人眼前昂然无惧的出去。 ###EN### Now they journeyed from Rameses in the first month, on the fifteenth day of the first month; on the day after the Passover the children of Israel went out with a high hand in the sight of all the Egyptians,
Verse_Ch: 33:4 那时，埃及人正葬埋他们所有的长子，就是耶和华在他们中间所击杀的；耶和华也对他们的神施行了审判。 ###EN### While the Egyptians were burying those whom Jehovah had struck down among them, all their firstborn; on their gods Jehovah also executed judgments.
Verse_Ch: 33:5 以色列人从兰塞起行，安营在疏割。 ###EN### And the children of Israel journeyed from Rameses and encamped at Succoth.
Verse_Ch: 33:6 从疏割起行，安营在旷野边的以倘。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Succoth and encamped at Etham, which is at the edge of the wilderness.
Verse_Ch: 33:7 从以倘起行，转回到巴力洗分对面的比哈希录，就在密夺前面安营。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Etham and turned back to Pi-hahiroth, which faces Baal-zephon; and they encamped before Migdol.
Verse_Ch: 33:8 从比哈希录起行，经过海中，进到书珥的旷野，又在伊坦的旷野走了三天的路程，就安营在玛拉。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Pi-hahiroth and passed through the midst of the sea into the wilderness, and they went three days' journey in the wilderness of Etham and encamped at Marah.
Verse_Ch: 33:9 从玛拉起行，来到以琳；在以琳有十二股水泉，七十棵棕树；他们就在那里安营。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Marah and came to Elim. And in Elim there were twelve springs of water and seventy palm trees, and they encamped there.
Verse_Ch: 33:10 从以琳起行，安营在红海边。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Elim and encamped by the Red Sea.
Verse_Ch: 33:11 从红海边起行，安营在汛的旷野。 ###EN### And they journeyed from the Red Sea and encamped in the wilderness of Sin.
Verse_Ch: 33:12 从汛的旷野起行，安营在脱加。 ###EN### And they journeyed from the wilderness of Sin and encamped at Dophkah.
Verse_Ch: 33:13 从脱加起行，安营在亚录。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Dophkah and encamped at Alush.
Verse_Ch: 33:14 从亚录起行，安营在利非订；在那里，百姓没有水喝。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Alush and encamped at Rephidim, and there was no water for the people to drink there.
Verse_Ch: 33:15 从利非订起行，安营在西乃的旷野。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Rephidim and encamped in the wilderness of Sinai.
Verse_Ch: 33:16 从西乃的旷野起行，安营在基博罗哈他瓦。 ###EN### And they journeyed from the wilderness of Sinai and encamped at Kibroth- hattaavah.
Verse_Ch: 33:17 从基博罗哈他瓦起行，安营在哈洗录。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Kibroth- hattaavah and encamped at Hazeroth.
Verse_Ch: 33:18 从哈洗录起行，安营在利提玛。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Hazeroth and encamped at Rithmah.
Verse_Ch: 33:19 从利提玛起行，安营在临门帕烈。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Rithmah and encamped at Rimmon-perez.
Verse_Ch: 33:20 从临门帕烈起行，安营在立拿。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Rimmon- perez and encamped at Libnah.
Verse_Ch: 33:21 从立拿起行，安营在勒撒。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Libnah and encamped at Rissah.
Verse_Ch: 33:22 从勒撒起行，安营在基希拉他。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Rissah and encamped at Kehelathah.
Verse_Ch: 33:23 从基希拉他起行，安营在沙斐山。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Kehelathah and encamped at Mount Shepher.
Verse_Ch: 33:24 从沙斐山起行，安营在哈拉大。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Mount Shepher and encamped at Haradah.
Verse_Ch: 33:25 从哈拉大起行，安营在玛吉希录。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Haradah and encamped at Makheloth.
Verse_Ch: 33:26 从玛吉希录起行，安营在他哈。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Makheloth and encamped at Tahath.
Verse_Ch: 33:27 从他哈起行，安营在他拉。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Tahath and encamped at Terah.
Verse_Ch: 33:28 从他拉起行，安营在密加。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Terah and encamped at Mithkah.
Verse_Ch: 33:29 从密加起行，安营在哈摩拿。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Mithkah and encamped at Hashmonah.
Verse_Ch: 33:30 从哈摩拿起行，安营在摩西录。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Hashmonah and encamped at Moseroth.
Verse_Ch: 33:31 从摩西录起行，安营在比尼亚干。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Moseroth and encamped at Bene-jaakan.
Verse_Ch: 33:32 从比尼亚干起行，安营在曷哈及甲。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Bene- jaakan and encamped at Hor-haggidgad.
Verse_Ch: 33:33 从曷哈及甲起行，安营在约巴他。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Hor- haggidgad and encamped at Jotbathah.
Verse_Ch: 33:34 从约巴他起行，安营在阿博拿。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Jotbathah and encamped at Abronah.
Verse_Ch: 33:35 从阿博拿起行，安营在以旬迦别。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Abronah and encamped at Ezion-geber.
Verse_Ch: 33:36 从以旬迦别起行，安营在寻的旷野，加低斯那里。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Ezion- geber and encamped in the wilderness of Zin, that is, Kadesh.
Verse_Ch: 33:37 从加低斯起行，安营在以东地边缘的何珥山。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Kadesh and encamped in Mount Hor at the edge of the land of Edom.
Verse_Ch: 33:38 以色列人出了埃及地后四十年，五月初一日，祭司亚伦照着耶和华的吩咐上了何珥山，死在那里。 ###EN### And Aaron the priest went up onto Mount Hor at the commandment of Jehovah and died there in the fortieth year after the children of Israel had come out of the land of Egypt, in the fifth month, on the first day of the month.
Verse_Ch: 33:39 亚伦死在何珥山的时候，年一百二十三岁。 ###EN### And Aaron was one hundred twenty- three years old when he died on Mount Hor.
Verse_Ch: 33:40 住在迦南南地的迦南人亚拉得王，听说以色列人来了。 ###EN### And the Canaanite, the king of Arad, who was dwelling in the Negev in the land of Canaan, heard of the coming of the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 33:41 以色列人从何珥山起行，安营在撒摩拿。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Mount Hor and encamped at Zalmonah.
Verse_Ch: 33:42 从撒摩拿起行，安营在普嫩。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Zalmonah and encamped at Punon.
Verse_Ch: 33:43 从普嫩起行，安营在阿伯。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Punon and encamped at Oboth.
Verse_Ch: 33:44 从阿伯起行，安营在摩押边界的以耶亚巴琳。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Oboth and encamped at Iye-abarim on the border of Moab.
Verse_Ch: 33:45 从以耶亚巴琳起行，安营在底本迦得。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Iyim and encamped at Dibon-gad.
Verse_Ch: 33:46 从底本迦得起行，安营在亚门低比拉太音。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Dibon-gad and encamped in Almon-diblathaim.
Verse_Ch: 33:47 从亚门低比拉太音起行，安营在尼波对面的亚巴琳山里。 ###EN### And they journeyed from Almon- diblathaim and encamped in the mountains of the Abarim before Nebo.
Verse_Ch: 33:48 从亚巴琳山起行，安营在摩押平原与耶利哥相对的约但河边。 ###EN### And they journeyed from the mountains of the Abarim and encamped in the plains of Moab beside the Jordan at Jericho.
Verse_Ch: 33:49 他们在摩押平原沿约但河边安营，从伯耶施末直到亚伯什亭。 ###EN### And they encamped beside the Jordan from Beth-jeshimoth as far as Abel- shittim in the plains of Moab.
Verse_Ch: 33:50 耶和华在摩押平原与耶利哥相对的约但河边，对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses in the plains of Moab by the Jordan at Jericho, saying,
Verse_Ch: 33:51 你要对以色列人说，你们过约但河进迦南地的时候， ###EN### Speak to the children of Israel, and say to them, When you pass over the Jordan into the land of Canaan,
Verse_Ch: 33:52 要从你们面前赶出那地所有的居民，毁灭他们一切錾成的石像，和他们一切铸成的神像，又拆毁他们一切的邱坛。 ###EN### You shall drive out all the inhabitants of the land from before you, and you shall destroy all their figured stones and destroy all their molten images and demolish all their high places;
Verse_Ch: 33:53 你们要夺取那地，住在其中，因我已经把那地赐给你们为业。 ###EN### And you shall take possession of the land and dwell in it, for to you I have given the land to possess it.
Verse_Ch: 33:54 你们要按家族拈阄，承受那地；人数多的，要把产业多分给他们；人数少的，要把产业少分给他们。拈出何地给何人，就要归何人。你们要按祖宗 的支派承受。 ###EN### And you shall inherit the land by lot according to your families; to the larger you shall give a larger inheritance, and to the smaller you shall give a smaller inheritance. Wherever the lot falls to anyone, that shall be his. You shall inherit according to the tribes of your fathers.
Verse_Ch: 33:55 倘若你们不把那地的居民从你们面前赶出去，所容让存留的居民必要成为你们眼中的刺，肋下的荆棘，也必在你们所住的地上扰害你们。 ###EN### But if you do not drive out the inhabitants of the land from before you, then those whom you let remain of them will become as splinters in your eyes and as thorns in your sides, and they will trouble you in the land in which you are dwelling.
Verse_Ch: 33:56 而且我定意怎样待他们，也必照样待你们。 ###EN### And just as I thought to do to them, so will I do to you.
Chapter_Header: 34
Verse_Ch: 34:1 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 34:2 你吩咐以色列人说，你们进了迦南地，就是归你们为业的地，这迦南地边界以内之地如下： ###EN### Command the children of Israel and say to them, When you come into the land of Canaan, this is the land that shall fall to you for an inheritance, the land of Canaan according to its borders.
Verse_Ch: 34:3 南面的地区要从寻的旷野，贴着以东的边界；南界东端要从盐海尽头起， ###EN### And your southern section shall be from the wilderness of Zin along the side of Edom, and your southern border shall begin from the end of the Salt Sea on the east.
Verse_Ch: 34:4 绕到亚克拉滨坡的南边，接连到寻，直通到加低斯巴尼亚的南边，又通到哈萨亚达，接连到押们， ###EN### And your border shall turn about south to the ascent of Akrabbim and pass on to Zin, and it shall go out to the south of Kadesh-barnea, even going out to Hazar-addar; then it shall pass on to Azmon.
Verse_Ch: 34:5 从押们转到埃及小河，直通到海为止。 ###EN### Then the border shall turn from Azmon to the brook of Egypt, and it shall go out to the sea.
Verse_Ch: 34:6 西边要以大海为界；这要作你们的西界。 ###EN### And for the western border you shall have the Great Sea and its coast; this shall be your western border.
Verse_Ch: 34:7 北界要从大海起，画到何珥山， ###EN### And this shall be your northern border: From the Great Sea you shall mark out a line for yourselves to Mount Hor.
Verse_Ch: 34:8 从何珥山画到哈马口，通到西达达， ###EN### From Mount Hor you shall mark out a line to the entrance of Hamath; and the border shall go out to Zedad;
Verse_Ch: 34:9 又通到西斐仑，直通到哈萨以难为止；这要作你们的北界。 ###EN### And the border shall go out to Ziphron, and it shall go out to Hazar-enan. This shall be your northern border.
Verse_Ch: 34:10 你们要从哈萨以难画到示番为东界； ###EN### And you shall mark out your eastern border from Hazar-enan to Shepham;
Verse_Ch: 34:11 这界要从示番下到亚延东边的利比拉，再往下达到基尼烈湖的东坡， ###EN### And the border shall go down from Shepham to Riblah on the east side of Ain; and the border shall go down and reach the slope on the east of the Sea of Chinnereth;
Verse_Ch: 34:12 再下到约但河，通到盐海为止。这四围的边界以内，要作你们的地。 ###EN### And the border shall go down to the Jordan, and it shall go out to the Salt Sea. This shall be your land according to its borders all around.
Verse_Ch: 34:13 摩西吩咐以色列人说，这地就是耶和华所吩咐，要给九个半支派拈阄承受为业的； ###EN### And Moses commanded the children of Israel, saying, This is the land which you shall inherit by lot, which Jehovah has commanded to give to the nine tribes and to the half-tribe.
Verse_Ch: 34:14 因为流便支派和迦得支派按着宗族受了产业，玛拿西半个支派也受了产业。 ###EN### For the tribe of the children of Reuben according to their fathers' households and the tribe of the children of Gad according to their fathers' households and the half-tribe of Manasseh have received their inheritance.
Verse_Ch: 34:15 这两个半支派已经在耶利哥对面、约但河东、向日出之地受了产业。 ###EN### The two tribes and the half-tribe have received their inheritance beyond the Jordan at Jericho eastward, toward the sunrise.
Verse_Ch: 34:16 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 34:17 要给你们分地为业之人的名字是：祭司以利亚撒和嫩的儿子约书亚。 ###EN### These are the names of the men who shall divide the land to you for inheritance: Eleazar the priest and Joshua the son of Nun.
Verse_Ch: 34:18 你们要从每支派中选取一个首领，帮助他们将地分给你们为业。 ###EN### And you shall take one leader from each tribe to divide the land for inheritance.
Verse_Ch: 34:19 这些人的名字如下：犹大支派有耶孚尼的儿子迦勒； ###EN### And these are the names of the men: For the tribe of Judah, Caleb the son of Jephunneh.
Verse_Ch: 34:20 西缅支派有亚米忽的儿子示母利； ###EN### And for the tribe of the children of Simeon, Shemuel the son of Ammihud.
Verse_Ch: 34:21 便雅悯支派有基斯伦的儿子以利达； ###EN### For the tribe of Benjamin, Elidad the son of Chislon.
Verse_Ch: 34:22 但支派有一个首领，约利的儿子布基； ###EN### And for the tribe of the children of Dan, a leader, Bukki the son of Jogli.
Verse_Ch: 34:23 约瑟的子孙玛拿西支派有一个首领，以弗的儿子汉聂； ###EN### For the children of Joseph: For the tribe of the children of Manasseh, a leader, Hanniel the son of Ephod.
Verse_Ch: 34:24 以法莲支派有一个首领，拾弗但的儿子基母利； ###EN### And for the tribe of the children of Ephraim, a leader, Kemuel the son of Shiphtan.
Verse_Ch: 34:25 西布伦支派有一个首领，帕纳的儿子以利撒番； ###EN### And for the tribe of the children of Zebulun, a leader, Elizaphan the son of Parnach.
Verse_Ch: 34:26 以萨迦支派有一个首领，阿散的儿子帕铁； ###EN### And for the tribe of the children of Issachar, a leader, Paltiel the son of Azzan.
Verse_Ch: 34:27 亚设支派有一个首领，示罗米的儿子亚希忽； ###EN### And for the tribe of the children of Asher, a leader, Ahihud the son of Shelomi.
Verse_Ch: 34:28 拿弗他利支派有一个首领，亚米忽的儿子比大黑。 ###EN### And for the tribe of the children of Naphtali, a leader, Pedahel the son of Ammihud.
Verse_Ch: 34:29 这些人就是耶和华所吩咐，在迦南地把产业分给以色列人的。 ###EN### These are those whom Jehovah commanded to divide the inheritance to the children of Israel in the land of Canaan.
Chapter_Header: 35
Verse_Ch: 35:1 耶和华在摩押平原与耶利哥相对的约但河边，对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses in the plains of Moab by the Jordan at Jericho, saying,
Verse_Ch: 35:2 你吩咐以色列人，要从所得为业的地中，把一些城给利未人居住，也要把这些城四围的郊野给利未人。 ###EN### Command the children of Israel to give to the Levites some of the inheritance of their possession, cities to dwell in; and you shall give to the Levites pasture lands around their cities.
Verse_Ch: 35:3 这些城要归他们居住，城的郊野可以牧放他们的牲畜、羊群、和一切的牲口。 ###EN### And the cities shall be for them to dwell in, and their pasture lands shall be for their cattle and for their livestock and for all their animals.
Verse_Ch: 35:4 你们给利未人的郊野，要从城墙起，四围往外量一千肘。 ###EN### And the pasture lands of the cities which you shall give to the Levites shall be from the city wall and outward, a thousand cubits all around.
Verse_Ch: 35:5 要从城外，东边量二千肘，南边量二千肘，西边量二千肘，北边量二千肘，城在当中；这要归他们作城的郊野。 ###EN### And you shall measure from the outside of the city on the east side two thousand cubits and on the south side two thousand cubits and on the west side two thousand cubits and on the north side two thousand cubits, with the city in the center. This shall be their pasture lands for the cities.
Verse_Ch: 35:6 你们给利未人的城，当有六座庇护城，使误杀人的可以逃到那里；此外，还要给他们四十二座城。 ###EN### And the cities which you shall give to the Levites shall be the six cities of refuge, which you shall give for the manslayer to flee to; and besides them you shall give forty-two cities.
Verse_Ch: 35:7 你们要给利未人的城，共有四十八座，连城带郊野都要给他们。 ###EN### All the cities which you shall give to the Levites shall be forty-eight cities, them and their pasture lands.
Verse_Ch: 35:8 你们要从以色列人所得的地业中，把一些城给利未人；人数多的就多给，人数少的就少给；各支派要按所承受为业之地，把一些城给利未人。 ###EN### And concerning the cities which you shall give from the possession of the children of Israel, from the larger tribe you shall take a larger number, and from the smaller tribe you shall take a smaller number; each one, according to its inheritance which they will inherit, shall give some of its cities to the Levites.
Verse_Ch: 35:9 耶和华对摩西说， ###EN### Then Jehovah spoke to Moses, saying,
Verse_Ch: 35:10 你要对以色列人说，你们过约但河，进了迦南地， ###EN### Speak to the children of Israel, and say to them, When you cross the Jordan into the land of Canaan,
Verse_Ch: 35:11 就要选定几座城，作你们的庇护城，使误杀人的可以逃到那里。 ###EN### Then you shall designate for yourselves cities to be your cities of refuge, so that the manslayer who kills any person unintentionally may flee there.
Verse_Ch: 35:12 这些城可以作你们逃避报仇之人的庇护处，使误杀人的不至于死，直等他站在会众面前受审判。 ###EN### And the cities shall be for you as a refuge from the avenger, so that the manslayer may not die unless he stands before the assembly for judgment.
Verse_Ch: 35:13 你们所拨出的城，有六座要作你们的庇护城。 ###EN### And the cities which you shall give shall be your six cities of refuge.
Verse_Ch: 35:14 在约但河东要拨出三座城，在迦南地也要拨出三座城，都作庇护城。 ###EN### You shall give three cities across the Jordan, and you shall give three cities in the land of Canaan; they shall be cities of refuge.
Verse_Ch: 35:15 这六座城要给以色列人，和他们中间的外人并寄居的，作为庇护城，使误杀人的都可以逃到那里。 ###EN### For the children of Israel and for the stranger and for the sojourner among them, these six cities shall be for refuge, so that anyone who kills a person unintentionally may flee there.
Verse_Ch: 35:16 人若用铁器打人，以致打死，他就是故意杀人的；故意杀人的必要被处死。 ###EN### But if he struck him with an instrument of iron, and he died, he is a murderer; the murderer shall surely be put to death.
Verse_Ch: 35:17 人若手中拿可以打死人的石头打死了人，他就是故意杀人的；故意杀人的必要被处死。 ###EN### And if he struck him with a stone in hand, by which one could die, and he did die, he is a murderer; the murderer shall surely be put to death.
Verse_Ch: 35:18 人若手中拿可以打死人的木器打死了人，他就是故意杀人的；故意杀人的必要被处死。 ###EN### Or if he struck him with a wooden object in hand, by which one could die, and he did die, he is a murderer; the murderer shall surely be put to death.
Verse_Ch: 35:19 报血仇的，要亲自杀那故意杀人的，一遇见就可以杀他。 ###EN### The avenger of blood himself shall put the murderer to death; when he encounters him, he shall put him to death.
Verse_Ch: 35:20 人若因怨恨把人推倒，或是埋伏着往人身上扔物，以致那人死了， ###EN### And if he pushed him out of hatred or threw something upon him while lying in wait, and he died,
Verse_Ch: 35:21 或是因仇恨用手打人，以致打死，那打人的必要被处死。他是故意杀人的；报血仇的一遇见，就可以杀他。 ###EN### Or in enmity struck him with his hand, and he died, the one who struck him shall surely be put to death; he is a murderer. The avenger of blood shall put the murderer to death when he encounters him.
Verse_Ch: 35:22 人若没有仇恨忽然将人推倒，或是没有埋伏把物扔在人身上， ###EN### But if he pushed him suddenly without enmity, or threw upon him anything without lying in wait,
Verse_Ch: 35:23 或是没有看见的时候，用可以打死人的石头扔在人身上，以致那人死了，本来与他无仇，也无意害他； ###EN### Or came upon him with any stone, by which someone could die, without seeing him and dropped it upon him, and he died, when he was not his enemy and did not seek his harm,
Verse_Ch: 35:24 会众就要照这些典章，在打死人的和报血仇的中间审判。 ###EN### Then the assembly shall judge between the slayer and the avenger of blood according to these ordinances.
Verse_Ch: 35:25 会众要救这误杀人的脱离报血仇之人的手，也要使他归回先前逃到的庇护城；他要住在其中，直等到受圣膏油膏抹的大祭司死了。 ###EN### And the assembly shall deliver the manslayer out of the hand of the avenger of blood, and the assembly shall return him to his city of refuge to which he had fled; and he shall dwell in it until the death of the high priest, who was anointed with the holy oil.
Verse_Ch: 35:26 但误杀人的，无论什么时候，若出了他所逃到的庇护城境外， ###EN### But if the manslayer shall at any time go beyond the boundary of his city of refuge to which he has fled,
Verse_Ch: 35:27 报血仇的在庇护城境外遇见他，将他杀了，报血仇的就没有流血之罪。 ###EN### And the avenger of blood finds him outside the boundary of his city of refuge and the avenger of blood slays the manslayer, he shall not have guilt for blood,
Verse_Ch: 35:28 因为误杀人的本该住在庇护城里，直等到大祭司死了；大祭司死了以后，误杀人的才可以回到他所得为业之地。 ###EN### Because he should have remained in his city of refuge until the death of the high priest; but after the death of the high priest the manslayer shall return to the land of his possession.
Verse_Ch: 35:29 这在你们一切的住处，要作你们世世代代判断的律例。 ###EN### And these things shall be for a statute of judgment to you throughout your generations in all your dwellings.
Verse_Ch: 35:30 无论谁杀了人，要凭几个见证人的口，才可把那故意杀人的杀了，只是不可凭一个见证人的见证叫人死。 ###EN### Whoever kills a person, the murderer shall be slain upon the testimony of witnesses; but one witness shall not testify against any person so that he die.
Verse_Ch: 35:31 故意杀人、犯了死罪的，你们不可收赎价代替他的命；他必要被处死。 ###EN### Moreover you shall not take a ransom for the life of a murderer who is guilty of death, but he shall surely be put to death.
Verse_Ch: 35:32 那逃到庇护城的人，你们不可为他收赎价，使他在大祭司未死以前回本地居住。 ###EN### And you shall not take a ransom for one who has fled to his city of refuge, so that he may return to live in the land before the death of the high priest.
Verse_Ch: 35:33 这样，你们就不污秽所在之地，因为血是污秽地的；若有在地上流人血的，除非流那杀人者的血，那地就不得遮罪。 ###EN### Thus you shall not pollute the land in which you are, for blood pollutes the land. And no expiation can be made for the land for the blood that is shed in it, except by the blood of the one who shed it.
Verse_Ch: 35:34 你们不可玷污所住之地，就是我住在其中之地，因为我耶和华是住在以色列人中间的。 ###EN### And you shall not defile the land in which you are dwelling, in the midst of which I tabernacle; for I Jehovah tabernacle in the midst of the children of Israel.
Chapter_Header: 36
Verse_Ch: 36:1 约瑟子孙的家族中，玛拿西的孙子，玛吉的儿子基列，他子孙家族之宗族的族长，都近前来到摩西和作首领的以色列人宗族的族长面前，说， ###EN### And the heads of the fathers' households of the family of the sons of Gilead, the son of Machir, the son of Manasseh, of the families of the sons of Joseph, came near and spoke before Moses and before the leaders, the heads of the fathers' house holds of the children of Israel;
Verse_Ch: 36:2 耶和华曾吩咐我主拈阄分地给以色列人为业，我主也受了耶和华的吩咐，将我们兄弟西罗非哈的产业分给他的众女儿。 ###EN### And they said, Jehovah commanded my lord to give the land for inheritance by lot to the children of Israel, and my lord was commanded by Jehovah to give the inheritance of Zelophehad our brother to his daughters.
Verse_Ch: 36:3 但她们若嫁给以色列别支派的人，她们的产业就必从我们祖宗的产业中减去，加在她们所要归属支派的产业中；这样，我们拈阄所得的产业就减少了。 ###EN### But if they are married to one of the sons of the other tribes of the children of Israel, then their inheritance will be taken away from the inheritance of our fathers and will be added to the inheritance of the tribe to which they belong; so it will be taken away from the lot of our inheritance.
Verse_Ch: 36:4 到了以色列人的禧年，她们的产业就必加在她们所要归属支派的产业中；这样，我们祖宗支派的产业就减少了。 ###EN### And when the jubilee of the children of Israel takes place, then their inheritance will be added to the inheritance of the tribe to which they belong; so their inheritance will be taken away from the inheritance of the tribe of our fathers.
Verse_Ch: 36:5 摩西照耶和华的话吩咐以色列人说，约瑟支派的人说得有理。 ###EN### Then Moses commanded the children of Israel according to the word of Jehovah, saying, The tribe of the sons of Joseph speaks correctly.
Verse_Ch: 36:6 论到西罗非哈的众女儿，耶和华这样吩咐说，她们可以嫁给自己看为好的人，只是要嫁给自己父亲支派家族的人。 ###EN### This is what Jehovah commands concerning the daughters of Zelophehad, saying, Let them be married to whom they think best; only into the family of the tribe of their father they shall marry.
Verse_Ch: 36:7 这样，以色列人的产业就不从这支派转到那支派，因为以色列人要各守住自己祖宗支派的产业。 ###EN### So an inheritance of the children of Israel shall not go around from tribe to tribe, for each one of the children of Israel shall cling to the inheritance of the tribe of his fathers.
Verse_Ch: 36:8 凡在以色列支派中得了产业的女子，必嫁给自己父亲支派家族的人，好叫以色列人各自承受他祖宗的产业。 ###EN### And every daughter who possesses an inheritance in any tribe of the children of Israel shall marry into one of the family of the tribe of her father, so that each one of the children of Israel may possess the inheritance of his fathers.
Verse_Ch: 36:9 这样，他们的产业就不从这支派转到那支派，因为以色列支派的人要各守住自己的产业。 ###EN### So an inheritance shall not go around from one tribe to another tribe, for each one of the tribes of the children of Israel shall cling to his own inheritance.
Verse_Ch: 36:10 耶和华怎样吩咐摩西，西罗非哈的众女儿就怎样行。 ###EN### Just as Jehovah had commanded Moses, so the daughters of Zelophehad did;
Verse_Ch: 36:11 西罗非哈的女儿玛拉、得撒、曷拉、密迦、挪阿都嫁给了她们伯叔的儿子。 ###EN### That is, Mahlah, Tirzah, and Hoglah, and Milcah and Noah, the daughters of Zelophedad, got married to their uncles' sons.
Verse_Ch: 36:12 她们嫁入约瑟儿子玛拿西之子孙的家族中；她们的产业仍留在自己父亲家族的支派中。 ###EN### They married into the families of the sons of Manasseh the son of Joseph, and their inheritance remained in the tribe of the family of their father.
Verse_Ch: 36:13 这是耶和华在摩押平原与耶利哥相对的约但河边，借着摩西所吩咐以色列人的命令和典章。 ###EN### These are the commandments and the ordinances which Jehovah commanded through Moses to the children of Israel in the plains of Moab by the Jordan at Jericho.
